ṣoḍaśīm tīrthānām paramam tīrtham maṅgalānām ca maṅgalam pavitram ca pavitrāṇām prapadyante divākaram śakra ādyaiḥ saṃstutam devam ye namasyanti bhāskaram munayaḥ ūcuḥ nāmnām aṣṭaśatam brūhi yat tvayā uktam purā raveḥ aṣṭottaraśatam nāmnām śṛṇudhvam gadataḥ mama bhāskarasya param guhyam svarga mokṣa pradam dvijāḥ om sūryaḥ aryamā bhagaḥ tvaṣṭā pūṣā arkaḥ savitā raviḥ gabhastimān ajaḥ kālaḥ mṛtyuḥ dhātā prabhākaraḥ pṛthivī āpaḥ ca tejaḥ ca kham vāyuḥ ca parāyaṇam indraḥ vivasvān dīpta aṃśuḥ śuciḥ śauriḥ śanaiścaraḥ brahmā viṣṇuḥ ca rudraḥ ca skandaḥ vaiśravaṇaḥ yamaḥ vaidyutaḥ jāṭharaḥ ca agniḥ aindhanaḥ tejasām patiḥ kṛtam tretā dvāparaḥ ca kaliḥ sarva amara āśrayaḥ kalā kāṣṭhā muhūrtāḥ ca kṣapāḥ yāmāḥ tathā kṣaṇāḥ puruṣaḥ śāśvataḥ yogī vyakta avyaktaḥ sanātanaḥ varuṇaḥ sāgaraḥ aṃśaḥ ca jīmūtaḥ jivanaḥ ari hā bhūta āśrayaḥ bhūtapatiḥ sarva loka namaskṛtaḥ sraṣṭā saṃvartakaḥ vahniḥ sarvasya ādiḥ a lolupaḥ anantaḥ kapilaḥ bhānuḥ kāma daḥ sarvatomukhaḥ jayaḥ viśālaḥ vara daḥ sarva bhūta niṣevitaḥ manaḥ suparṇaḥ bhūtādiḥ śīghragaḥ prāṇa dhāraṇaḥ dvādaśa ātmā raviḥ dakṣaḥ pitā mātā pitāmahaḥ svargadvāram prajādvāram mokṣadvāram triviṣṭapam dehakartā praśānta ātmā viśvātmā viśvatomukhaḥ carācara ātmā sūkṣma ātmā maitreyaḥ karuṇā anvitaḥ nāmnām aṣṭaśatam ramyam mayā proktam dvijottamāḥ sūrya udaye yaḥ su samāhitaḥ paṭhet smṛtim ca medhām ca sa vindate parām prakīrtayet śuddha manāḥ samāhitaḥ vidrāvya vibudhān sarvān siddha vidyādharān ṛṣīn gandharva yakṣa nāgān ca tathā anyān ca samāgatān jaghāna pūrvam dakṣasya yajataḥ dharaṇī tale yajñam samṛddham ratna āḍhyam sarva saṃbhāra saṃbhṛtam yasya pratāpa saṃtrastāḥ śakra ādyāḥ tridivaukasaḥ śāntim na lebhire viprāḥ kailāsam śaraṇam gatāḥ saḥ āste tatra vara daḥ śūla pāṇiḥ vṛṣa dhvajaḥ pinākapāṇiḥ bhagavān dakṣa yajña vināśanaḥ mahādevaḥ akale deśe kṛttivāsāḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ ekāmrake muni śreṣṭhāḥ sarva kāma pradaḥ haraḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ jaghāna yajñam dakṣasya devaiḥ sarvaiḥ alaṃkṛtam śrotum icchāmahe brūhi param kautūhalam hi naḥ dakṣasya āsan aṣṭa kanyāḥ yāḥ ca evam pati saṃgatāḥ svebhyaḥ gṛhebhyaḥ ca ānīya tāḥ pitā abhyarcayat gṛhe tāsām jyeṣṭhā satī nāma patnī yā tryambakasya vai na ajuhāva ātmajām tām vai dakṣaḥ rudram abhidviṣan akarot saṃnatim dakṣe na ca kāṃcid maheśvaraḥ jāmātā śvaśure tasmin svabhāvāt tejasi sthitaḥ tatas jñātvā satī sarvāḥ tāḥ tu prāptāḥ pituḥ gṛham jagāma sā api anāhūtā satī tu sva pituḥ gṛham tābhyaḥ hīnām pitā cakre satyāḥ pūjām a saṃmatām tatas abravīt sā pitaram devī krodha samākulā yavīyasībhyaḥ śreṣṭhā aham kim na pūjasi mām prabho asatkṛtām avasthām yaḥ kṛtavān asi garhitām aham jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā ca mām tvam satkartum arhasi evam uktaḥ abravīt enām dakṣaḥ saṃrakta locanaḥ dakṣaḥ uvāca tvattaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ variṣṭhāḥ ca pūjyāḥ bālāḥ sutāḥ mama tāsām ye ca eva bhartāraḥ te me bahu matāḥ sati brahmiṣṭhāḥ ca vrata sthāḥ ca mahā yogāḥ su dhārmikāḥ guṇaiḥ ca eva adhikāḥ ślāghyāḥ sarve te tryambakāt sati vasiṣṭhaḥ atriḥ pulastyaḥ ca aṅgirāḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ bhṛguḥ marīciḥ ca tathā śreṣṭhāḥ jāmātaraḥ mama tena tvām na bubhūṣāmi pratikūlaḥ hi me bhavaḥ iti uktavān tadā dakṣaḥ saṃpramūḍhena cetasā śāpa artham ātmanaḥ ca eva yena uktāḥ vai mahā ṛṣayaḥ vāc manaḥ karmabhiḥ yasmāt aduṣṭām mām vigarhasi tasmāt tyajāmi aham deham imam tāta tava ātmajam tatas tena apamānena satī duḥkhāt amarṣitā tatra api aham asaṃmūḍhā saṃbhūtā dhārmikī punar tatra eva atha samāsīnā ruṣṭa ātmānam samādadhe dhārayām āsa ca āgneyīm dhāraṇām ātmanā ātmani tatas sva ātmānam utthāpya vāyunā samudīritaḥ tat upaśrutya nidhanam satyāḥ devyāḥ sa śūladhṛk saṃvādam ca tayoḥ buddhvā yāthātathyena śaṃkaraḥ dakṣasya ca vināśāya cukopa bhagavān prabhuḥ uvāca yasmāt avamatā dakṣa sahasā eva āgatā satī praśastāḥ ca itarāḥ sarvāḥ tvad sutāḥ bhartṛbhiḥ saha hute vai brahmaṇaḥ sattre cākṣuṣasya antare manoḥ abhivyāhṛtya saptarṣīn dakṣam saḥ abhyaśapat punar bhavitā mānuṣaḥ rājā cākṣuṣasya antare manoḥ prācīnabarhiṣaḥ pautraḥ putraḥ ca api pracetasaḥ dakṣaḥ iti eva nāmnā tvam māriṣāyām janiṣyasi kanyāyām śākhinām ca eva prāpte vai cākṣuṣa antare dakṣaḥ uvāca yasmāt tvam mad kṛte krūraḥ ṛṣīn vyāhṛtavān asi tasmāt sārdham suraiḥ yajñe na tvām yakṣyanti vai dvijāḥ kṛtvā āhutim tava krūra apaḥ spṛśanti karmasu cāturvarṇyam tu devānām te ca api ekatra bhuñjate sarveṣām ca eva lokānām ādiḥ bhūrlokaḥ ucyate tam aham dhārayāmi ekaḥ sva icchayā na tava ājñayā tasmin dhṛte sarva lokāḥ sarve tiṣṭhanti śāśvatāḥ tasmāt aham vasāmi iha satatam na tava ājñayā tatas abhivyāhṛtaḥ dakṣaḥ rudreṇa amita tejasā svāyaṃbhuvīm tanum tyaktvā utpannaḥ mānuṣeṣu iha yadā gṛhapatiḥ dakṣaḥ yajñānām īśvaraḥ prabhuḥ menāyām tām umām devīm janayām āsa śailarāj sā tu devī satī pūrvam āsīt paścāt umā bhavat mārīcam kaśyapam devī yathā aditiḥ anuvratā sārdham nārāyaṇam śrīḥ tu maghavantam śacī yathā viṣṇum kīrtiḥ uṣāḥ sūryam vasiṣṭham ca api arundhatī evam prācetasaḥ dakṣaḥ jajñe vai cākṣuṣe antare prācīnabarhiṣaḥ pautraḥ putraḥ ca api pracetasām daśabhyaḥ tu pracetobhyaḥ māriṣāyām punar nṛpa jajñe rudra abhiśāpena dvitīyam iti naḥ śrutam iti eṣaḥ anuśayaḥ hi āsīt tayoḥ jāti antare gataḥ tasmāt na anuśayaḥ kāryaḥ vareṣu iha kadācana jāti antara gatasya api bhāvitasya śubha aśubhaiḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ katham roṣeṇa sā pūrvam dakṣasya duhitā satī tyaktvā deham punar jātāḥ girirāja gṛhe prabho deha antare katham tasyāḥ pūrva dehaḥ babhūva ha bhavena saha saṃyogaḥ saṃvādaḥ ca tayoḥ katham vivāhaḥ ca jagannātha sarva āścarya samanvitaḥ śrotum icchāmahe puṇyām kathām ca ati manoharām śṛṇudhvam muni śārdūlāḥ kathām pāpa praṇāśinīm umā śaṃkarayoḥ puṇyām sarva kāma phala pradām kadācid sva gṛhāt prāptam kaśyapam dvipadām varam kena akṣayāḥ ca lokāḥ syuḥ khyātiḥ ca paramā mune kaśyapaḥ uvāca mama akhyātiḥ apatyena brahmaṇā ṛṣibhiḥ saha kim na paśyasi śaila indra yatas mām paripṛcchasi vartayiṣyāmi yat ca api yathādṛṣṭam purā acala vārāṇasīm aham gacchan apaśyam saṃsthitam divi tasya adhastāt ārta nādam garta sthāne śṛṇomi aham tam aham tapasā jñātvā tatra eva antarhitaḥ sthitaḥ athā agāt tatra śaila indra vipraḥ niyamavān śuciḥ tīrtha abhiṣeka pūta ātmā pare tapasi saṃsthitaḥ atha sa vrajamānaḥ tu vyāghreṇa abhīṣitaḥ dvijaḥ viveśa tam tadā deśam sa gartaḥ yatra bhūdhara gartāyām vīraṇa stambe lambamānān tadā munīn apaśyat ārtaḥ duḥkha ārtān tān apṛcchat ca sa dvijaḥ ke yūyam vīraṇa stambe lambamānāḥ hi adhomukhāḥ duḥkhitāḥ kena mokṣaḥ ca yuṣmākam bhavitā anaghāḥ pitaraḥ ūcuḥ vayam te kṛta puṇyasya pitaraḥ sa pitāmahāḥ prapitāmahāḥ ca kliśyāmaḥ tava duṣṭena karmaṇā narakaḥ ayam mahābhāga garta rūpeṇa saṃsthitaḥ yāvat tvam jīvase vipra tāvat eva vayam sthitāḥ mṛte tvayi gamiṣyāmaḥ narakam pāpa cetasaḥ yadi tvam dāra saṃyogam kṛtvā apatyam guṇa uttaram na anyena tapasā putra tīrthānām ca phalena ca kaśyapaḥ uvāca sa tathā iti pratijñāya ārādhya vṛṣabhadhvajam pitṝn gartāt samuddhṛtya gaṇapān pracakāra ha svayam rudrasya dayitaḥ suveśaḥ nāma nāmataḥ tasmāt kṛtvā tapaḥ ghoram apatyam guṇavat bhṛśam utpādayasva śaila indra sutām tvam varavarṇinīm saḥ evam uktvā ṛṣiṇā śailendraḥ niyama sthitaḥ tapaḥ cakāra api atulam yena tuṣṭiḥ abhūt mama tadā tam utpapāta aham vara daḥ asmi iti ca abravam himavān uvāca yasyāḥ prabhāvāt sarvatra kīrtim āpsyasi śobhanām arcitaḥ sarva devānām tīrtha koṭi samāvṛtaḥ pāvanaḥ ca eva puṇyena devānām api sarvatas jyeṣṭhā ca sā bhavitrī te anye ca atra tatas śubhe aparṇām ekaparṇām ca tathā ca eva ekapāṭalām nyagrodham eka parṇam tu pāṭalam ca ekapāṭalām śatam varṣa sahasrāṇām duścaram deva dānavaiḥ āhāram eka parṇam tu ekaparṇā samācarat pūrṇe varṣa sahasre tu āhāram tāḥ pracakratuḥ aparṇā tu nirāhārā tām mātā pratyabhāṣata niṣedhayantī ca u mā iti mātṛ snehena duḥkhitā sā tathā uktā tayā mātrā devī duścara cāriṇī tena eva nāmnā lokeṣu vikhyātā sura pūjitā etāsām tapasām vṛttam yāvat bhūmiḥ dhariṣyati tapaḥ śarīrāḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ tisraḥ yogam samāśritāḥ sarvāḥ ca eva mahābhāgāḥ tathā ca sthira yauvanāḥ anugṛhṇanti lokān ca tapasā svena sarvadā umā tāsām variṣṭhā ca jyeṣṭhā ca varavarṇinī dattakaḥ ca uśanā tasya putraḥ sa bhṛgu nandanaḥ āsīt tasya ekaparṇā tu devalam suṣuve sutam yā tu tāsām kumārīṇām tṛtīyā hi ekapāṭalā umā tu yā mayā tubhyam kīrtitā varavarṇinī devi kim tapasā lokān tāpayiṣyasi śobhane tvayā sṛṣṭam idam sarvam mā kṛtvā tat vināśaya tvam hi dhārayase lokān imān sarvān sva tejasā brūhi kim te jaganmātar prārthitam saṃprati iha naḥ tvam eva tat vijānīṣe tatas pṛcchasi kim punar śarvaḥ eva patiḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarva loka īśvara īśvaraḥ vayam sadā eva yasya ime vaśyāḥ vai kiṃkarāḥ śubhe udāra rūpaḥ vikṛta ādi rūpaḥ maheśvaraḥ parvata loka vāsī vibhīṣaṇam rūpam iva āsthitaḥ yaḥ devi śīghreṇa kālena dhūrjaṭiḥ nīlalohitaḥ sa bhartā tava deveśaḥ bhavitā mā tapaḥ kṛthāḥ tatas pradakṣiṇīkṛtya devāḥ viprāḥ gireḥ sutām jagmuḥ ca adarśanam tasyāḥ sā ca api virarāma ha sā devī sūktam iti evam uktvā svasya āśrame śubhe dvāri jātam aśokam ca samupāśritya ca āsthitā vikṛtam rūpam āsthāya hrasvaḥ bāhukaḥ eva ca vibhagna nāsikaḥ bhūtvā kubjaḥ keśānta piṅgalaḥ uvāca vikṛta āsyaḥ ca devi tvām varayāmi aham atha umā yoga saṃsiddhā jñātvā śaṃkaram āgatam antar bhāva viśuddha ātmā kṛpā anuṣṭhāna lipsayā tam uvāca argha pādyābhyām madhuparkeṇa ca eva ha saṃpūjya sumanobhiḥ tam brāhmaṇam brāhmaṇa priyā uvāca śailarājānam sutām me yaccha śailarāj sa tam vikṛta rūpeṇa jñātvā rudram atha avyayam bhītaḥ śāpāt ca vimanāḥ idam vacanam abravīt bhagavat na avamanye aham brāhmaṇān bhuvi devatāḥ manīṣitam tu yat pūrvam tat śṛṇuṣva mahāmate tat śrutvā śaila vacanam bhagavān vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ devyāḥ samīpam āgatya idam āha mahāmanāḥ śivaḥ uvāca devi pitrā tu anujñātaḥ svayaṃvare iti śrutiḥ tat āpṛcchya gamiṣyāmi durlabhām tvām varānane rūpavantam samutsṛjya vṛṇoṣi a sadṛśam katham tena uktā sā tadā tatra bhāvayantī tad īritam bhāvam ca rudra nihitam prasādam manasaḥ tathā saṃprāpya uvāca deveśam mā te abhūt buddhiḥ anyathā aham tvām varayiṣyāmi na adbhutam tu kathaṃcana gṛhītvā stabakam sā tu hastābhyām tatra saṃsthitā skandhe śaṃbhoḥ samādhāya devī prāha vṛtaḥ asi me tatas sa bhagavān devaḥ tayā devyā vṛtaḥ tadā uvāca tam aśokam vai vācā saṃjīvayan iva śivaḥ uvāca kāmarūpī kāma puṣpaḥ kāma daḥ dayitaḥ mama sarva ābharaṇa puṣpa āḍhyaḥ sarva puṣpa phala upagaḥ sarva gandhaḥ ca devānām bhaviṣyasi dṛḍha priyaḥ āśramam vedam atyartham citrakūṭa iti viśrutam yaḥ hi yāsyati puṇya arthī saḥ aśvamedham avāpsyati antardadhe jagatsraṣṭā sarvabhūtapaḥ īśvaraḥ tatas eva unmukhī bhūtvā śilāyām saṃbabhūva ha atha śuśrāva śabdam ca bālasya ārtasya śailajā sarasi udaka saṃpūrṇe samīpe ca āśramasya ca sa kṛtvā bāla rūpam tu devadevaḥ svayam śivaḥ yogamāyām samāsthāya prapañca udbhava kāraṇam tat rūpam sarasaḥ madhye kṛtvā evam samabhāṣata bālaḥ uvāca trātu mām kaścid iti āha grāheṇa hṛta cetasam dhik kaṣṭam bālaḥ eva aham aprāpta artha manorathaḥ śocāmi na svakam deham grāha grastaḥ su duḥkhitaḥ yathā śocāmi pitaram mātaram ca tapasvinīm grāha gṛhītam mām śrutvā prāptam nidhanam utsukau priya putrau eka putrau prāṇān nūnam tyajiṣyataḥ aho bata su kaṣṭam vai yaḥ aham bālaḥ a kṛta āśramaḥ śrutvā tu devī tam nādam viprasya ārtasya śobhanā sā apaśyat indu vadanā bālakam cāru rūpiṇam saḥ api grāha varaḥ śrīmān dṛṣṭvā devīm upāgatām tam gṛhītvā drutam yātaḥ madhyam sarasaḥ eva hi sa kṛṣyamāṇaḥ tejasvī nādam ārtam tadā akarot atha āha devī duḥkha ārtā bālam dṛṣṭvā graha āvṛtam pārvatī uvāca vimuñca imam mahā daṃṣṭra kṣipram bhīma parākrama grāhaḥ uvāca saḥ ayam mama mahābhāge ṣaṣṭhe ahani girīndraje brahmaṇā preritaḥ nūnam na enam mokṣye kathaṃcana grāhaḥ uvāca mā vyayaḥ tapasaḥ devi bhṛśam bāle śubha ānane yat bravīmi kuru śreṣṭhe tathā mokṣam avāpsyati tat kṛtam na atra saṃdehaḥ yatas me brāhmaṇāḥ priyāḥ grāhaḥ uvāca janma prabhṛti yat puṇyam mahā grāha kṛtam mayā tat te sarvam mayā dattam bālam muñca mahā graha prajajvāla tatas grāhaḥ tapasā tena bhūṣitaḥ uvāca ca evam tuṣṭa ātmā devīm lokasya dhāriṇīm grāhaḥ uvāca gṛhāṇa tapaḥ eva tvam bālam ca imam sumadhyame sā tu evam uktā grāheṇa uvāca idam mahāvratā dehena api mayā grāha rakṣyaḥ vipraḥ prayatnataḥ tapaḥ punar mayā prāpyam na prāpyaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ punar su niścitya mahā grāha kṛtam bālasya mokṣaṇam na viprebhyaḥ tapaḥ śreṣṭham śreṣṭhāḥ me brāhmaṇāḥ matāḥ dattvā ca aham na gṛhṇāmi grāha indra vihitam hi te tvayi eva ramatām etat bālaḥ ca ayam vimucyatām tathā uktaḥ tām praśasya atha muktvā bālam namasya ca devīm āditya avabhāsaḥ tatra eva antaradhīyata kartu kāmām tapaḥ bhūyas jñātvā tām śaṃkaraḥ svayam provāca vacanam viprāḥ mā kṛthāḥ tapaḥ iti uta svayaṃvaram udīkṣantī tasthau prītā mudā yutā bāla anubhāva ācaraṇam hi śaṃbhoḥ vistṛte himavat pṛṣṭhe vimāna śata saṃkule abhavat sa tu kālena śailaputryāḥ svayaṃvaraḥ jānan api mahā śailaḥ samaya arakṣaṇa īpsayā deva dānava siddhānām sarva loka nivāsinām vṛṇuyāt parameśānam samakṣam yadi me sutā tat eva sukṛtam ślāghyam mama abhyudaya saṃmatam iti saṃcintya śailendraḥ kṛtvā hṛdi maheśvaram ābrahmakeṣu deveṣu devyāḥ śailendra sattamaḥ kṛtvā ratna ākulam deśam svayaṃvaram acīkarat deva ādayaḥ sarva jagat nivāsāḥ samāyayuḥ tatra gṛhīta veśāḥ praphulla padmāsana saṃniviṣṭaḥ vijñāpitaḥ tena mahīdhra rājñā akṣṇām sahasram surarāj sa bibhrat divya aṅga hāra sraj udāra rūpaḥ āruhya sarva amara rāj sa vajram bibhrat samāgāt puratas surāṇām tejaḥ prabhāva adhika tulya rūpī ārūḍhaḥ āgāt tvaritam javena maṇi pradīpta ujjvala kuṇḍalaḥ ca āditya madhyāt bhaga nāmadhārī pīna aṅgayaṣṭiḥ su kṛta aṅgahāra tejaḥ bala ājñā sadṛśa prabhāvaḥ daṇḍam samāgṛhya kṛtāntaḥ āgāt āruhya bhīmam mahiṣam javena mahā mahīdhra ucchraya pīna gātraḥ svarṇa ādi ratna āñcita cāru veśaḥ saṃtāpayan sarva sura asura īśān nānā maṇi prajvalita aṅgayaṣṭiḥ āruhya sarva draviṇa adhipa īśaḥ āpyāyayan sarva sura asura īśān kāntyā ca veśena ca cāru rūpaḥ vimānam āruhya śaśī samāyāt śyāma aṅgayaṣṭiḥ su vicitra veśaḥ sarva aṅgaḥ ābaddha sugandhi mālyaḥ tārkṣyam samāruhya mahīdhra kalpam atha aśvinau ca api bhiṣagvarau dvau bibhrat tadānīm jvalana arka tejāḥ sārdham sa nāgaiḥ aparaiḥ mahātmā diteḥ sutānām ca mahā asurāṇām vara anurūpam pravidhāya veśam vṛndam samāgāt puratas surāṇām gandharva rājaḥ sa ca cāru rūpī śakra ājñayā tatra samājagāma anye ca devāḥ tridivāt tadānīm pṛthak pṛthak cāru gṛhīta veśāḥ ājagmuḥ āruhya vimāna pṛṣṭham rarāja rāja adhika lakṣya mūrtiḥ ājñā bala aiśvarya kṛta pramodaḥ svayaṃvaram tam samalaṃcakāra mātā ca teṣām sa sura asurāṇām patnī ca śaṃbhoḥ puruṣasya dhīmataḥ gītā purāṇe prakṛtiḥ parā yā dakṣasya kopāt himavat gṛham sā kārya artham āyāt tridivaukasām hi vimāna pṛṣṭhe maṇi hema juṣṭe sthitā valat cāmara vījita aṅgī sarva ṛtu puṣpām su su gandha mālām mālām pragṛhya devyām tu sthitāyām deva saṃsadi śakra ādyaiḥ āgataiḥ devaiḥ svayaṃvare upāgate devyā jijñāsayā śaṃbhuḥ bhūtvā pañca śikhaḥ śiśuḥ tatas dadarśa tam devī śiśum pañcaśikham sthitam jñātvā tam samavadhyānāt jagṛhe prīti saṃyutā atha sā śuddha saṃkalpā kāṅkṣitam prāpya sat patim nivṛttā ca tadā tasthau kṛtvā sā hṛdi tam vibhum tatas dṛṣṭvā śiśum devāḥ devyāḥ utsaṅga vartinam vajram āhārayat tasya bāhum utkṣipya vṛtrahā stambhitaḥ śiśu rūpeṇa devadevena śaṃbhunā vajram kṣeptum na śaśāka vṛtrahā calitum na ca bhagaḥ nāma tatas devaḥ ādityaḥ kāśyapaḥ balī śiraḥ prakampayan viṣṇuḥ śaṃkaram samavaikṣata aham parama saṃvignaḥ dhyānam āsthāya sādaram jñātvā aham parameśānam śīghram utthāya sādaram vavande caraṇam śaṃbhoḥ stutavān tam aham dvijāḥ purāṇaiḥ sāma saṃgītaiḥ puṇya ākhyaiḥ guhya nāmabhiḥ ajaḥ tvam ajaraḥ devaḥ sraṣṭā vibhuḥ parāparam amṛtam paramātmā ca īśvaraḥ kāraṇam mahat brahmasṛj prakṛteḥ sraṣṭā sarva kṛt prakṛteḥ paraḥ iyam ca prakṛtiḥ devī sadā te sṛṣṭi kāraṇam patnī rūpam samāsthāya jagat kāraṇam āgatā prasādāt tava deveśa niyogāt ca mayā prajāḥ deva ādyāḥ tu imāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ mūḍhāḥ tvad yoga māyayā kuru prasādam eteṣām yathāpūrvam bhavantu ime stambhitān sarva devān tān idam ca aham tadā uktavān mūḍhāḥ ca devatāḥ sarvāḥ na enam budhyata śaṃkaram gacchadhvam śaraṇam śīghram enam eva maheśvaram sārdham mayā eva deveśam paramātmānam avyayam praṇemuḥ manasā śarvam bhāva śuddhena cetasā atha teṣām prasannaḥ abhūt devadevaḥ maheśvaraḥ yathāpūrvam cakāra āśu devatānām tanūḥ tadā tebhyaḥ sa paramam cakṣuḥ sva vapuḥ dṛṣṭi śaktimat prādāt parama deveśam apaśyan te tadā vibhum te dṛṣṭvā parameśānam tṛtīya īkṣaṇa dhāriṇam śakra ādyāḥ menire devāḥ sarve eva sura īśvarāḥ tasya devī tadā hṛṣṭā samakṣam tridivaukasām pādayoḥ sthāpayām āsa sraj mālām amita dyutiḥ saha devyāḥ namaḥ cakruḥ śirobhiḥ bhū tala āśritaiḥ himavantam mahā śailam uktavān ca mahā dyutim ślāghyaḥ pūjyaḥ ca vandyaḥ ca sarveṣām tvam mahān asi kriyatām cāruḥ udvāhaḥ kimartham sthīyate param tatas praṇamya himavān tadā mām pratyabhāṣata himavān uvāca tatas evam vacaḥ śrutvā girirājasya bho dvijāḥ udvāhaḥ kriyatām devaḥ iti aham ca uktavān vibhum mām āha śaṃkaraḥ devaḥ yathā iṣṭam iti lokapaḥ udvāha artham maheśasya nānā ratna upaśobhitam citrā mārakatī bhūmiḥ suvarṇa stambha śobhitā soma ādityau samam tatra tāpayantau mahā maṇī saurabheyam manaḥ ramyam gandham ādāya mārutaḥ samudrāḥ tatra catvāraḥ śakra ādyāḥ ca sura uttamāḥ gandharva apsarasaḥ sarve nāgāḥ yakṣāḥ sarākṣasāḥ audakāḥ khecarāḥ ca anye kiṃnarāḥ deva cāraṇāḥ tumburuḥ nāradaḥ hāhā hūhūḥ ca eva tu sāma gāḥ ramyāṇi ādāya vādyāni tatra ājagmuḥ tadā puram ṛṣayaḥ tu kathāḥ tatra veda gītāḥ tapodhanāḥ puṇyān vaivāhikān mantrān jepuḥ saṃhṛṣṭa mānasāḥ jagataḥ mātaraḥ sarvāḥ deva kanyāḥ ca kṛtsnaśas gāyanti harṣitāḥ sarvāḥ udvāhe parameṣṭhinaḥ ṛtavaḥ ṣaṭ samam tatra nānā gandha sukha āvahāḥ udvāhaḥ śaṃkarasya iti mūrtimantaḥ upasthitāḥ nīla jīmūta saṃkāśaiḥ mantra dhvani praharṣibhiḥ kekāyamānaiḥ śikhibhiḥ nṛtyamānaiḥ ca sarvaśas vilola piṅgala spaṣṭa vidyut lekhā vihāsitā kumuda āpīḍa śuklābhiḥ balākābhiḥ ca śobhitā pratyagra saṃjāta śilīndhra kandalī latā druma ādi udgata pallavā śubhā śubha ambu dhārā praṇaya prabodhitaiḥ mahā alasaiḥ bheka gaṇaiḥ ca nāditā priyeṣu māna uddhata mānasānām manasvinīnām api kāminīnām mayūra kekā abhirutaiḥ kṣaṇena tathā vivarṇa ujjvala cāru mūrtinā śaśāṅka lekhā kuṭilena sarvatas mahā indracāpena bhṛśam virājitā ghana ambu saṃparka tayā suśītalaiḥ sura aṅganānām alaka āvalīḥ śubhāḥ nirīkṣitā sa ādaram utsukābhiḥ niśvāsa dhūmram pathika aṅganābhiḥ haṃsa nūpura śabda āḍhyā samunnata payodharā calat vidyut latā āhārā spaṣṭa padma vilocanā surabhi kusuma reṇu kḥpta sarva aṅga śobhā giriduhitṛ vivāhe prāvṛṣ āvirbabhūva vistīrṇa pulina śroṇī kūjat sārasa mekhalā nava śyāma latā śyāma romarāji puraskṛtā candra aṃśu hāra vargeṇa kaṇṭha urasthala gāminā prahlādayantī cetāṃsi sarveṣām tridivaukasām calat kumuda saṃghāta cāru kuṇḍala śobhinī tad puṣpa saṃcaya mayaiḥ vāsobhiḥ samalaṃkṛtā rakta utpala agra caraṇā jātī puṣpa nakha āvalī kadalī stambha vāma ūrūḥ śaśāṅka vadanā tathā sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpannā sarva alaṃkāra bhūṣitā premṇā spṛśati kāntā iva sa anurāgā manoramā nirmukta asita megha kañcuka paṭā pūrṇa indu bimba ānanā nānā puṣparajaḥ sugandhi pavana prahrādanī cetasām tatra āsīt kalahaṃsa nūpura ravā devyāḥ vivāhe śarad atyartha śītala ambhobhiḥ plāvayantau diśaḥ sadā ṛtū hemanta śiśirau ājagmatuḥ atidyutī tābhyām ṛtubhyām saṃprāptaḥ himavān sa naga uttamaḥ prāleya cūrṇa varṣibhyām kṣipram raupya haraḥ babhau agādhena tadā reje kṣīrodaḥ iva sāgaraḥ ṛtu pāryaya saṃprāptaḥ babhūva sa mahā giriḥ sādhu upacārāt sahasā kṛtārthaḥ iva durjanaḥ prāleya paṭala channaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ tu śuśubhe nagaḥ chattraiḥ iva mahābhāgaiḥ pāṇḍaraiḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ manobhava udreka karāḥ surāṇām surāṅganānām ca muhur samīrāḥ svaccha ambu pūrṇāḥ ca tathā nalinyaḥ padma utpalānām kusumaiḥ upetāḥ vivāhe guru kanyāyāḥ vasantaḥ samagāt ṛtuḥ nāryaḥ yathā ramyatarāḥ babhūvuḥ na ati uṣṇa śītāni payaḥ sarāṃsi kiñjalka cūrṇaiḥ kapilīkṛtāni yayuḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ sura danti mukhyāḥ priyaṅgūḥ cūta taravaḥ cūtān ca api priyaṅgavaḥ tarjayantaḥ iva anyonyam mañjarībhiḥ cakāśire hima śṛṅgeṣu śukleṣu tilakāḥ kusuma utkarāḥ śuśubhuḥ kāryam uddiśya vṛddhāḥ iva samāgatāḥ phulla aśoka latāḥ tatra śāla saṃśritāḥ kāminyaḥ iva kāntānām kaṇṭha ālambita bāhavaḥ tālāḥ stamālāḥ saralāḥ kapitthāḥ aśoka sarja arjuna kovidārāḥ puṃnāga nāgeśvara karṇikārāḥ lavaṅga tāla aguru saptaparṇā nyagrodha śobhāñjana nārikelāḥ vṛkṣāḥ tathā anye phala puṣpavantaḥ dṛśyāḥ babhūvuḥ su manohara aṅgāḥ jalāśayāḥ ca eva suvarṇa toyāḥ cakrāṅga kāraṇḍava haṃsa juṣ koyaṣṭi dātyūha balāka yuktā dṛśyāḥ tu padma utpala mīna pūrṇāḥ khagāḥ ca nānāvidha bhūṣita aṅgāḥ dṛśyāḥ tu vṛkṣeṣu su citra pakṣāḥ krīḍāsu yuktān atha tarjayantaḥ kurvanti śabdam madana īrita aṅgāḥ vavuḥ ca vātāḥ sukha śītala aṅgāḥ puṣpāṇi śubhrāṇi api pātayantaḥ śanais nagebhyaḥ malaya adri jātāḥ tathā eva sarve ṛtavaḥ ca puṇyāḥ cakāśire anyonya vimiśrita aṅgāḥ yeṣām su liṅgāni ca kīrtitāni te tatra āsan su manojña rūpāḥ samada ali kula udgīta śilā kusuma saṃcayaiḥ nīlāni nīla amburuhaiḥ payāṃsi gaurāṇi gauraiḥ ca mṛṇāla daṇḍaiḥ raktaiḥ ca raktāni bhṛśam kṛtāni haimāni vistīrṇa jaleṣu kaścitsu nirantaram cārutarāṇi keṣucid vaidūrya nālāni saraḥsu kaścitsu vāpyaḥ tatra abhavan ramyāḥ kamala utpala puṣpitāḥ nānā vihaṃga saṃjuṣṭāḥ haima sopānapaṅktayaḥ śṛṅgāṇi tasya tu gireḥ karṇikāraiḥ su puṣpitaiḥ īṣat vibhinna kusumaiḥ pāṭalaiḥ ca api pāṭalāḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ pavana ākampi mūrtibhiḥ kṛṣṇa arjunāḥ daśaguṇāḥ nīla aśoka mahīruhāḥ cāru rāva vijuṣṭāni kiṃśukānām vanāni ca nīla jīmūta saṃghātaiḥ nilīnaiḥ iva saṃdhiṣu nikāma puṣpaiḥ su viśāla śākhaiḥ himācalaḥ atīva tadā rarāja śrutvā śabdam mṛdu mada kalam sarvatas kokilānām cañcat pakṣāḥ sa madhurataram nīlakaṇṭhāḥ vineduḥ teṣām śabdaiḥ upacita balaḥ puṣpacāpa iṣu hastaḥ sajjībhūtaḥ tridaśa vanitāḥ veddhum aṅgeṣu anaṅgaḥ paṭuḥ sūrya ātapaḥ ca api prāyaśas alpa jalāśayaḥ devī vivāha samaye grīṣmaḥ āgāt himācalam śobhayām āsa śṛṅgāṇi prāleya adreḥ samantataḥ vavuḥ pāṭala vistīrṇa kadamba arjuna gandhinaḥ abhavan taṭa saṃghuṣṭa phalahaṃsa kadambakāḥ tathā kurabakāḥ ca api kusuma āpāṇḍu mūrtayaḥ sarveṣu naga śṛṅgeṣu bhramara āvali sevitāḥ bakulāḥ ca nitambeṣu viśāleṣu mahībhṛtaḥ vividha vihaṃgama nāda ramya deśāḥ ṣaṭ upayayuḥ ṛtavaḥ muni pravīrāḥ nānā vādya samākīrṇe aham tatra dvijātayaḥ śailaputrīm alaṃkṛtya yogi ābharaṇa saṃpadā puram praveśitavān tām svayam ādāya bho dvijāḥ dadāsi mahyam yadi ājñām kartavyaḥ ayam kriyā vidhiḥ mām āha śaṃkaraḥ ca evam devadevaḥ jagatpatiḥ śivaḥ uvāca yat uddiṣṭam sureśāna tat kuruṣva yathā īpsitam tatas ca aham prahṛṣṭa ātmā kuśān ādāya sa tvaram jvalanaḥ ca svayam tatra kṛta añjali puṭaḥ sthitaḥ tatas tam jvalanam sarvam kārayitvā pradakṣiṇam putraiḥ ca mānasaiḥ siddhaiḥ prahṛṣṭena antarātmanā vṛtte udvāha kāle tu praṇamya ca vṛṣadhvajam udvāhaḥ sa paraḥ vṛttaḥ yam devāḥ na viduḥ kvacid iti vaḥ sarvam ākhyātam svayaṃvaram idam śubham udvāhaḥ ca eva devasya śṛṇudhvam parama adbhutam praharṣam atulam gatvā devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ vāgbhiḥ ādyābhiḥ praṇemuḥ te maheśvaram devāḥ ūcuḥ namaḥ parvata liṅgāya parvata īśāya vai namaḥ namaḥ pavana vegāya virūpāya ajitāya ca namaḥ kleśa vināśāya dātre ca śubha saṃpadām namaḥ nīlaśikhaṇḍāya ambikāpataye namaḥ namaḥ pavana rūpāya śata rūpāya vai namaḥ viṣṭambhanāya śakrasya bāhvoḥ veda aṅkurāya ca salilāśaya liṅgāya yuga antāya namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ kapāla mālāya kapāla sūtra dhāriṇe namaḥ kapāla hastāya daṇḍine gadine namaḥ namaḥ khaṭvāṅga hastāya pramatha ārti harāya ca namaḥ yajña śiraḥ hantre kṛṣṇa keśa apahāriṇe bhaga netra nipātāya pūṣṇaḥ danta harāya ca namaḥ pināka śūla asi khaḍga mudgara dhāriṇe namaḥ astu kāla kālāya tṛtīya nayanāya ca suvarṇa retase ca eva namaḥ kuṇḍala dhāriṇe daityānām yoga nāśāya yoginām gurave namaḥ śaśāṅka āditya netrāya lalāṭa nayanāya ca namaḥ śmaśāna rataye śmaśāna vara dāya ca gṛhastha sādhave nityam jaṭile brahmacāriṇe namaḥ muṇḍa ardha muṇḍāya paśūnām pataye namaḥ namaḥ śāntāya dāntāya pralaya utpatti kāriṇe namaḥ rudrāya vasavaḥ ādityāya aśvine namaḥ namaḥ pitre atha sāṃkhyāya viśvedevāya vai namaḥ namaḥ śarvāya ugrāya śivāya vara dāya ca namaḥ bhīmāya senānye paśūnām pataye namaḥ śucaye vairi hānāya sadyojātāya vai namaḥ pradhānāya aprameyāya kāryāya kāraṇāya ca namaḥ puruṣa saṃyoga pradhāna guṇa kāriṇe pravartakāya prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca sarvaśas kāla jñāya ca sarveṣām namaḥ niyama kāriṇe namaḥ vaiṣamya kartre ca guṇānām vṛtti dāya ca stūyamānaḥ suraiḥ sarvaiḥ amarān idam abravīt uvāca draṣṭum sukhaḥ ca saumyaḥ ca devānām asmi bhoḥ surāḥ varam varayata kṣipram dātāsmi tam asaṃśayam devāḥ ūcuḥ yadā kāryam tadā naḥ tvam dāsyase varam īpsitam lokān ca pramathaiḥ sārdham viveśa bhavanam svakam saḥ apratirūpa gaṇa īśa samānaḥ vipra varyāḥ stavam hi imam śṛṇuyāt vā paṭhet ca yaḥ praviṣṭe bhavanam deve su upaviṣṭe varāsane tam anācāra saṃyuktam durātmānam kula adhamam lokān sarvān pīḍayantam sarva aṅga āvaraṇa ātmakam ṛṣīṇām vighna kartāram niyamānām vrataiḥ saha atha ātatāyinam viprāḥ veddhu kāmam sureśvaraḥ nayanena tṛtīyena sa avajñam samavaikṣata prasādayan ca tam devam papāta dharaṇī tale papāta sahasā mūrchām kṣaṇena samapadyata patnī tu karuṇam tasya vilalāpa su duḥkhitā devīm devam ca duḥkha ārtā ayācat karuṇāvatī tasyāḥ ca karuṇām jñātvā devau tau karuṇā ātmakau ūcatuḥ tām samālokya samāśvāsya ca duḥkhitām umā maheśvarau ūcatuḥ aśarīraḥ api te bhadre kāryam sarvam kariṣyati yadā tu viṣṇuḥ bhagavān vasudeva sutaḥ śubhe tatas sā tu varam labdhvā kāmapatnī śubha ānanā jagāma iṣṭam tadā deśam prīti yuktā gata klamā dagdhvā kāmam tatas viprāḥ sa tu devaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ reme tatra umayā sārdham prahṛṣṭaḥ tu himācale nadī tīreṣu kānteṣu kiṃnara ācariteṣu ca śṛṅgeṣu śailarājasya taḍāgeṣu saraḥsu ca vana rājiṣu ramyāsu nānā pakṣi ruteṣu ca tīrtheṣu puṇya toyeṣu munīnām āśrameṣu ca eteṣu puṇyeṣu manohareṣu deśeṣu vidyādhara bhūṣiteṣu tasmin nage harṣam avāpa śaṃbhuḥ nṛtyanti tatra apsarasaḥ sura īśāḥ gāyanti gandharva gaṇāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ mahā balaiḥ śakra yama agni tulyaiḥ devyāḥ priya artham bhaga netra hantā girim na tatyāja tadā mahātmā ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ devyāḥ samam tu bhagavān tiṣṭhan tatra sa kāma hā gaṇeśaiḥ vividha ākāraiḥ hāsam saṃjanayan muhur devīm bāla indu tilakaḥ ramayan ca rarāma ca mahā anubhāvaiḥ sarvajñaiḥ kāma rūpa dharaiḥ śubhaiḥ atha devī āsasāda ekā mātaram parameśvarī āsīnām kāñcane śubhre āsane parama adbhute atha dṛṣṭvā satīm devīm āgatām sura rūpiṇīm āsanena mahārheṇa śaṃpādayat aninditām āsīnām tām atha uvāca menā himavataḥ priyā daridrā krīḍanaiḥ tvam hi bhartrā krīḍasi saṃgatā ume te evam krīḍanti yathā tava patiḥ śubhe sā evam uktā atha mātrā tu na ati hṛṣṭa manāḥ bhavat mahatyā kṣamayā yuktā na kiṃcid tām uvāca ha visṛṣṭā ca tadā mātrā gatvā devam uvāca ha pārvatī uvāca anyam kuru mama āvāsam bhuvaneṣu mahā dyute sadā tvam ucyamānā vai mayā vāsa artham īśvari idānīm svayam eva tvam vāsam anyatra śobhane gṛham gatā asmi deveśa pituḥ adya mahātmanaḥ dṛṣṭvā ca tatra me mātā vijane loka bhāvane āsana ādibhiḥ abhyarcya sā mām evam abhāṣata ume tava sadā bhartā daridraḥ krīḍanaiḥ śubhe krīḍate nahi devānām krīḍā bhavati tādṛśī ramase tat aniṣṭam hi mama mātuḥ vṛṣadhvaja tatas devaḥ prahasya āha devīm hāsayitum prabhuḥ kṛttivāsāḥ hi avāsāḥ ca śmaśānanilayaḥ ca ha aniketaḥ hi araṇyeṣu parvatānām guhāsu ca tathā kuru mahādeva yathā aham sukham āpnuyām śrutvā sa devyāḥ vacanam sureśaḥ tasyāḥ priya arthe sva girim vihāya bhāryā sahāyaḥ sva gaṇaiḥ ca yuktaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ devyāḥ manyu kṛtam buddhvā kruddhaḥ sarva ātmakaḥ prabhuḥ katham vināśitaḥ yajñaḥ dakṣasya amita tejasaḥ mahādevena roṣāt vai tat naḥ prabrūhi vistarāt varṇayiṣyāmi vaḥ viprāḥ mahādevena vai yathā krodhāt vidhvaṃsitaḥ yajñaḥ devyāḥ priya cikīrṣayā purā meroḥ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ śṛṅgam trailokya pūjitam paryaṅke iva vistīrṇaḥ upaviṣṭaḥ babhūva ha śailarājasutā ca asya nityam pārśva sthitā abhavat ādityāḥ ca mahātmānaḥ vasavaḥ ca mahā ojasaḥ tathā eva ca mahātmānau aśvinau bhiṣajām varau tathā vaiśravaṇaḥ rājā guhyakaiḥ parivāritaḥ yakṣāṇām īśvaraḥ śrīmān kailāsa nilayaḥ prabhuḥ upāsate mahātmānam uśanā ca mahā muniḥ aṅgiraḥ pramukhāḥ ca eva tathā devarṣayaḥ api ca apsaraḥ gaṇa saṃghāḥ ca samājagmuḥ anekaśas vavau sukha śivaḥ vāyuḥ nānā gandha vahaḥ śuciḥ tathā vidyādharāḥ sādhyāḥ siddhāḥ ca eva tapodhanāḥ bhūtāni ca tathā anyāni nānā rūpa dharāṇi atha rākṣasāḥ ca mahā raudrāḥ piśācāḥ ca mahā balāḥ bahu rūpa dharāḥ dhṛṣṭāḥ nānā praharaṇa āyudhāḥ pragṛhya jvalitam śūlam dīpyamānam sva tejasā gaṅgā ca saritām śreṣṭhā sarva tīrtha jala udbhavā paryupāsata tam devam rūpiṇī dvijasattamāḥ evam sa bhagavān tatra pūjyamānaḥ sura ṛṣibhiḥ devaiḥ ca su mahābhāgaiḥ mahādevaḥ vyatiṣṭhata svarga sthānāt atha āgamya dakṣam āpedire tathā devasya anumate agacchan gaṅgādvāram iti śrutiḥ gandharva apsarasā ākīrṇam nānā druma latā āvṛtam ṛṣi siddhaiḥ parivṛtam dakṣam dharma bhṛtām varam ādityāḥ vasavaḥ rudrāḥ sādhyāḥ sarve marut gaṇāḥ viṣṇunā sahitāḥ sarve āgatāḥ yajña bhāginaḥ ūṣmapāḥ dhūmapāḥ ca eva ājyapāḥ somapāḥ tathā aśvinau marutaḥ ca eva nānā deva gaṇaiḥ saha jarāyu ja aṇḍa jāḥ ca eva tathā eva sveda ja udbhidaḥ āgatāḥ sattriṇaḥ sarve devāḥ strībhiḥ saha ṛṣibhiḥ virājante vimāna sthāḥ dīpyamānāḥ iva agnayaḥ tān dṛṣṭvā manyunā āviṣṭaḥ dadhīciḥ vākyam abravīt dadhīciḥ uvāca a pūjya pūjane ca eva pūjyānām ca api a pūjane naraḥ pāpam avāpnoti mahat vai na atra saṃśayaḥ evam uktvā tu viprarṣiḥ punar dakṣam abhāṣata dadhīciḥ uvāca pūjyam ca paśubhartāram kasmāt na arcayase prabhum dakṣaḥ uvāca santi me bahavaḥ rudrāḥ śūla hastāḥ kapardinaḥ ekādaśa sthāna gatāḥ na anyam vidmaḥ maheśvaram dadhīciḥ uvāca yathā aham śaṃkarāt ūrdhvam na anyam paśyāmi daivatam dakṣaḥ uvāca dakṣaḥ uvāca viṣṇoḥ ca bhāgāḥ vividhāḥ pradattāḥ dadāmi bhāgam na tu śaṃkarāya gatāḥ tu devatāḥ jñātvā śailarājasutā tadā uvāca vacanam śarvam devam paśupatim patim bhagavan kutra yānti ete devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ dakṣaḥ nāma mahābhāge prajānām patiḥ uttamaḥ yajñam etam mahābhāga kimartham na anugacchasi pūrva āgatena gantavyam mārgeṇa varavarṇini ajeyaḥ ca api adhṛṣyaḥ ca tejasā yaśasā śriyā atīva duḥkham āpannāḥ vepathuḥ ca mahān ayam kim nāma dānam niyamam tapaḥ vā evam bruvāṇām bhagavān vicintya patnīm prahṛṣṭaḥ kṣubhitām uvāca na vetsi mām devi kṛśa udara aṅgi aham vijānāmi viśāla netre mām adhvara īśam nitarām stuvanti mām brāhmaṇāḥ brahma mantraiḥ yajanti stauṣi garvāyase ca api svam ātmānam na saṃśayaḥ bhagavān uvāca saṃsrakṣyāmi varārohe bhāga arthe varavarṇini iti uktvā bhagavān patnīm umām prāṇaiḥ api priyām saḥ asṛjat bhagavān vaktrāt bhūtam krodha agni saṃbhavam nāśaya āśu kratum tasya dakṣasya mad anujñayā devyāḥ manyu kṛtam jñātvā hataḥ dakṣasya sa kratuḥ manyunā ca mahā bhīmā bhadrakālī maheśvarī ātmanaḥ karma sākṣi tve tena sārdham saha anugā saḥ eṣa bhagavān krodhaḥ preta āvāsa kṛta ālayaḥ saḥ asṛjat romakūpebhyaḥ ātmanā eva gaṇa īśvarān rudra anugān gaṇān raudrān rudra vīrya parākramān rudrasya anucarāḥ sarve sarve rudra parākramāḥ te nipetuḥ tatas tūrṇam śataśas atha sahasraśas tatas kilakilā śabdaḥ ākāśam pūrayan iva samabhūt su mahān viprāḥ sarva rudra gaṇaiḥ kṛtaḥ parvatāḥ ca vyaśīryanta cakampe ca vasuṃdharā marutaḥ ca vavuḥ krūrāḥ cukṣubhe varuṇālayaḥ grahāḥ na eva prakāśante nakṣatrāṇi na tārakāḥ ṛṣayaḥ na prabhāsante na devāḥ na ca dānavāḥ evam hi timirībhūte nirdahanti gaṇeśvarāḥ tvaritam vai pradhāvanti vāyu vegāḥ manaḥ javāḥ cūrṇyante yajña pātrāṇi yajñasya āyatanāni ca śīryamāṇāni adṛśyanta tārāḥ iva nabhastalāt divya anna pāna bhakṣyāṇām rāśayaḥ parvata upamāḥ kṣīra nadyaḥ tathā ca anyāḥ ghṛta pāyasa kardamāḥ madhumaṇḍa udakāḥ divyāḥ khaṇḍa śarkara vālukāḥ ṣaṣ rasān nivahanti anyāḥ guḍakulyāḥ manoramāḥ uccāvacāni māṃsāni bhakṣyāṇi vividhāni ca yāni kāni ca divyāni lehya coṣyāṇi yāni ca rudra kopāḥ mahā kopāḥ kālāgni sadṛśa upamāḥ bhakṣayantaḥ atha śaila ābhāḥ bhīṣayantaḥ ca sarvatas krīḍanti vividha ākārāḥ cikṣipuḥ sura yoṣitaḥ evam gaṇāḥ ca taiḥ yuktaḥ vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān tam yajñam adahat śīghram bhadrakālyāḥ samīpatas tatas śakra ādayaḥ devāḥ dakṣaḥ ca eva prajāpatiḥ ūcuḥ prāñjalayaḥ bhūtvā kathyatām kaḥ bhavān iti na eva draṣṭum ca deva indrāḥ na ca kautūhala anvitāḥ dakṣa yajña vināśa artham saṃprāptaḥ aham sura uttamāḥ vīrabhadra iti vikhyātaḥ rudra kopāt viniḥsṛtaḥ bhadrakālī ca vikhyātā devyāḥ krodhāt vinirgatā preṣitā devadevena yajña antikam upāgatā utpatadbhiḥ patadbhiḥ ca gṛdhraiḥ āmiṣa gṛdhnubhiḥ pakṣa vāta vinirdhūtaiḥ śivā ruta vināditaiḥ sa tasya yajñaḥ nṛpateḥ bādhyamānaḥ tadā gaṇaiḥ āsthāya mṛga rūpam vai kham eva abhyapatat tadā tam tu yajñam tathārūpam gacchantam upalabhya saḥ dhanuḥ ādāya bāṇam ca tad artham agamat prabhuḥ lalāṭāt prasṛtaḥ ghoraḥ sveda binduḥ babhūva ha prādurbhūtaḥ mahān agniḥ jvalat kāla anala upamaḥ hrasvaḥ atimātraḥ rakta akṣaḥ harit śmaśruḥ vibhīṣaṇaḥ ūrdhva keśaḥ ati roma aṅgaḥ śoṇa karṇaḥ tathā eva ca karāla kṛṣṇa varṇaḥ ca rakta vāsāḥ tathā eva ca tam yajñam sa mahā sattvaḥ adahat kakṣam iva analaḥ devāḥ ca pradrutāḥ sarve gatāḥ bhītāḥ diśaḥ daśa pṛthivī vyacalat sarvā saptadvīpā samantataḥ tadā ca aham mahādevam abravam pratipūjayan kriyatām pratisaṃhāraḥ sarva deva īśvara tvayā imāḥ ca devatāḥ sarvāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca sahasraśas yaḥ ca eṣa puruṣaḥ jātaḥ sveda jaḥ te surarṣabha samarthā sakalā pṛthvī bahudhā sṛjyatām ayam bhagavān mām tathā iti āha devadevaḥ pinākadhṛk parām ca prītim agamat sa svayam ca pinākadhṛk dakṣaḥ api manasā devam bhavam śaraṇam anvagāt prāṇa apānau samārudhya cakṣuḥ sthāne prayatnataḥ vidhārya sarvatas dṛṣṭim bahu dṛṣṭiḥ amitra jit smitam kṛtvā abravīt vākyam brūhi kim karavāṇi te śrāvite ca mahā ākhyāne devānām pitṛbhiḥ saha tam uvāca añjalim kṛtvā dakṣaḥ devam prajāpatiḥ bhītaḥ śaṅkita cittaḥ tu sa bāṣpa vadana īkṣaṇaḥ dakṣaḥ uvāca yat bhakṣyam bhakṣitam pītam trāsitam yat ca nāśitam cūrṇīkṛta apaviddham ca yajña saṃbhāram īdṛśam dharma adhyakṣam mahādevam tryambakam ca prajāpatiḥ jānubhyām avanīm gatvā dakṣaḥ labdhvā bhavāt varam nāmnām ca aṣṭa sahasreṇa stutavān vṛṣabhadhvajam evam dṛṣṭvā tadā dakṣaḥ śaṃbhoḥ vīryam dvijottamāḥ prāñjaliḥ praṇataḥ bhūtvā saṃstotum upacakrame dakṣaḥ uvāca deva indra tvam bala śreṣṭha deva dānava pūjita sahasrākṣa virūpākṣa tryakṣa yakṣādhipa priya sarvatas pāṇi pādaḥ tvam sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukhaḥ sarvatas śrutimān loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhasi śaṅkukarṇaḥ mahākarṇaḥ kumbhakarṇaḥ arṇavālayaḥ śatodaraḥ śatāvartaḥ śatajihvaḥ sanātanaḥ gāyanti tvām gāyatriṇaḥ arcayanti arkam arkiṇaḥ deva dānava goptā ca brahmā ca tvam śatakratuḥ mūrtimān tvam mahā mūrtiḥ samudraḥ sarasām nidhiḥ tvayi sarvāḥ devatāḥ hi gāvaḥ goṣṭhe iva āsate tvattaḥ śarīre paśyāmi somam agni jala īśvaram ādityam atha viṣṇum ca brahmāṇam sa bṛhaspatim kriyā karaṇa kārye ca kartā kāraṇam eva ca trijaṭāya triśīrṣāya triśūla vara dhāriṇe namaḥ caṇḍāya muṇḍāya viśva caṇḍa dharāya ca daṇḍine śaṅkukarṇāya daṇḍi daṇḍāya vai namaḥ namaḥ ardhadaṇḍi keśāya śuṣkāya vikṛtāya ca vilohitāya dhūmrāya nīlagrīvāya vai namaḥ namaḥ astu apratirūpāya virūpāya śivāya ca namaḥ pramatha nāśāya vṛṣa skandhāya vai namaḥ hiraṇya kṛta cūḍāya hiraṇyapataye namaḥ śatru ghātāya caṇḍāya parṇa saṃgha śayāya ca namaḥ stutāya stutaye stūyamānāya vai namaḥ sarvāya sarva bhakṣāya sarva bhūta antarātmane namaḥ tvām śayamānāya śayitāya utthitāya ca sthitāya dhāvamānāya kubjāya kuṭilāya ca namaḥ nartana śīlāya mukha vāditra kāriṇe bādhā apahāya lubdhāya gīta vāditra kāriṇe namaḥ jyeṣṭhāya śreṣṭhāya bala pramathanāya ca vibhīṣaṇāya bhīmāya bhīṣma vrata dharāya ca nānā vikṛta vaktrāya khaḍga jihvā ugra daṃṣṭriṇe pakṣa māsa lava ardhāya tumbī vīṇā priyāya ca namaḥ śivāya śāntāya namaḥ śāntatamāya ca namaḥ buddhāya śuddhāya saṃvibhāga priyāya ca pavanāya pataṃgāya namaḥ sāṃkhya parāya ca namaḥ caṇḍa eka ghaṇṭāya ghaṇṭā jalpāya ghaṇṭine sahasra śata ghaṇṭāya ghaṇṭā mālā priyāya ca prāṇa daṇḍāya nityāya namaḥ te lohitāya ca hūṃhūṃkārāya rudrāya bhaga ākāra priyāya ca yajña vāhāya dāntāya tapyāya ca bhagāya ca namaḥ taṭāya taṭyāya taṭinīpataye namaḥ namaḥ sahasra śīrṣāya sahasra caraṇāya ca namaḥ bāla arka varṇāya bāla rūpa dharāya ca namaḥ bāla arka rūpāya bāla krīḍanakāya ca namaḥ śuddhāya buddhāya kṣobhaṇāya kṣayāya ca taraṃga aṅkita keśāya muktakeśāya vai namaḥ namaḥ ṣaṣ karma niṣṭhāya tri karma niyatāya ca varṇa āśramāṇām vidhivat pṛthak dharma pravartine namaḥ śreṣṭhāya jyeṣṭhāya namaḥ kalakalāya ca śveta piṅgala netrāya kṛṣṇa rakta īkṣaṇāya ca sāṃkhyāya sāṃkhya mukhyāya yoga adhipataye namaḥ kṛṣṇājina uttarīyāya vyāla yajña upavītine īśāna rudra saṃghāta harikeśa namaḥ astu te kāla kāma da kāma ghna duṣṭa udvṛtta niṣūdana unmādana śatāvarta gaṅgā toya ārdra mūrdhaja jarāyu ja aṇḍa jāḥ ca eva sveda ja udbhid jaḥ eva ca carācarasya sraṣṭā tvam pratihartā tvam eva ca sarvasya paramā yoniḥ sudhā aṃśaḥ jyotiṣām nidhiḥ ṛk sāmāni tathā oṃkāram āhuḥ tvām brahma vādinaḥ hāyi hāyi hare hāyi huvāhāva iti vā asakṛt gāyanti tvām sura śreṣṭhāḥ sāma gāḥ brahma vādinaḥ yajuḥ mayaḥ ṛk mayaḥ ca sāma atharva yutaḥ tathā paṭhyase brahma vidbhiḥ tvam kalpa upaniṣadām gaṇaiḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ varṇa āśramāḥ ca ye saṃvatsaraḥ tvam ṛtavaḥ māsāḥ māsa ardham eva ca kalā kāṣṭhā nimeṣāḥ ca nakṣatrāṇi yugāni ca vṛṣāṇām kakudam tvam hi girīṇām śikharāṇi ca siṃhaḥ mṛgāṇām patayaḥ takṣaka ananta bhoginām kṣīrodaḥ hi udadhīnām ca mantrāṇām praṇavaḥ tathā vajram praharaṇānām ca vratānām satyam eva ca tvam eva icchā ca dveṣaḥ ca rāgaḥ mohaḥ śamaḥ kṣamā tvam gadī tvam śarī cāpī khaṭvāṅgī mudgarī tathā chettā bhettā prahartā ca netā mantāsi naḥ mataḥ daśa lakṣaṇa saṃyuktaḥ dharmaḥ arthaḥ kāmaḥ eva ca induḥ samudraḥ saritaḥ palvalāni sarāṃsi ca latā vallyaḥ tṛṇauṣadhyaḥ paśavaḥ mṛga pakṣiṇaḥ ādiḥ ca antaḥ ca madhyaḥ ca gāyatrī oṃkāraḥ eva ca haritaḥ lohitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ nīlaḥ pītaḥ tathā kṣaṇaḥ suvarṇaretāḥ vikhyātaḥ suvarṇaḥ ca api atho mataḥ pavitram ca pavitrāṇām maṅgalānām ca maṅgalam prāṇaḥ ca tvam rajaḥ ca tvam tamaḥ sattva yutaḥ tathā prāṇaḥ apānaḥ samānaḥ ca udānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca unmeṣaḥ ca nimeṣaḥ ca kṣudh tṛṣ jṛmbhā tathā eva ca lohitāṅgaḥ ca daṃṣṭrī ca mahāvaktraḥ mahodaraḥ śuci romā harit śmaśruḥ ūrdhva keśaḥ cala acalaḥ matsyaḥ jālaḥ jalaḥ ajayyaḥ jalavyālaḥ kuṭīcaraḥ vikālaḥ ca sukālaḥ ca duṣkālaḥ kālanāśanaḥ mṛtyuḥ ca eva akṣayaḥ antaḥ ca kṣamā māyā kara utkaraḥ ghaṇṭākī ghaṇṭakī ghaṇṭī cūḍālaḥ lavaṇa udadhiḥ brahmā kālāgni vaktraḥ ca daṇḍī muṇḍaḥ tridaṇḍa dhṛk cāturāśramya netā ca cāturvarṇya karaḥ ca ha kṣara akṣaraḥ priyaḥ dhūrtaḥ gaṇaiḥ gaṇyaḥ gaṇādhipaḥ śilpīśaḥ śilpinaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarva śilpi pravartakaḥ bhaga netra antakaḥ caṇḍaḥ pūṣṇaḥ danta vināśanaḥ svāhā svadhā vaṣaṭkāraḥ namaskāra namaḥ astu te gūḍha vrataḥ ca gūḍhaḥ ca gūḍha vrata niṣevitaḥ taraṇaḥ tāraṇaḥ ca eva sarva bhūteṣu tāraṇaḥ dhātā vidhātā saṃdhātā nidhātā dhāraṇaḥ dharaḥ brahmāvartaḥ surāvartaḥ kāmāvarta namaḥ astu te gonetā gopracāraḥ ca govṛṣa īśvara vāhanaḥ adharma hā mahā dakṣaḥ daṇḍadhāraḥ raṇa priyaḥ tiṣṭhan sthiraḥ ca sthāṇuḥ ca niṣkampaḥ ca su niścalaḥ śaśaḥ śaśāṅka nayana śīta uṣṇaḥ kṣudh tṛṣā jarā ādhayaḥ vyādhayaḥ ca eva vyādhi hā vyādhipaḥ ca yaḥ sahyaḥ yajña mṛga vyādhaḥ vyādhīnām ākaraḥ akaraḥ śikhaṇḍī puṇḍarīkaḥ ca puṇḍarīkāvalokanaḥ daṇḍadhṛk cakradaṇḍaḥ ca raudrabhāgavināśanaḥ viṣapaḥ amṛtapaḥ ca eva surāpaḥ kṣīrasomapaḥ madhupaḥ ca āpapaḥ ca eva sarvapaḥ ca balābalaḥ vṛṣā aṅgarāmbhaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ tathā vṛṣabhalocanaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ ca eva vikhyātaḥ lokānām loka saṃskṛtaḥ candra ādityau cakṣuṣī te hṛdayam ca pitāmahaḥ na brahmā na ca govindaḥ purāṇa ṛṣayaḥ na ca māhātmyam veditum śaktāḥ yāthātathyena te śiva śivāḥ yāḥ mūrtayaḥ sūkṣmāḥ te mahyam yāntu darśanam rakṣa mām rakṣaṇīyaḥ aham tava anagha namaḥ astu te bhakta anukampī bhagavān bhaktaḥ ca aham sadā tvayi yaḥ sahasrāṇi anekāni puṃsām āvṛtya durdṛśām tiṣṭhati ekaḥ samudra ante sa me goptā astu nityaśas yam vinidrāḥ jita śvāsāḥ sattva sthāḥ sama darśinaḥ jyotiḥ paśyanti yuñjānāḥ tasmai yoga ātmane namaḥ praviśya vadanam rāhoḥ yaḥ somam pibate niśi aṅguṣṭha mātrāḥ puruṣāḥ deha sthāḥ sarva dehinām rakṣantu te ca mām nityam nityam ca āpyāyayantu mām yena api utpāditāḥ garbhāḥ apaḥ bhāga gatāḥ ca ye teṣām svāhā svadhā ca eva āpnuvanti svadanti ca vṛkṣa mūleṣu goṣṭheṣu kāntāra gahaneṣu ca hasti aśva ratha śālāsu jīrṇa udyāna ālayeṣu ca yeṣu pañcasu bhūteṣu diśāsu vidiśāsu ca rasātala gatāḥ ye ca ye ca tasmāt param gatāḥ athavā māyayā deva mohitaḥ sūkṣmayā tava tasmāt tu kāraṇāt vā api tvam mayā na nimantritaḥ tvam gatiḥ tvam pratiṣṭhā ca na ca anyaḥ asti iti me matiḥ stutvā evam sa mahādevam virarāma mahāmatiḥ bhagavān api su prītaḥ punar dakṣam abhāṣata śrī bhagavān uvāca kṛtvā āśvāsa karam vākyam sarvajñaḥ vākya saṃhitam uvāca dakṣa duḥkham na kartavyam yajña vidhvaṃsanam prati aham yajña hanaḥ tubhyam dṛṣṭam etat purā anagha bhūyas ca tvam varam imam mattaḥ gṛhṇīṣva suvrata prasanna su mukhaḥ bhūtvā mama ekāgra manāḥ śṛṇu prajāpate mad prasādāt phala bhāgī bhaviṣyasi vedān ṣaṣ aṅgān budhyasva sāṃkhya yogān ca kṛtsnaśas tapaḥ ca vipulam taptvā duścaram deva dānavaiḥ samāgatam vyavasitam paśu pāśa vimokṣaṇam sarveṣām āśramāṇām ca mayā pāśupatam vratam utpāditam dakṣa śubham sarva pāpa vimocanam tat ca astu su mahābhāga mānasaḥ tyajyatām jvaraḥ evam uktvā tu deveśaḥ sa patnīkaḥ saha anugaḥ avāpya ca tathā bhāgam yathā uktam ca umayā bhavaḥ śānti artham sarva bhūtānām śṛṇudhvam atha vai dvijāḥ śikhā abhitāpaḥ nāgānām parvatānām śilājatu apām tu nīlikām vidyāt nirmokaḥ bhujageṣu ca khorakaḥ saurabheyāṇām ūkharaḥ pṛthivī tale śunām api ca dharma jñāḥ dṛṣṭi pratyavarodhanam randhrāgatam atha aśvānām śikhā udbhedaḥ ca barhiṇām netra rāgaḥ kokilānām dveṣaḥ proktaḥ mahātmanām janānām api bhedaḥ ca sarveṣām iti naḥ śrutam śukānām api sarveṣām hikkikā procyate jvaraḥ śārdūleṣu atha vai viprāḥ śramaḥ jvaraḥ iha ucyate mānuṣeṣu ca sarva jñāḥ jvaraḥ nāma eṣa kīrtitaḥ etat māheśvaram tejaḥ jvaraḥ nāma su dāruṇaḥ namasyaḥ ca eva mānyaḥ ca sarva prāṇibhiḥ īśvaraḥ imām jvara utpattim adīna mānasaḥ paṭhet sadā yaḥ su samāhitaḥ naraḥ labheta kāmān ca yathā manīṣitān dakṣa proktam stavam ca api kīrtayet yaḥ śṛṇoti vā na aśubham prāpnuyāt kiṃcid dīrgham āyuḥ avāpnuyāt yathā sarveṣu deveṣu variṣṭhaḥ bhagavān bhavaḥ tathā stavaḥ variṣṭhaḥ ayam stavānām dakṣa nirmitaḥ yaśaḥ svarga sura aiśvarya vitta ādi jaya kāṅkṣibhiḥ anena eva ca dehena gaṇānām ca maheśvarāt iha loke sukham prāpya gaṇa rāj upajāyate na yakṣāḥ na piśācāḥ vā na nāgāḥ na vināyakāḥ śṛṇuyāt vai idam nārī bhaktyā atha bhava bhāvitā pitṛ pakṣe bhartṛ pakṣe pūjyā bhavati ca eva ha śṛṇuyāt vai idam sarvam kīrtayet vā api abhīkṣṇaśas tasya sarvāṇi kāryāṇi siddhim gacchanti avighnataḥ manasā cintitam yat ca yat ca vācā api udāhṛtam tatas prayuktaḥ gṛhṇīyāt nāmāni āśu yathākramam īpsitān labhate api arthān kāmān bhogān ca mānavaḥ mṛtaḥ ca svargam āpnoti strī sahasra samāvṛtaḥ paṭhan dakṣa kṛtam stotram sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate mṛtaḥ ca gaṇa sāyujyam pūjyamānaḥ sura asuraiḥ vṛṣeṇa viniyuktena vimānena virājate ā bhūta saṃplava sthāyī rudrasya anucaraḥ bhavet iti āha bhagavān vyāsaḥ parāśara sutaḥ prabhuḥ śrutvā imam paramam guhyam ye api syuḥ pāpa yonayaḥ vaiśyāḥ striyaḥ ca śūdrāḥ ca rudra lokam avāpnuyuḥ lomaharṣaṇaḥ uvāca śrutvā evam vai muni śreṣṭhāḥ kathām pāpa praṇāśinīm rudra krodha udbhavām puṇyām vyāsasya vadataḥ dvijāḥ pārvatyāḥ ca tathā roṣam krodham śaṃbhoḥ ca duḥsaham dakṣa yajña vināśam ca vīryam śaṃbhoḥ tathā adbhutam punar prasādam devasya dakṣasya su mahātmanaḥ hṛṣṭāḥ babhūvuḥ saṃprītāḥ vismitāḥ ca punar punar papracchuḥ ca punar vyāsam kathā śeṣam tathā dvijāḥ pṛṣṭaḥ provāca tān vyāsaḥ kṣetram ekāmrakam punar vyāsaḥ uvāca brahma proktām kathām puṇyām śrutvā tu ṛṣi puṃgavāḥ praśaśaṃsuḥ tadā hṛṣṭāḥ romāñcita tanūruhāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ aho devasya māhātmyam tvayā śaṃbhoḥ prakīrtitam dakṣasya ca suraśreṣṭha yajña vidhvaṃsanam tathā vyāsaḥ uvāca teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā loka nāthaḥ caturmukhaḥ provāca śaṃbhoḥ tat kṣetram bhū tale duṣkṛta chadam śṛṇudhvam muni śārdūlāḥ pravakṣyāmi samāsatas liṅga koṭi samāyuktam vārāṇasī samam śubham ekāmraka iti vikhyātam tīrtha aṣṭaka samanvitam ekāmra vṛkṣaḥ tatra āsīt purā kalpe dvijottamāḥ hṛṣṭa puṣṭa jana ākīrṇam nara nārī samanvitam bhūyiṣṭham dhana dhānya ādi saṃyutam gṛha gopura saṃbādham tri kacā dvāra bhūṣitam nānā vaṇij samākīrṇam nānā ratna upaśobhitam pura aṭṭālaka saṃyuktam rathibhiḥ samalaṃkṛtam rājahaṃsa nibhaiḥ śubhraiḥ prāsādaiḥ upaśobhitam mārga ga dvāra saṃyuktam sita prākāra śobhitam rakṣitam śastra saṃghaiḥ ca parikhābhiḥ alaṃkṛtam sita raktaiḥ tathā pītaiḥ kṛṣṇa śyāmaiḥ ca varṇakaiḥ samīraṇa uddhatābhiḥ ca patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛtam vīṇā veṇu mṛdaṅgaiḥ ca kṣepaṇībhiḥ alaṃkṛtam devatāyatanaiḥ divyaiḥ prākāra udyāna maṇḍitaiḥ hāraiḥ alaṃkṛta grīvāḥ padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇāḥ pīna unnata kucāḥ śyāmāḥ pūrṇa candra nibha ānanāḥ sthira alakāḥ su kapolāḥ kāñcī nūpura nāditāḥ su keśyaḥ cāru jaghanāḥ karṇa anta āyata locanāḥ sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpannāḥ sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ divya vastra dharāḥ śubhrāḥ kāścid kāñcana saṃnibhāḥ haṃsa vāraṇa gāminyaḥ kuca bhāra avanāmitāḥ divya gandha anulipta aṅgāḥ karṇa ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ mada alasāḥ ca su śroṇyaḥ nityam prahasita ānanāḥ īṣat vispaṣṭa daśanāḥ bimba oṣṭhāḥ madhura svarāḥ tāmbūla rañjita mukhāḥ vidagdhāḥ priya darśanāḥ divya vastra dharāḥ sarvāḥ sadā cāritra maṇḍitāḥ krīḍanti tāḥ sadā tatra striyaḥ ca apsarasā upamāḥ sve sve gṛhe pramuditāḥ divā rātrau vara ānanāḥ puruṣāḥ tatra dṛśyante rūpa yauvana garvitāḥ sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpannāḥ sumṛṣṭa maṇi kuṇḍalāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca muni sattamāḥ anyāḥ ca tatra tiṣṭhanti vāramukhyāḥ su locanāḥ ghṛtācī menakā tulyāḥ tathā sama tila uttamāḥ urvaśī sadṛśāḥ ca eva vipracitti nibhāḥ tathā viśvācī sahajanya ābhāḥ pramlocā sadṛśāḥ tathā sarvāḥ tāḥ priya vādinyaḥ sarvāḥ vihasita ānanāḥ kalā kauśala saṃyuktāḥ sarvāḥ tāḥ guṇa saṃyutāḥ evam paṇya striyaḥ tatra nṛtya gīta viśāradāḥ nivasanti muni śreṣṭhāḥ sarva strī guṇa garvitāḥ prekṣaṇa ālāpa kuśalāḥ sundaryaḥ priya darśanāḥ na rūpa hīnāḥ durvṛttāḥ na para droha kārikāḥ yāsām kaṭākṣa pātena moham gacchanti mānavāḥ na rūpa hīnāḥ durvṛttāḥ na para droha kāriṇaḥ tiṣṭhanti mānavāḥ tatra kṣetre jagati viśrute nānā jana samākīrṇam sarva sasya samanvitam cūta nimba kadambaiḥ ca tathā anyaiḥ puṣpa jātibhiḥ śālaiḥ tālaiḥ tamālaiḥ ca nārikelaiḥ śubhāñjanaiḥ palāśaiḥ mucukundaiḥ ca pārijātaiḥ sa kubjakaiḥ kadalī vana khaṇḍaiḥ ca jambū pūga phalaiḥ tathā ketakī karavīraiḥ ca atimuktaiḥ ca kiṃśukaiḥ mandāra kunda puṣpaiḥ ca tathā anyaiḥ puṣpa jātibhiḥ cakoraiḥ śatapattraiḥ ca bhṛṅgarājaiḥ ca kokilaiḥ jīvaṃjīvaka hārītaiḥ cātakaiḥ vana veṣṭitaiḥ nānā pakṣi gaṇaiḥ ca anyaiḥ kūjadbhiḥ madhura svaraiḥ dīrghikābhiḥ taḍāgaiḥ ca puṣkariṇībhiḥ ca vāpibhiḥ nānā jalāśayaiḥ ca anyaiḥ padminī khaṇḍa maṇḍitaiḥ kumudaiḥ puṇḍarīkaiḥ ca tathā nīlotpalaiḥ śubhaiḥ kāraṇḍavaiḥ plavaiḥ haṃsaiḥ tathā anyaiḥ jalacāribhiḥ evam nānāvidhaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpaiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ varaiḥ nānā jalāśayaiḥ puṇyaiḥ śobhitam tat samantataḥ āste tatra svayam devaḥ kṛttivāsāḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ pṛthivyām yāni tīrthāni saritaḥ ca sarāṃsi ca puṣkariṇyaḥ taḍāgāni vāpyaḥ kūpāḥ ca sāgarāḥ tebhyaḥ pūrvam samāhṛtya jala bindūn pṛthak pṛthak cakāra ṛṣibhiḥ sārdham tena bindusaraḥ smṛtam aṣṭamyām bahule pakṣe mārgaśīrṣe dvijottamāḥ devān ṛṣīn manuṣyān ca pitṝn saṃtarpya vāgyataḥ graha uparāge viṣuve saṃkrāntyām ayane tathā yuga ādiṣu ṣaḍaśītyām tathā anyatra śubhe tithau piṇḍam ye saṃprayacchanti pitṛbhyaḥ sarasaḥ taṭe pitṝṇām akṣayām tṛptim te kurvanti na saṃśayaḥ tatas śaṃbhoḥ gṛham gatvā vāgyataḥ saṃyata indriyaḥ praviśya pūjayet śarvam kṛtvā tam tris pradakṣiṇam ghṛta kṣīra ādibhiḥ snānam kārayitvā bhavam śuciḥ a dīkṣitaḥ tu nāmnā eva mūlamantreṇa ca arcayet evam saṃpūjya tam devam gandha puṣpa anurāgibhiḥ daṇḍa vat praṇipātaiḥ ca gītaiḥ vādyaiḥ manoharaiḥ nṛtya japya namaskāraiḥ jaya śabdaiḥ pradakṣiṇaiḥ kula ekaviṃśam uddhṛtya divya ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ sauvarṇena vimānena kiṅkiṇī jāla mālinā uddyotayan diśaḥ sarvāḥ śiva lokam sa gacchati tat loka vāsibhiḥ sārdham yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam tatas tasmāt iha āyātaḥ pṛthivyām puṇya saṃkṣaye jāyate yoginām gehe catur vedī dvijottamāḥ yogam pāśupatam prāpya tatas mokṣam avāpnuyāt śayana utthāpane ca eva saṃkrāntyām ayane tathā aśokākhyām tathā aṣṭamyām pavitra āropaṇe tathā tasmin kṣetra vare liṅgam bhāskareśvara saṃjñitam paśyanti ye tu tam devam snātvā kuṇḍe maheśvaram ādityena arcitam pūrvam devadevam trilocanam sarva pāpa vinirmuktāḥ vimāna varam āsthitāḥ tiṣṭhanti tatra muditāḥ kalpam ekam dvijottamāḥ bhuktvā tu vipulān bhogān śiva loke manoramān puṇya kṣayāt iha āyātāḥ jāyante pravare kule athavā yoginām gehe veda vedāṅga pāragāḥ mokṣa śāstra artha kuśalāḥ sarvatra sama buddhayaḥ yogam śaṃbhoḥ varam prāpya tatas mokṣam vrajanti te tasmin kṣetra vare puṇye liṅgam yat dṛśyate dvijāḥ pūjya apūjyam ca sarvatra vane rathyā antare api vā catuṣpathe śmaśāne vā yatra kutra ca tiṣṭhati dṛṣṭvā tat liṅgam avyagraḥ śraddhayā su samāhitaḥ daṇḍa vat praṇipātaiḥ ca nṛtya gīta ādibhiḥ tathā saṃpūjya evam vidhānena śiva lokam vrajet naraḥ nārī vā dvija śārdūlāḥ saṃpūjya śraddhayā anvitā pūrva uktam phalam āpnoti na atra kāryā vicāraṇā kaḥ śaknoti guṇān vaktum samagrān muni sattamāḥ tasya kṣetra varasya atha ṛte devān maheśvarāt tasmin kṣetra uttame gatvā śraddhayā aśraddhayā api vā mādhava ādiṣu māseṣu naraḥ vā yadi vā aṅganā paśyet devam virūpākṣam devīm ca vara dām śivām gaṇam caṇḍam kārttikeyam gaṇeśam vṛṣabham tathā kalpadrumam ca sāvitrīm śiva lokam sa gacchati snātvā ca kāpile tīrthe vidhivat pāpa nāśane prāpnoti abhimatān kāmān śiva lokam sa gacchati ekāmrake śiva kṣetre vārāṇasī same śubhe viraje virajā mātā brahmāṇī saṃpratiṣṭhitā yasyāḥ saṃdarśanāt martyaḥ punāti āsaptamam kulam sakṛt dṛṣṭvā tu tām devīm bhaktyā āpūjya praṇamya ca anyāḥ ca tatra tiṣṭhanti viraje loka mātaraḥ āste vaitaraṇī tatra sarva pāpa harā nadī yasyām snātvā nara śreṣṭhaḥ sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate āste svayaṃbhūḥ tatra eva kroḍa rūpī hariḥ svayam dṛṣṭvā praṇamya tam bhaktyā param viṣṇum vrajanti te kāpile gograhe some tīrthe ca alābu saṃjñite mṛtyuṃjaye kroḍatīrthe vāsuke siddhakeśvare tīrtheṣu eteṣu matimān viraje saṃyata indriyaḥ gatvā aṣṭatīrtham vidhivat snātvā devān praṇamya ca sa karoti akṣayām tṛptim pitṝṇām na atra saṃśayaḥ snātvā yaḥ sāgare martyaḥ dṛṣṭvā ca kapilam harim paśyet devīm ca vārāhīm sa yāti tridaśālayam santi ca anyāni tīrthāni puṇyāni āyatanāni ca tad kāle tu muni śreṣṭhāḥ veditavyāni tāni vai āste guhyam param kṣetram mukti dam pāpa nāśanam sarvatra vālukā ākīrṇam pavitram sarva kāma dam aśoka arjuna puṃnāgaiḥ bakulaiḥ sarala drumaiḥ panasaiḥ nārikelaiḥ ca śālaiḥ tālaiḥ kapitthakaiḥ campakaiḥ karṇikāraiḥ ca cūta bilvaiḥ sa pāṭalaiḥ prācīnāmalakaiḥ lodhraiḥ nāraṅgaiḥ dhava khādiraiḥ sarja bhūrja aśvakarṇaiḥ ca tamālaiḥ devadārubhiḥ mandāraiḥ pārijātaiḥ ca nyagrodha aguru candanaiḥ kharjūra āmrātakaiḥ siddhaiḥ mucukundaiḥ sa kiṃśukaiḥ aśvatthaiḥ saptaparṇaiḥ ca madhu dhāra śubhāñjanaiḥ śiṃśapā āmalakaiḥ nīpaiḥ nimba tindu vibhītakaiḥ manaḥ hlāda karaiḥ śubhraiḥ nānā vihaga nāditaiḥ cakoraiḥ śatapattraiḥ ca bhṛṅgarājaiḥ tathā śukaiḥ kokilaiḥ kalaviṅkaiḥ ca hārītaiḥ jīvajīvakaiḥ śrotra ramyaiḥ priya karaiḥ kūjadbhiḥ cāru adhiṣṭhitaiḥ mālatī kunda bāṇaiḥ ca karavīraiḥ sitetaraiḥ jambīra karuṇā aṅkolaiḥ dāḍimaiḥ bījapūrakaiḥ mātuluṅgaiḥ pūga phalaiḥ hintālaiḥ kadalī vanaiḥ anyaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpaiḥ ca anyaiḥ manoharaiḥ latā vitāna gulmaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ ca jalāśayaiḥ dīrghikābhiḥ taḍāgaiḥ ca puṣkariṇībhiḥ ca vāpibhiḥ nānā jalāśayaiḥ puṇyaiḥ padminī khaṇḍa maṇḍitaiḥ kumudaiḥ puṇḍarīkaiḥ ca tathā nīlotpalaiḥ śubhaiḥ kahlāraiḥ kamalaiḥ ca api ācitāni samantataḥ kāraṇḍavaiḥ plavaiḥ haṃsaiḥ kūrmaiḥ matsyaiḥ ca madgubhiḥ dātyūha sārasa ākīrṇaiḥ koyaṣṭi baka śobhitaiḥ etaiḥ ca anyaiḥ ca kūjadbhiḥ samantāt jalacāribhiḥ evam nānāvidhaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpaiḥ sthala jala udbhavaiḥ hṛṣṭa puṣṭa jana ākīrṇam nara nārī samākulam aśeṣa vidyā nilayam sarva dharma guṇa ākaram āste tatra muni śreṣṭhāḥ vikhyātaḥ puruṣottamaḥ yāvat utkala maryādā diś krameṇa prakīrtitā tāvat kṛṣṇa prasādena deśaḥ puṇyatamaḥ hi saḥ yatra tiṣṭhati viśvātmā deśe sa puruṣottamaḥ aham rudraḥ ca śakraḥ ca devāḥ ca agni purogamāḥ nivasāmaḥ muni śreṣṭhāḥ tasmin deśe sadā vayam gandharva apsarasaḥ sarvāḥ pitaraḥ deva mānuṣāḥ yakṣāḥ vidyādharāḥ siddhāḥ munayaḥ saṃśita vratāḥ ṛṣayaḥ vālakhilyāḥ ca kaśyapa ādyāḥ prajeśvarāḥ suparṇāḥ kiṃnarāḥ nāgāḥ tathā anye svarga vāsinaḥ sa aṅgāḥ ca caturaḥ vedāḥ śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca itihāsa purāṇāni yajñāḥ ca vara dakṣiṇāḥ nadyaḥ ca vividhāḥ puṇyāḥ tīrthāni āyatanāni ca sāgarāḥ ca tathā śailāḥ tasmin deśe vyavasthitāḥ śreṣṭha tvam kasya deśasya kim ca anyat adhikam tatas tīrtha rāja jale snātvā paśyanti puruṣottamam saphalam jīvitam teṣām utkalānām sumedhasām cāru bhrū keśa mukuṭam cāru karṇa avataṃsakam cāru smitam cāru dantam cāru kuṇḍala maṇḍitam su nāsam su kapolam ca su lalāṭam su lakṣaṇam purā kṛta yuge viprāḥ śakra tulya parākramaḥ babhūva nṛpatiḥ śrīmān indradyumnaḥ iti śrutaḥ satya vādī śuciḥ dakṣaḥ sarva śāstra viśāradaḥ rūpavān subhagaḥ śūraḥ dātā bhoktā priyaṃvadaḥ yaṣṭā samasta yajñānām brahmaṇyaḥ satya saṃgaraḥ dhanurvede ca vede ca śāstre ca nipuṇaḥ kṛtī vallabhaḥ nara nārīṇām paurṇamāsyām yathā śaśī ādityaḥ iva duṣprekṣyaḥ śatru saṃgha bhayaṃkaraḥ adhyetā yoga sāṃkhyānām mumukṣuḥ dharma tatparaḥ evam sa pālayan pṛthvīm rājā sarva guṇa ākaraḥ katham ārādhayiṣyāmi devadevam janārdanam kasmin kṣetre athavā tīrthe nadī tīre tathā āśrame evam cintā paraḥ saḥ atha nirīkṣya manasā mahīm ālokya sarva tīrthāni kṣetrāṇi atha purāṇi api tāni sarvāṇi saṃtyajya jagāma āyatanam punar vikhyātam paramam kṣetram mukti dam puruṣottamam sa gatvā tat kṣetra varam samṛddha bala vāhanaḥ ayajat ca aśvamedhena vidhivat bhūri dakṣiṇaḥ kārayitvā mahā utsedham prāsādam ca eva viśrutam tatra saṃkarṣaṇam kṛṣṇam subhadrām sthāpya vīryavān pañcatīrtham ca vidhivat kṛtvā tatra mahīpatiḥ snānam dānam tapaḥ homam devatā prekṣaṇam tathā mārkaṇḍeyam ca kṛṣṇam ca dṛṣṭvā rāmam ca bho dvijāḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ jagāma paramam kṣetram mukti dam puruṣottamam gatvā tatra suraśreṣṭha katham sa nṛpa sattamaḥ prāsādam kārayām āsa ca iṣṭam trailokya viśrutam katham sa kṛṣṇam rāmam ca subhadrām ca prajāpate nirmame rāja śārdūlaḥ kṣetram rakṣitavān katham katham tatra mahīpālaḥ prāsāde bhuvana uttame sthāpayām āsa matimān kṛṣṇa ādīn tridaśa arcitān vaktum arhasi aśeṣeṇa caritam tasya dhīmataḥ sādhu sādhu dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ yat pṛcchadhvam purātanam vakṣyāmi tasya caritam yathāvṛttam kṛte yuge śṛṇudhvam muni śārdūlāḥ prayatāḥ saṃyata indriyāḥ avantī nāma nagarī mālave bhuvi viśrutā babhūva tasya nṛpateḥ pṛthivī kakuda upamā hṛṣṭa puṣṭa jana ākīrṇā dṛḍha prākāra toraṇā dṛḍha yantra argala dvārā parikhābhiḥ alaṃkṛtā nānā vaṇij samākīrṇā nānā bhāṇḍa su vikriyā rathyā āpaṇavatī ramyā suvibhakta catuṣpathā gṛha gopura saṃbādhā vīthībhiḥ samalaṃkṛtā rājahaṃsa nibhaiḥ śubhraiḥ citra grīvaiḥ manoharaiḥ aneka śata sāhasraiḥ prāsādaiḥ samalaṃkṛtā nānā varṇa patākābhiḥ dhvajaiḥ ca samalaṃkṛtā hasti aśva ratha saṃkīrṇā padāti gaṇa saṃkulā nānā yodha samākīrṇā nānā janapadaiḥ yutā brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiḥ ca eva dvijātibhiḥ samṛddhā sā muni śreṣṭhāḥ vidvadbhiḥ samalaṃkṛtā na tatra malināḥ santi na mūrkhāḥ na api nirdhanāḥ na rogiṇaḥ na hīna aṅgāḥ na dyūta vyasana anvitāḥ sadā hṛṣṭāḥ sumanasaḥ dṛśyante puruṣāḥ striyaḥ krīḍanti sma divā rātrau hṛṣṭāḥ tatra pṛthak pṛthak su veṣāḥ puruṣāḥ tatra dṛśyante mṛṣṭa kuṇḍalāḥ surūpāḥ su guṇāḥ ca eva divya alaṃkāra bhūṣitāḥ kāmadeva pratīkāśāḥ sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣitāḥ su keśāḥ su kapolāḥ ca su mukhāḥ śmaśru dhāriṇaḥ jñātāraḥ sarva śāstrāṇām bhettāraḥ śatru vāhinīm dātāraḥ sarva ratnānām bhoktāraḥ sarva saṃpadām striyaḥ tatra muni śreṣṭhāḥ dṛśyante su manoharāḥ haṃsa vāraṇa gāminyaḥ praphulla ambhoja locanāḥ su madhyamāḥ su jaghanāḥ pīna unnata payodharāḥ su keśāḥ cāru vadanāḥ su kapolāḥ sthira alakāḥ hāva bhāva ānata grīvāḥ karṇa ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ bimba oṣṭhyaḥ rañjita mukhāḥ tāmbūlena virājitāḥ suvarṇa ābharaṇa upetāḥ sarva alaṃkāra bhūṣitāḥ śyāma avadātāḥ su śroṇyaḥ kāñcī nūpura nāditāḥ divya mālya ambara dharāḥ divya gandha anulepanāḥ vidagdhāḥ subhagāḥ kāntāḥ cāru aṅgyaḥ priya darśanāḥ rūpa lāvaṇya saṃyuktāḥ sarvāḥ prahasita ānanāḥ krīḍantyaḥ ca mada unmattāḥ sabhāsu catvareṣu ca gīta vādya kathā ālāpaiḥ ramayantyaḥ ca tāḥ striyaḥ vāramukhyāḥ ca dṛśyante nṛtya gīta viśāradāḥ prekṣaṇa ālāpa kuśalāḥ sarva yoṣit guṇa anvitāḥ anyāḥ ca tatra dṛśyante guṇa ācāryāḥ kulastriyaḥ pativratāḥ ca subhagāḥ guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ śālaiḥ tālaiḥ tamālaiḥ ca bakulaiḥ nāgakesaraiḥ nāraṅgaiḥ lakucaiḥ lodhraiḥ saptaparṇaiḥ śubhāñjanaiḥ cūta bilva kadambaiḥ ca śiṃśapaiḥ dhava khādiraiḥ pāṭalā aśoka tagaraiḥ karavīraiḥ sitetaraiḥ pīta arjunaka bhallātaiḥ siddhaiḥ āmrātakaiḥ tathā nyagrodha aśvattha kāśmaryaiḥ palāśaiḥ devadārubhiḥ mandāraiḥ pārijātaiḥ ca tintiḍīka vibhītakaiḥ prācīnāmalakaiḥ plakṣaiḥ jambū śirīṣa pādapaiḥ kāleyaiḥ kāñcanāraiḥ ca madhu jambīra tindukaiḥ kharjūra agastya bakulaiḥ śākhoṭaka harītakaiḥ mallikā kunda bāṇaiḥ ca kadalī khaṇḍa maṇḍitaiḥ mātuluṅgaiḥ pūgaphalaiḥ karuṇaiḥ sindhuvārakaiḥ anyaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ puṣpa vṛkṣaiḥ ca anyaiḥ manoharaiḥ sadā kusuma gandha āḍhyaiḥ sadā phala bhara ānataiḥ nānā pakṣi rutaiḥ ramyaiḥ nānā mṛga gaṇa āvṛtaiḥ cakoraiḥ śatapattraiḥ ca bhṛṅgāraiḥ priyaputrakaiḥ kapotaiḥ khañjarīṭaiḥ ca śyenaiḥ pārāvataiḥ tathā saritaḥ puṣkariṇyaḥ ca sarāṃsi su bahūni ca anyaiḥ jalāśayaiḥ puṇyaiḥ kumuda utpala maṇḍitaiḥ haṃsa kāraṇḍava ākīrṇaiḥ cakravāka upaśobhitaiḥ sārasaiḥ ca balākaiḥ ca kūrmaiḥ matsyaiḥ sa nakrakaiḥ khagaiḥ jalacaraiḥ ca anyaiḥ nānā rava vibhūṣitaiḥ nānā varṇaiḥ sadā hṛṣṭaiḥ añcitāni samantataḥ evam nānāvidhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ vividhaiḥ ca jalāśayaiḥ devatāyatanaiḥ divyaiḥ śobhitā sā mahā purī mahākāla iti vikhyātaḥ sarva kāma pradaḥ śivaḥ śivakuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā vidhivat pāpa nāśane devān pitṝn ṛṣīn ca eva saṃtarpya vidhivat budhaḥ gatvā śivālayam paścāt kṛtvā tam tris pradakṣiṇam praviśya saṃyataḥ bhūtvā dhauta vāsāḥ jita indriyaḥ snānaiḥ puṣpaiḥ tathā gandhaiḥ dhūpaiḥ dīpaiḥ ca bhaktitaḥ naivedyaiḥ upahāraiḥ ca gīta vādyaiḥ pradakṣiṇaiḥ daṇḍa vat praṇipātaiḥ ca nṛtyaiḥ stotraiḥ ca śaṃkaram saṃpūjya vidhivat bhaktyā mahākālam sakṛt śivam pāpaiḥ sarvaiḥ vinirmuktaḥ vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ divya rūpa dharaḥ śrīmān divya alaṃkāra bhūṣitaḥ bhuṅkte tatra varān bhogān yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam śiva loke muni śreṣṭhāḥ jarā maraṇa varjitaḥ puṇya kṣayāt iha āyātaḥ pravare brāhmaṇe kule catur vedī bhavet vipraḥ sarva śāstra viśāradaḥ yogam pāśupatam prāpya tatas mokṣam avāpnuyāt āste tatra nadī puṇyā śiprā nāma iti viśrutā tasyām snātaḥ tu vidhivat saṃtarpya pitṛ devatāḥ tam dṛṣṭvā muktim āpnoti tri sapta kula saṃyutaḥ vimānena arka varṇena kiṅkiṇī jāla mālinā bhuṅkte ca vividhān kāmān nirātaṅkaḥ gata jvaraḥ ābhūtasaṃplavam yāvat surūpaḥ subhagaḥ sukhī kālena āgatya matimān brāhmaṇaḥ syāt mahī tale vaiṣṇavam yogam āsthāya tatas mokṣam avāpnuyāt vikramasvāmi nāmānam viṣṇum tatra eva bho dvijāḥ dṛṣṭvā naraḥ vā nārī vā phalam pūrva uditam labhet anye api tatra tiṣṭhanti devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ mātaraḥ ca muni śreṣṭhāḥ sarva kāma phala pradāḥ dṛṣṭvā tān vidhivat bhaktyā saṃpūjya praṇipatya ca evam sā nagarī ramyā rāja siṃhena pālitā pura aṣṭādaśa saṃyuktā su vistīrṇa catuṣpathā dhanuḥ jyā ghoṣa ninadā siddha saṃgama bhūṣitā vidyāvat gaṇa bhūyiṣṭhā veda nirghoṣa nāditā itihāsa purāṇāni śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca kāvya ālāpa kathāḥ ca eva śrūyante aharniśam dvijāḥ evam mayā guṇa āḍhyā sā samudāhṛtā yasyām rājā abhavat pūrvam indradyumnaḥ mahāmatiḥ tasyām sa nṛpatiḥ pūrvam kurvan rājyam anuttamam pālayām āsa matimān prajāḥ putrān iva aurasān satya vādī mahā prājñaḥ śūraḥ sarva guṇa ākaraḥ matimān dharma saṃpannaḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ satyavān śīlavān dāntaḥ śrīmān parapuraṃjayaḥ vardhamāna sura āścaryaḥ śakra tulya parākramaḥ śārada induḥ iva ābhāti lakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ āhartā sarva yajñānām hayamedha ādi kṛt tathā suvarṇa maṇi muktānām gaja aśvānām ca bhūpatiḥ hasti aśva ratha mukhyānām kambala ajina vāsasām sarva kāma samṛddha ātmā kurvan rājyam akaṇṭakam vicārya sarva śāstrāṇi tantrāṇi āgama vistaram itihāsa purāṇāni vedāṅgāni ca sarvaśas dharma śāstrāṇi sarvāṇi niyamān ṛṣi bhāṣitān vedāṅgāni ca śāstrāṇi vidyā sthānāni yāni ca gurum saṃsevya yatnena brāhmaṇān vedapāragān ādhāya paramām kāṣṭhām kṛtakṛtyaḥ abhavat tadā bhrānti jñānāt atītaḥ tu mumukṣuḥ saṃyata indriyaḥ katham ārādhayiṣyāmi devadevam sanātanam pīta vastram catur bāhum śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam vanamālā vṛta uraskam padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇam śrīvatsa uraḥ samāyuktam mukuṭa aṅgada śobhitam sva purāt sa tu niṣkrāntaḥ ujjayinyāḥ prajāpatiḥ anujagmuḥ tu tam sarve rathinaḥ śastra pāṇayaḥ rathaiḥ vimāna saṃkāśaiḥ patākā dhvaja sevitaiḥ sādinaḥ ca tathā sarve prāsa tomara pāṇayaḥ aśvaiḥ pavana saṃkāśaiḥ anujagmuḥ tu tam nṛpam īṣā dantaiḥ sadā mattaiḥ pracaṇḍaiḥ ṣaṣṭihāyanaiḥ hema kakṣaiḥ sa patākaiḥ ghaṇṭā rava vibhūṣitaiḥ anujagmuḥ ca tam sarve gaja yuddha viśāradāḥ asaṃkhyeyāḥ ca pādātāḥ dhanuṣprāsa asi pāṇayaḥ divya mālya ambara dharāḥ divya gandha anulepanāḥ anujagmuḥ ca tam sarve yuvānaḥ mṛṣṭa kuṇḍalāḥ sarva astra kuśalāḥ śūrāḥ sadā saṃgrāma lālasāḥ antaḥpura nivāsinyaḥ striyaḥ sarvāḥ su alaṃkṛtāḥ bimba oṣṭha cāru daśanāḥ sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ divya vastra dharāḥ sarvāḥ divya mālya vibhūṣitāḥ divya gandha anulipta aṅgāḥ śarad candra nibha ānanāḥ su madhyamāḥ cāru veṣāḥ cāru karṇa alaka āñcitāḥ tāmbūla rañjita mukhāḥ rakṣibhiḥ ca su rakṣitāḥ yānaiḥ uccāvacaiḥ śubhraiḥ maṇi kāñcana bhūṣitaiḥ upagīyamānāḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ gāyanaiḥ stuti pāṭhakaiḥ veṣṭitāḥ śastra hastaiḥ ca padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ anujagmuḥ ca tam nṛpam vaṇij grāma gaṇāḥ sarve nānā pura nivāsinaḥ dhanaiḥ ratnaiḥ suvarṇaiḥ ca sa dārāḥ sa paricchadāḥ astra vikrayakāḥ ca eva tāmbūla paṇya jīvinaḥ tṛṇa vikrayakāḥ ca eva kāṣṭha vikraya kārakāḥ raṅga upajīvinaḥ sarve māṃsa vikrayiṇaḥ tathā tathā java sahārāḥ ca rajakāḥ ca sahasraśas gopālāḥ nāpitāḥ ca eva tathā anye vastrasūcakāḥ meṣa pālāḥ ca aja pālāḥ mṛga pālāḥ ca haṃsakāḥ guḍa vikrayikāḥ ca eva tathā lavaṇa jīvinaḥ gāyanāḥ nartakāḥ ca eva tathā maṅgalapāṭhakāḥ śailūṣāḥ kathakāḥ ca eva purāṇa artha viśāradāḥ kavayaḥ kāvya kartāraḥ nānā kāvya viśāradāḥ viṣa ghnāḥ gāruḍāḥ ca eva nānā ratna parīkṣakāḥ vyokārāḥ tāmrakārāḥ ca kāṃsyakārāḥ ca rūṭhakāḥ kauṣakārāḥ citrakārāḥ kundakārāḥ ca pāvakāḥ daṇḍakārāḥ ca asikārāḥ surā dhūta upajīvinaḥ mallāḥ dūtāḥ ca kāyasthāḥ ye ca anye karma kāriṇaḥ tantuvāyāḥ rūpakārāḥ vārtikāḥ tailapāṭhakāḥ lāvajīvāḥ taittirikāḥ mṛga pakṣi upajīvinaḥ gaja vaidyāḥ ca vaidyāḥ ca nara vaidyāḥ ca ye narāḥ vṛkṣa vaidyāḥ ca go vaidyāḥ ye ca anye cheda dāhakāḥ ete nāgarakāḥ sarve ye ca anye na anukīrtitāḥ yathā vrajantam pitaram grāma antaram samutsukāḥ anuyānti yathā putrāḥ tathā tam te api nāgarāḥ evam sa nṛpatiḥ śrīmān vṛtaḥ sarvaiḥ mahājanaiḥ hasti aśva ratha pādātaiḥ jagāma ca śanais śanais evam gatvā sa nṛpatiḥ dakṣiṇasya udadheḥ taṭam nānā ratna ālayam pūrṇam nānā prāṇi samākulam vīcī taraṅga bahulam mahā āścarya samanvitam tīrtha rājam mahā śabdam apāram su bhayaṃkaram megha vṛnda pratīkāśam agādham makara ālayam matsyaiḥ kūrmaiḥ ca śaṅkhaiḥ ca śuktikā nakra śaṅkubhiḥ śiṃśumāraiḥ karkaṭaiḥ ca vṛtam sarpaiḥ mahāviṣaiḥ lavaṇodam hareḥ sthānam śayanasya nadīpatim sarva pāpa haram puṇyam sarva vāñchā phala pradam aneka āvarta gambhīram dānavānām samāśrayam amṛtasya araṇim divyam devayonim apām patim viśiṣṭam sarva bhūtānām prāṇinām jīva dhāraṇam su pavitram pavitrāṇām maṅgalānām ca maṅgalam tīrthānām uttamam tīrtham avyayam yādasām patim abhedyam sarva bhūtānām devānām amṛta ālayam upajīvyam ca sarveṣām puṇyam nadanadīpatim dṛṣṭvā tam nṛpati śreṣṭhaḥ vismayam paramam gataḥ vṛtam śālaiḥ kadambaiḥ ca puṃnāgaiḥ sarala drumaiḥ tālaiḥ pippalaiḥ kharjūraiḥ nāraṅgaiḥ bījapūrakaiḥ kapitthaiḥ karṇikāraiḥ ca pāṭalā aśoka campakaiḥ dāḍimaiḥ ca tamālaiḥ ca pārijātaiḥ tathā arjunaiḥ prācīnāmalakaiḥ bilvaiḥ priyaṅgu vaṭa khādiraiḥ iṅgudī saptaparṇaiḥ ca aśvattha agastya jambukaiḥ madhukaiḥ karṇikāraiḥ ca bahuvāraiḥ sa tindukaiḥ palāśa badaraiḥ nīpaiḥ siddhanimba śubhāñjanaiḥ vārakaiḥ kovidāraiḥ ca bhallāta āmalakaiḥ tathā iti hintālaka aṅkolaiḥ karañjaiḥ sa vibhītakaiḥ sa sarja madhu kāśmaryaiḥ śālmalī devadārubhiḥ śākhoṭhakaiḥ nimba vaṭaiḥ kumbhīkā oṣṭha harītakaiḥ guggulaiḥ candanaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ tathā eva aguru pāṭalaiḥ jambīra karuṇaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ tintiḍī raktacandanaiḥ evam nānāvidhaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ tathā anyaiḥ bahu pādapaiḥ mayūra vara saṃghuṣṭaiḥ śuka sārika saṃkulaiḥ hārītaiḥ bhṛṅgarājaiḥ ca cātakaiḥ bahuputrakaiḥ jīvaṃjīvaka kākolaiḥ kalaviṅkaiḥ kapotakaiḥ puṣpita agreṣu vṛkṣeṣu kūjadbhiḥ cāru adhiṣṭhitaiḥ ketakī vana khaṇḍaiḥ ca sadā puṣpa dharaiḥ sitaiḥ kuṭajaiḥ bāṇapuṣpaiḥ ca atimuktaiḥ sa kubjakaiḥ mālatī karavīraiḥ ca tathā kadala kāñcanaiḥ anyaiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ su gandhaiḥ cāru darśanaiḥ vidyādhara gaṇa ākīrṇaiḥ siddha cāraṇa sevitaiḥ muni yakṣa gaṇa ākīrṇaiḥ nānā sattva niṣevitaiḥ mṛgaiḥ śākhāmṛgaiḥ siṃhaiḥ varāha mahiṣa ākulaiḥ tathā anyaiḥ kṛṣṇasāra ādyaiḥ mṛgaiḥ sarvatra śobhitaiḥ śārdūlaiḥ dīpta mātaṅgaiḥ tathā anyaiḥ vana cāribhiḥ evam nānāvidhaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ udyānaiḥ nandana upamaiḥ latā gulma vitānaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ ca jalāśayaiḥ haṃsa kāraṇḍava ākīrṇaiḥ padminī khaṇḍa maṇḍitaiḥ kādambaiḥ ca plavaiḥ haṃsaiḥ cakravāka upaśobhitaiḥ parvataiḥ dīpta śikharaiḥ cāru kandara maṇḍitaiḥ nānā vṛkṣa samākīrṇaiḥ nānā dhātu vibhūṣitaiḥ sarva āścarya mayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ sarva bhūta ālayaiḥ śubhaiḥ dadarśa sa mahīpālaḥ sthānam trailokya pūjitam daśa yojana vistīrṇam pañca yojanam āyatam nānā āścarya samāyuktam kṣetram parama durlabham munayaḥ ūcuḥ kim tatra pratimā pūrvam na sthitā vaiṣṇavī prabho sthāpayām āsa kṛṣṇam ca rāmam bhadrām śubha pradām śrotum icchāmahe sarvam brūhi tad kāraṇam ca naḥ śṛṇudhvam pūrva saṃvṛttām kathām pāpa praṇāśinīm pravakṣyāmi samāsena śriyā pṛṣṭaḥ purā hariḥ sumeroḥ kāñcane śṛṅge sarva āścarya samanvite anyaiḥ devālayaiḥ sādhyaiḥ kaśyapa ādyaiḥ prajeśvaraiḥ jātarūpa pratīkāśaiḥ bhūṣite sūrya saṃnibhaiḥ anyaiḥ ca bahubhiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ śāla tāla ādibhiḥ vanaiḥ puṃnāga aśoka sarala nyagrodha āmrātaka arjunaiḥ dhava khādira pālāśa śīrṣa āmalaka tindukaiḥ nāriṅga kola bakula lodhra dāḍima dārukaiḥ sarjaiḥ ca karṇaiḥ tagaraiḥ śiśi bhūrja vanimbakaiḥ anyaiḥ ca kāñcanaiḥ ca eva phala bhāraiḥ ca nāmitaiḥ nānā kusuma gandha āḍhyaiḥ bhūṣite puṣpa pādapaiḥ pāṭalā agastya kuṭaja mandāra kusuma ādibhiḥ anyaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ manasaḥ prīti dāyakaiḥ evam nānāvidhaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpaiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ tathā praṇamya śirasā devī lokānām hita kāmyayā śrīḥ uvāca brūhi tvam sarva loka īśa saṃśayam me hṛdi sthitam yena mucyeta deveśa asmāt saṃsāra sāgarāt ācakṣva sarva deva īśa praṇatām yadi manyase tvat ṛte nā asti loke asmin vaktā saṃśaya nirṇaye śrutvā evam vacanam tasyāḥ devadevaḥ janārdanaḥ provāca parayā prītyā param sāra amṛta upamam śrī bhagavān uvāca sukha upāsyaḥ susādhyaḥ ca abhirāmaḥ ca su sat phalaḥ āste tīrtha vare devi vikhyātaḥ puruṣottamaḥ na tena sadṛśaḥ kaścid triṣu lokeṣu vidyate tat te aham saṃpravakṣyāmi tīrtha rājam ca sāṃpratam bhāvena ekena suśroṇi śṛṇuṣva varavarṇini āsīt kalpe samutpanne naṣṭe sthāvara jaṅgame tamaḥ bhūtam idam sarvam na prājñāyata kiṃcana tasmin jāgarti bhūtātmā paramātmā jagadguruḥ śrīmān tri mūrti kṛt devaḥ jagatkartā maheśvaraḥ vāsudeva iti vikhyātaḥ yoga ātmā hariḥ īśvaraḥ padma kesara saṃkāśam brahmāṇam bhūtam avyayam tādṛś bhūtaḥ tatas brahmā sarva loka mahā īśvaraḥ pañcabhūta samāyuktam sṛjate ca śanais śanais mātrā yonīni bhūtāni sthūla sūkṣmāṇi yāni ca caturvidhāni sarvāṇi sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca saṃcintya manasā ātmānam sasarja vividhāḥ prajāḥ marīci ādīn munīn sarvān deva asura pitṝn api yakṣa vidyādharān ca anyān gaṅgā ādyāḥ saritaḥ tathā nara vānara siṃhān ca vividhān ca vihaṃgamān jarāyūn aṇḍa jān devi sveda ja udbheda jān tathā brahma kṣatram tathā vaiśyam śūdram ca eva catuṣṭayam antya jātān ca mlecchān ca sasarja vividhān pṛthak yat kiṃcid jīva saṃjñam tu tṛṇa gulma pipīlikam dakṣiṇa aṅge tathā ātmānam saṃcintya puruṣam svayam vāme ca eva tu nārīm sa dvidhā bhūtam akalpayat adhama uttama madhyāḥ ca mama kṣetrāṇi yāni ca jagāma dhyānam āsthāya vāsudeva ātmikām tanum tasmin kṣaṇe samutpannaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapād sahasra śīrṣā puruṣaḥ puṇḍarīka nibha īkṣaṇaḥ salila dhvānta megha ābhaḥ śrīmān śrīvatsa lakṣaṇaḥ apaśyat sahasā tam tu brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ tuṣṭāva paramaiḥ stotraiḥ viriñciḥ su samāhitaḥ kāraṇam vada mām tāta mama dhyānasya sāṃpratam svarga dvārasya mārgāṇi yajña dāna vratāni ca yogaḥ satyam tapaḥ śraddhā tīrthāni vividhāni ca vihāya sarvam eteṣām sukham tad sādhanam vada sthānam jagatpate mahyām utkṛṣṭam ca yat ucyate sarveṣām uttamam sthānam brūhi me puruṣottama uttamam sarva kṣetrāṇām dhanyam saṃsāra tāraṇam go brāhmaṇa hitam puṇyam cāturvarṇya sukha udayam bhukti mukti pradam nṝṇām kṣetram parama durlabham mahā puṇyam tu sarveṣām siddhi dam vai pitāmahe tasmāt āsīt samutpannam tīrtha rājam sanātanam sarveṣām eva devānām ṛṣīṇām brahmacāriṇām nāga vidyādharāṇām ca sthāvarasya carasya ca uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ yasmāt tasmāt sa puruṣottamaḥ dṛṣṭa mātre vaṭe tasmin chāyām ākramya ca asakṛt pradakṣiṇā kṛtā yaiḥ tu namaskāraḥ ca jantubhiḥ sarve vidhūta pāpmānaḥ te gatāḥ keśava ālayam pratimām tatra vai dṛṣṭvā svayam devena nirmitām anāyāsena vai yānti bhuvanam me tatas narāḥ gacchamānān tu tān prekṣya ekadā dharmarāj priye kṣīroda vāsinam devam śeṣa bhoga anuśāyinam varam vareṇyam vara dam kartāram a kṛtam prabhum viśveśvaram ajam viṣṇum sarvajñam aparājitam nīlotpala dala śyāmam puṇḍarīka nibha īkṣaṇam sarvajñam nirguṇam śāntam jagat dhātāram avyayam purāṇam puruṣam vedyam vyakta avyaktam sanātanam parāvarāṇām sraṣṭāram loka nātham jagadgurum śrīvatsa uraska saṃyuktam vanamālā vibhūṣitam pīta vastram catur bāhum śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam hāra keyūra saṃyuktam mukuṭa aṅgada dhāriṇam kūṭastham acalam sūkṣmam jyotiḥ rūpam sanātanam bhāva abhāva vinirmuktam vyāpinam prakṛteḥ param stutvā nānāvidhaiḥ stotraiḥ praṇāmam akarot tadā tam dṛṣṭvā tu mahābhāge praṇatam prāñjali sthitam stotrasya kāraṇam devi pṛṣṭavān aham antakam kimartham stutavān mām tvam saṃkṣepāt tat bravīhi me indranīla mayī śreṣṭhā pratimā sārvakāmikī tām dṛṣṭvā puṇḍarīkākṣa bhāvena ekena śraddhayā śveta ākhyam bhavanam yānti niṣkāmāḥ ca eva mānavāḥ atas kartum na śaknomi vyāpāram ari sūdana yama tām gopayiṣyāmi sikatābhiḥ samantataḥ yathā tatra na paśyanti manujāḥ svarga kāṅkṣiṇaḥ yamam prasthāpayām āsa svām purīm dakṣiṇām diśam luptāyām pratimāyām tu indranīlasya bho dvijāḥ tam sarvam kathayām āsa sa tasyai bhagavān purā kṣetrasya varṇanam ca eva prāsāda karaṇam tathā lavaṇasya udadheḥ tīre kāṣṭhasya darśanam tathā darśanam vāsudevasya śilpi rājasya ca dvijāḥ nirmāṇam pratimāyāḥ tu yathāvarṇam viśeṣataḥ sthāpanam ca eva sarveṣām prāsāde bhuvana uttame yātrā kāle ca vipra indrāḥ kalpa saṃkīrtanam tathā mārkaṇḍeyasya caritam sthāpanam śaṃkarasya ca pañcatīrthasya māhātmyam darśanam śūlapāṇinaḥ vaṭasya darśanam ca eva vyuṣṭim tasya ca bho dvijāḥ darśanam baladevasya kṛṣṇasya ca viśeṣataḥ subhadrāyāḥ ca tatra eva māhātmyam ca eva sarvaśas darśanam narasiṃhasya vyuṣṭi saṃkīrtanam tathā śvetamādhavamāhātmyam svargadvārasya darśanam pañca tīrtha phalam ca eva mahājyeṣṭham tathā eva ca sthānam kṛṣṇasya halinaḥ parva yātrā phalam tathā varṇanam viṣṇu lokasya kṣetrasya ca punar punar munayaḥ ūcuḥ śrotum icchāmahe deva kathā śeṣam mahīpateḥ tasmin kṣetra vare gatvā kim cakāra narādhipaḥ śṛṇudhvam muni śārdūlāḥ pravakṣyāmi samāsatas kṣetra saṃdarśanam ca eva kṛtyam tasya ca bhūpateḥ dadarśa ramaṇīyāni sthānāni saritaḥ tathā nadī tatra mahā puṇyā vindhya pāda vinirgatā svittropalā iti vikhyātā sarva pāpa harā śivā gaṅgā tulyā mahā srotāḥ dakṣiṇa arṇava gāminī mahānadī iti nāmnā sā puṇya toyā sarit varā dakṣiṇasya udadheḥ garbham gatā āvartā ati śobhitā ubhayoḥ taṭayoḥ yasyāḥ grāmāḥ ca nagarāṇi ca dṛśyante muni śārdūlāḥ su sasyāḥ su manoharāḥ hṛṣṭa puṣṭa jana ākīrṇāḥ vastra alaṃkāra bhūṣitāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ tatra pṛthak pṛthak svadharma niratāḥ śāntāḥ dṛśyante śubha lakṣaṇāḥ tāmbūla pūrṇa vadanāḥ mālā dāma vibhūṣitāḥ veda pūrṇa mukhāḥ viprāḥ sa ṣaḍaṅga padakramāḥ sarva śāstra artha kuśalāḥ yajvānaḥ bhūri dakṣiṇāḥ catvāre rājamārgeṣu vaneṣu upavaneṣu ca sabhā maṇḍala harmyeṣu devatāyataneṣu ca itihāsa purāṇāni vedāḥ sa aṅgāḥ su lakṣaṇāḥ kāvya śāstra kathāḥ tatra śrūyante ca mahājanaiḥ saṃpūrṇa lakṣaṇa upetāḥ vistīrṇa śroṇi maṇḍalāḥ saroruha mukhāḥ śyāmāḥ śarad candra nibha ānanāḥ pīna unnata stanāḥ sarvāḥ samṛddhyā cāru darśanāḥ sauvarṇa valaya ākrāntāḥ divyaiḥ vastraiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ kadalī garbha saṃkāśāḥ padma kiñjalka saprabhāḥ bimba adhara puṭāḥ kāntāḥ karṇa anta āyata locanāḥ su mukhāḥ cāru keśāḥ ca hāva bhāva avanāmitāḥ kāścid padma palāśa akṣyaḥ kāścid indīvara īkṣaṇāḥ vidyut vispaṣṭa daśanāḥ tanu aṅgyaḥ ca tathā aparāḥ kuṭila alaka saṃyuktāḥ sīmantena virājitāḥ grīvā ābharaṇa saṃyuktāḥ mālya dāma vibhūṣitāḥ kuṇḍalaiḥ ratna saṃyuktaiḥ karṇapūraiḥ manoharaiḥ deva yoṣit pratīkāśāḥ dṛśyante śubha lakṣaṇāḥ divya gīta varaiḥ dhanyaiḥ krīḍamānāḥ vara aṅganāḥ vīṇā veṇu mṛdaṅgaiḥ ca paṇavaiḥ ca eva gomukhaiḥ śaṅkha dundubhi nirghoṣaiḥ nānā vādyaiḥ manoharaiḥ krīḍantyaḥ tāḥ sadā hṛṣṭāḥ vilāsinyaḥ parasparam evamādi tathā aneka gīta vādya viśāradāḥ divā rātrau samāyuktāḥ kāma unmattāḥ vara aṅganāḥ iti evam dadṛśe rājā kṣetram parama śobhanam atra eva ārādhayiṣyāmi bhagavantam sanātanam jagadgurum param devam param pāram param padam sarva īśvara īśvaram viṣṇum anantam aparājitam idam tat mānasam tīrtham jñātam me puruṣottamam kalpavṛkṣaḥ mahā kāyaḥ nyagrodhaḥ yatra tiṣṭhati pratimā ca indranīla ākhyā svayam devena gopitā na ca atra dṛśyate ca anyā pratimā vaiṣṇavī śubhā tathā yatnam kariṣyāmi yathā devaḥ jagatpatiḥ pratyakṣam mama ca abhyeti viṣṇuḥ satya parākramaḥ evam sa pṛthivīpālaḥ cintayitvā dvijottamāḥ ānāyya gaṇakān sarvān ācāryān śāstra pāragān bhūmim saṃśodhya yatnena rājā tu parayā mudā brāhmaṇaiḥ jñāna saṃpannaiḥ veda śāstra artha pāragaiḥ amātyaiḥ mantribhiḥ ca eva vāstu vidyā viśāradaiḥ taiḥ sārdham sa samālocya su muhūrte śubhe dine su candra tārā saṃyoge graha ānukūlya saṃyute jaya maṅgala śabdaiḥ ca nānā vādyaiḥ manoharaiḥ puṣpa lāja akṣataiḥ gandhaiḥ pūrṇa kumbhaiḥ sa dīpakaiḥ dadau arghyam tatas rājā śraddhayā su samāhitaḥ kaliṅga adhipatim śūram utkala adhipatim tathā kośala adhipatim ca eva tān uvāca tadā nṛpaḥ rājā uvāca gacchadhvam sahitāḥ sarve śilā arthe su samāhitāḥ gṛhītvā śilpi mukhyān ca śilākarma viśāradān nirūpya sarva sānūni chedayitvā śilāḥ śubhāḥ saṃvāhyantām ca śakaṭaiḥ naukābhiḥ mā vilambatha evam gantum samādiśya tān nṛpān sa mahīpatiḥ punar eva abravīt vākyam sa amātyān sa purohitān rājā uvāca gacchantu dūtāḥ sarvatra mama ājñām pravadantu vai yatra tiṣṭhanti rājānaḥ pṛthivyām tān su śīghra gāḥ hasti aśva ratha pādātaiḥ sa amātyaiḥ sa purohitaiḥ evam dūtāḥ samājñātāḥ rājñā tena mahātmanā gatvā tadā nṛpān ūcuḥ vacanam tasya bhūpateḥ śrutvā tu te tathā sarve dūtānām vacanam nṛpāḥ ājagmuḥ tvaritāḥ sarve sva sainyaiḥ parivāritāḥ ye nṛpāḥ sarva digbhāge ye ca dakṣiṇatas sthitāḥ paścimāyām sthitāḥ ye ca uttarāpatha saṃsthitāḥ pārvatīyāḥ ca ye kecid tathā dvīpa nivāsinaḥ saṃprāptāḥ bahuśas viprāḥ śrutvā indradyumna śāsanam tān āgatān nṛpān dṛṣṭvā sa amātyān sa purohitān provāca rājā hṛṣṭa ātmā kāryam uddiśya sa ādaram rājā uvāca śṛṇudhvam nṛpa śārdūlāḥ yathā kiṃcid bravīmi aham hayamedham mahā yajñam prāsādam ca eva vaiṣṇavam yadi yūyam sahāyāḥ me bhavadhvam nṛpa sattamāḥ iti evam vadamānasya rājarājasya dhīmataḥ sarve pramuditāḥ hṛṣṭāḥ bhūpāḥ te tasya śāsanāt kambala ajina ratnaiḥ ca rāṅkava āstaraṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ vajra vaidūrya māṇikyaiḥ padmarāga indranīlakaiḥ śāli vrīhi yavaiḥ ca eva māṣa mudga tilaiḥ tathā śyāmākaiḥ madhukaiḥ ca eva nīvāraiḥ sa kulatthakaiḥ anyaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ dhānyaiḥ grāmya āraṇyaiḥ sahasraśas bahu dhānya sahasrāṇām taṇḍulānām ca rāśibhiḥ gavyasya haviṣaḥ kumbhaiḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas rājānaḥ pūrayām āsuḥ yat kiṃcid dravya saṃbhavaiḥ tān dṛṣṭvā yajña saṃbhārān sarva saṃpad samanvitān yajña karma vidaḥ viprān veda vedāṅga pāragān śāstreṣu nipuṇān dakṣān kuśalān sarva karmasu ṛṣīn ca eva mahā ṛṣīn ca deva ṛṣīn ca eva tāpasān brahmacāri gṛhasthān ca vānaprasthān yatīn tathā snātakān brāhmaṇān ca anyān agnihotre sadā sthitān ācārya upādhyāya varān svādhyāya tapasā anvitān sadasyān śāstra kuśalān tathā anyān pāvakān bahūn dṛṣṭvā tān nṛpatiḥ śrīmān uvāca svam purohitam rājā uvāca tatas prayāntu vidvāṃsaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ vedapāragāḥ vājimedha artha siddhi artham deśam paśyantu yajñiyam hṛṣṭaḥ sa mantribhiḥ sārdham tadā rāja purohitaḥ brāhmaṇān agratas kṛtvā kuśalān yajña karmaṇi tam deśam dhīvara grāmam sa pratoli viṭaṅkinam kārayām āsa vipraḥ asau yajña vāṭam yathāvidhi prāsāda śata saṃbādham maṇi pravara śobhitam stambhān kanaka citrān ca toraṇāni bṛhanti ca yajña āyatana deśeṣu dattvā śuddham ca kāñcanam antaḥpurāṇi rājñām ca nānā deśa nivāsinām kārayām āsa dharma ātmā tatra tatra yathāvidhi brāhmaṇānām ca vaiśyānām nānā deśa samīyuṣām kārayām āsa vidhivat śālāḥ tatra api anekaśas priya artham tasya nṛpateḥ āyayuḥ nṛpa sattamāḥ ratnāni anekāni ādāya striyaḥ ca āyayuḥ utsave teṣām nirviśatām sveṣu śibireṣu mahātmanām teṣām abhyāgatānām ca sa rājā muni sattamāḥ vyādideśa āyatanāni śayyāḥ ca api upacārataḥ bhojanāni vicitrāṇi śāli ikṣu yava gorasaiḥ upetya nṛpati śreṣṭhaḥ vyādideśa svayam tadā samājagmuḥ sa śiṣyāḥ tān pratijagrāha pārthivaḥ sarvān ca tān anuyayau yāvat āvasathān iti tatas kṛtvā sva śilpam ca śilpinaḥ anye ca ye tadā kṛtsnam yajña vidhim rājñe tadā tasmai nyavedayan tatas śrutvā nṛpa śreṣṭhaḥ kṛtam sarvam atandritaḥ hṛṣṭa romā bhavat rājā saha mantribhiḥ acyutaḥ hetuvādān bahūn āhuḥ paraspara jigīṣavaḥ dadṛśuḥ toraṇāni atra śātakumbha mayāni ca śayyā āsana vikārān ca su bahūn ratna saṃcayān ghaṭa pātrī kaṭāhāni kalaśān vardhamānakān yūpān ca śāstra paṭhitān dāravān hema bhūṣitān upakṣiptān yathākālam vidhivat bhūri varcasaḥ sthala jāḥ jala jāḥ ye ca paśavaḥ kecana dvijāḥ sarvān eva samānītān apaśyan tatra te nṛpāḥ gāḥ ca eva mahiṣīḥ ca eva tathā vṛddha striyaḥ api ca audakāni ca sattvāni śvāpadāni vayāṃsi ca jarāyu ja aṇḍa jātāni sveda jāni udbhidāni ca parvatāni upadhānyāni bhūtāni dadṛśuḥ ca te evam pramuditam sarvam paśutaḥ dhana dhānyataḥ yajña vāṭam nṛpāḥ dṛṣṭvā vismayam paramam gatāḥ brāhmaṇānām viśām ca eva bahu miṣṭa annam ṛddhimat pūrṇe śata sahasre tu viprāṇām tatra bhuñjatām evam sa vavṛdhe yajñaḥ tasya rājñaḥ tu dhīmataḥ dadhi kulyāḥ ca dadṛśuḥ payasaḥ ca hradān tathā dvijāḥ ca tatra dṛśyante rājñaḥ tasya mahā makhe tatra yāni sahasrāṇi puruṣāṇām tatas tatas gṛhītvā bhājanam jagmuḥ bahūni dvijasattamāḥ śrāviṇaḥ ca api te sarve su mṛṣṭa maṇi kuṇḍalāḥ paryaveṣayan dvijātīn śataśas atha sahasraśas vividhāni anupānāni puruṣāḥ ye anuyāyinaḥ samāgatān veda vidaḥ rājñaḥ ca pṛthivīśvarān pūjām cakre tadā teṣām vidhivat bhūri dakṣiṇaḥ digdeśāt āgatān rājñaḥ mahā saṃgrāma śālinaḥ naṭa nartakaka ādīn ca gīta stuti viśāradān indīvara palāśa akṣyaḥ śarad candra nibha ānanāḥ kula śīla guṇa upetāḥ sahasra ekam śata adhikam ratna mālā ākulam divyam patākā dhvaja sevitam kariṇaḥ parvata ākārān mada siktān mahā balān śataśas koṭi saṃghātaiḥ dantibhiḥ danta bhūṣaṇaiḥ vāta vega javaiḥ aśvaiḥ sindhu jātaiḥ su śobhanaiḥ śveta aśvaiḥ śyāmakarṇaiḥ ca koṭi anekaiḥ java anvitaiḥ saṃnaddha baddha kakṣaiḥ ca nānā praharaṇa udyataiḥ iti evam dadṛśe rājā yajña saṃbhāra vistaram mudam lebhe tadā rājā saṃhṛṣṭaḥ vākyam abravīt rājā uvāca ānayadhvam haya śreṣṭham sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣitam cārayadhvam pṛthivyām vai rāja putrāḥ su saṃyatāḥ kṛṣṇa chāgam ca mahiṣam kṛṣṇa sāra mṛgam dvijān anaḍvāham ca gāḥ ca eva sarvān ca paśu pālakān iṣṭayaḥ ca pravartantām prāsādam vaiṣṇavam tatas striyaḥ ca ratna koṭyaḥ ca grāmāḥ ca nagarāṇi ca samyak samṛddha bhūmyaḥ ca viṣayāḥ ca evam arthinām anyāni dravya jātāni manojñāni bahūni ca sarveṣām yācamānānām na asti hi etat na bhāṣayet tāvat pravartatām yajñaḥ yāvat devaḥ purā tu iha pratyakṣam mama ca abhyeti yajñasya asya samīpatas evam uktvā tadā viprāḥ rāja siṃhaḥ mahā bhujaḥ dadau suvarṇa saṃghātam koṭīnām ca eva bhūṣaṇam kareṇu śata sāhasram vājinaḥ niyutāni ca arbudam ca eva vṛṣabham svarṇa śṛṅgīḥ ca dhenukāḥ surūpāḥ surabhīḥ ca eva kāṃsya dohāḥ payasvinīḥ vāsāṃsi ca mahārhāṇi rāṅkava āstaraṇāni ca su śuklāni ca śubhrāṇi pravāla maṇim uttamam vajra vaidūrya māṇikya muktika ādyāni yāni ca alaṃkāravatīḥ śubhrāḥ kanyāḥ rājīva locanāḥ śatāni pañca viprebhyaḥ rājā hṛṣṭaḥ pradattavān striyaḥ pīna payaḥ bhārāḥ kañcukaiḥ sva stana āvṛtāḥ madhya hīnāḥ ca su śroṇyaḥ padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇāḥ hāva bhāva anvita grīvāḥ bahvyaḥ valaya bhūṣitāḥ pāda nūpura saṃyuktāḥ paṭṭa dukūla vāsasaḥ ekaikaśas adadāt tasmin kāmyāḥ ca kāminīḥ bahūḥ bhakṣyam bhojyam ca saṃpūrṇam nānā saṃbhāra saṃyutam khaṇḍaka ādyāni anekāni svinna pakvān ca piṣṭakān annāni anyāni medhyān ca ghṛtapūrān ca khāṇḍavān madhurān tarjitān pūpān annam mṛṣṭam supākikam prīti artham sarva sattvānām dīyate annam punar punar evam dṛṣṭvā mahā yajñam deva daityāḥ sa vāraṇāḥ gandharva apsarasaḥ siddhāḥ
