ṛṣayaḥ ca prajā īśvarāḥ vismayam paramam yātāḥ dṛṣṭvā kratu varam śubham purodhāḥ mantriṇaḥ rājā hṛṣṭāḥ tatra eva sarvaśas na tatra malinaḥ kaścid na dīnaḥ na kṣudhā anvitaḥ na akāla maraṇam tatra na daṃśaḥ na grahāḥ viṣam hṛṣṭa puṣṭa janāḥ sarve tasmin rājñaḥ mahā utsave na jātam tādṛśam yajñam dhana dhānya samanvitam evam sa rājā vidhivat vājimedham dvijottamāḥ kratum samāpayām āsa prāsādam vaiṣṇavam tathā munayaḥ ūcuḥ brūhi naḥ devadeveśa yat pṛcchāmaḥ purātanam yathā tāḥ pratimāḥ pūrvam indradyumnena nirmitāḥ kena ca eva prakāreṇa tuṣṭaḥ tasmai sa mādhavaḥ tat sarvam vada ca asmākam param kautūhalam hi naḥ śṛṇudhvam muni śārdūlāḥ purāṇam veda saṃmitam kathayāmi purā vṛttam pratimānām ca saṃbhavam cintā āviṣṭaḥ tu abhūt rājā śete rātrau divā api na śaila mṛd dāru jāteṣu praśastam kim mahī tale viṣṇu pratimā yogyam ca sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣitam etaiḥ eva trayāṇām tu dayitam syāt sura arcitam pañcarātra vidhānena saṃpūjya puruṣottamam cintā āviṣṭaḥ mahīpālaḥ saṃstotum upacakrame trāhi mām sarva loka īśa janma saṃsāra sāgarāt saṃkarṣaṇa namaḥ te astu trāhi mām dharaṇīdhara ratikānta namaḥ te astu trāhi mām saṃvara antaka nārāyaṇa namaḥ te astu trāhi mām śaraṇa āgatam namaḥ te balinām śreṣṭha namaḥ te lāṅgala āyudha trāhi viṣṇo jagannātha magnam mām bhava sāgare narasiṃha mahā vīrya trāhi mām dīpta locana yathā rasātalāt urvī tvayā daṃṣṭra uddhṛtā purā tathā mahāvarāhaḥ tvam trāhi mām duḥkha sāgarāt tava etāḥ mūrtayaḥ kṛṣṇa vara dāḥ saṃstutāḥ mayā tava ime baladeva ādyāḥ pṛthak rūpeṇa saṃsthitāḥ aṅgāni tava deveśa garutman ādyāḥ tathā prabho dikpālāḥ sa āyudhāḥ ca eva keśava ādyāḥ tathā acyuta ye ca anye tava deveśa bhedāḥ proktāḥ manīṣibhiḥ mayā arcitāḥ stutāḥ sarve tathā yūyam namaskṛtāḥ bhedāḥ te kīrtitāḥ ye tu hare saṃkarṣaṇa ādayaḥ tava pūjā artha saṃbhūtāḥ tatas tvayi samāśritāḥ advaitam tvām katham dvaitam vaktum śaknoti mānavaḥ ekaḥ tvam hi hare vyāpī cit svabhāvaḥ nirañjanaḥ paramam tava yat rūpam bhāva abhāva vivarjitam nirlepam nirguṇam śreṣṭham kūṭastham acalam dhruvam tat devāḥ ca na jānanti katham jānāmi aham prabho śaṅkha cakra gadā pāṇi mukuṭa aṅgada dhāriṇam śrīvatsa uraska saṃyuktam vanamālā vibhūṣitam tat arcayanti vibudhāḥ ye ca anye tava saṃśrayāḥ trāhi mām padma pattra akṣa magnam viṣaya sāgare na anyam paśyāmi lokeśa yasya aham śaraṇam vraje tvām ṛte kamalā kānta prasīda madhusūdana jarā vyādhi śataiḥ yuktaḥ nānā duḥkhaiḥ nipīḍitaḥ harṣa śoka anvitaḥ mūḍhaḥ karma pāśaiḥ su yantritaḥ viṣama udaka duṣpāre rāga dveṣa jhaṣa ākule indriya āvarta gambhīre tṛṣṇā śoka ūrmi saṃkule nirāśraye nirālambe niḥsāre atyanta cañcale nānā jāti sahasreṣu jāyamānaḥ punar punar mayā janmāni anekāni sahasrāṇi ayutāni ca vividhāni anubhūtāni saṃsāre asmin janārdana vedāḥ sa aṅgāḥ mayā adhītāḥ śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca itihāsa purāṇāni tathā śilpāni anekaśas a saṃtoṣāḥ ca saṃtoṣāḥ saṃcaya apacayāḥ vyayāḥ mayā prāptāḥ jagannātha kṣaya vṛddhi akṣaya itarāḥ bhāryā ari mitra bandhūnām viyogāḥ saṃgamāḥ tathā pitaraḥ vividhāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ mātaraḥ ca tathā mayā duḥkhāni ca anubhūtāni yāni saukhyāni anekaśas prāptāḥ ca bāndhavāḥ putrāḥ bhrātaraḥ jñātayaḥ tathā ma yoṣitam tathā strīṇām koṣṭhe viṣ mūtra picchale vārdhake ca hṛṣīkeśa tāni prāptāni vai mayā maraṇe yāni duḥkhāni yama mārge yama ālaye mayā tāni anubhūtāni narake yātanāḥ tathā kṛmi kīṭa drumāṇām ca hasti aśva mṛga pakṣiṇām mahiṣa uṣṭra gavām ca eva tathā anyeṣām vanaukasām dvijātīnām ca sarveṣām śūdrāṇām ca eva yoniṣu dhaninām kṣatriyāṇām ca daridrāṇām tapasvinām nṛpāṇām nṛpa bhṛtyānām tathā anyeṣām ca dehinām gṛheṣu teṣām utpannaḥ deva ca aham punar punar gataḥ asmi dāsa tām nātha bhṛtyānām bahuśas nṛṇām daridra tvam ca īśvara tvam svāmi tvam ca tathā gataḥ hataḥ mayā hatāḥ ca anye ghātitaḥ ghātitāḥ tathā pitṛ mātṛ suhṛd bhrātṛ kalatrāṇām kṛtena ca dhaninām śrotriyāṇām ca daridrāṇām tapasvinām uktam dainyam ca vividham tyaktvā lajjām janārdana deva tiryak manuṣyeṣu sthāvareṣu careṣu ca tathā ca aham suraśreṣṭha karma rajju samāvṛtaḥ bhramāmi su ciram kālam na antam paśyāmi karhicit śoka tṛṣṇā abhibhūtaḥ aham kāṃdiśīkaḥ vicetanaḥ idānīm tvām aham deva vihvalaḥ śaraṇam gataḥ trāhi mām duḥkhitam kṛṣṇa magnam saṃsāra sāgare kṛpām kuru jagannātha bhaktam mām yadi manyase ye tu tvām vidhivat deva na arcayanti nara adhamāḥ sugatiḥ tu katham teṣām bhavet saṃsāra bandhanāt kim teṣām kula śīlena vidyayā jīvitena ca yeṣām na jāyate bhaktiḥ jagaddhātari keśave prakṛtim tu āsurīm prāpya ye tvām nindanti mohitāḥ patanti narake ghore jāyamānāḥ punar punar na teṣām niṣkṛtiḥ tasmāt vidyate naraka arṇavāt ye dūṣayanti durvṛttāḥ tvām deva puruṣa adhamāḥ ārādhya tvām surāḥ daityāḥ narāḥ ca anye api saṃyatāḥ avāpuḥ paramām siddhim kaḥ tvām deva na pūjayet na śaknuvanti brahma ādyāḥ stotum tvām tridaśāḥ hare katham mānuṣa buddhyā aham staumi tvām prakṛteḥ param tathā ca ajñāna bhāvena saṃstutaḥ asi mayā prabho kṛta aparādhe api hare kṣamām kurvanti sādhavaḥ tasmāt prasīda deveśa bhakta sneham samāśritaḥ yaḥ saṃpūjya jagannātham pratyaham stauti mānavaḥ trisaṃdhyam yaḥ japet vidvān idam stotra varam śuciḥ dharmam ca artham ca kāmam ca mokṣam ca labhate naraḥ yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api śrāvayet vā samāhitaḥ sa lokam śāśvatam viṣṇoḥ yāti nirdhūta kalmaṣaḥ na nāstikāya mūrkhāya na kṛtaghnāya mānine na duṣṭa mataye dadyāt na abhaktāya kadācana dātavyam bhakti yuktāya guṇa śīla anvitāya ca viṣṇu bhaktāya śāntāya śraddhā anuṣṭhāna śāline idam samasta agha vināśa hetuḥ kāruṇya saṃjñam sukha mokṣa dam ca aśeṣa vāñchā phala dam variṣṭham ye tam su sūkṣmam vimalāḥ murārim dhyāyanti nityam puruṣam purāṇam te mukti bhājaḥ praviśanti viṣṇum paraḥ pareṣām na tatas asti ca anyat draṣṭā sa pātā sa tu nāśa kartā kim vidyayā kim sva guṇaiḥ ca teṣām yajñaiḥ ca dānaiḥ ca tapobhiḥ ugraiḥ yeṣām na bhaktiḥ bhavati iha kṛṣṇe makhaiḥ tapobhiḥ sa guṇaiḥ variṣṭhaḥ jñātā sa dātā sa tu satya vaktā stutvā evam muni śārdūlāḥ praṇamya ca sanātanam cintā āviṣṭaḥ mahīpālaḥ kuśān āstīrya bhū tale vastram ca tad manāḥ bhūtvā suṣvāpa dharaṇī tale ātmānam darśayām āsa śaṅkha cakra gadā bhṛtam śaṅkha cakra dharam devam gadā cakra ugra pāṇinam śārṅga bāṇa dharam devam jvalat tejoti maṇḍalam yuga anta āditya varṇa ābham nīla vaidūrya saṃnibham suparṇa aṃse tam āsīnam ṣoḍaśa ardha bhujam śubham sa ca asmai prābravīt dhīrāḥ sādhu rājan mahāmate tuṣṭaḥ asmi te mahīpāla vṛthā kim anuśocasi yat atra pratimā rājan jagat pūjyā sanātanī yathā sā prāpyate bhūpa tat upāyam bravīmi te gatāyām adya śarvaryām nirmale bhāskara udite sāgarasya jalasya ante nānā druma vibhūṣite jalam tathā eva velāyām dṛśyate tatra vai mahat kūla ante hi mahā vṛkṣaḥ sthitaḥ sthala jaleṣu ca ekākī viharan rājan sa tvam paśyasi pādapam īdṛś cihnam samālokya chedaya tvam aśaṅkitaḥ chedyamānam tu tam vṛkṣam prātar adbhuta darśanam dṛṣṭvā tena eva saṃcintya tatas bhūpāla darśanāt kuru tām pratimām divyām jahi cintām vimohinīm evam uktvā mahābhāgaḥ jagāma adarśanam hariḥ tām niśām sa samudvīkṣya sthitaḥ tad gata mānasaḥ vyāharan vaiṣṇavān mantrān sūktam ca eva tad ātmakam pragatāyām rajanyām tu utthitaḥ na anya mānasaḥ sa snātvā sāgare samyak yathāvat vidhinā tatas dattvā dānam ca viprebhyaḥ grāmān ca nagarāṇi ca kṛtvā paurvāhṇikam karma jagāma sa nṛpa uttamaḥ na ca aśvaḥ na padātiḥ ca na gajaḥ na ca sārathiḥ ekākī sa mahā velām praviveśa mahīpatiḥ tam dadarśa mahā vṛkṣam tejasvantam mahā drumam mahā utsedham mahā kāyam prasuptam ca jala antike sāndra māñjiṣṭha varṇa ābham nāma jāti vivarjitam naranāthaḥ tadā viprāḥ drumam dṛṣṭvā mudā anvitaḥ paraśunā śātayām āsa niśitena dṛḍhena ca nirīkṣyamāṇe kāṣṭhe tu babhūva adbhuta darśanam viśvakarmā ca viṣṇuḥ ca vipra rūpa dharau ubhau tau ūcatuḥ mahā rāja kim atra tvam kariṣyasi kimartham ca mahā bāho śātitaḥ ca vanaspatiḥ mahā sindhu taṭe ca eva katham vai śātitaḥ drumaḥ tayoḥ śrutvā vacaḥ viprāḥ sa tu rājā mudā anvitaḥ babhāṣe vacanam tābhyām mṛdulam madhuram tathā dṛṣṭvā tau brāhmaṇau tatra candra sūryau iva āgatau rājā uvāca ārādhayitum pratimām karomi iti matiḥ mama svapna ante ca samuddiṣṭaḥ bhavadbhyām śrāvitam mayā viṣṇuḥ uvāca nānā vyādhi śata āvarte jala budbuda saṃnibhe yatas te matiḥ utpannā viṣṇoḥ ārādhanāya vai dhanyaḥ tvam nṛpa śārdūla guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ alaṃkṛtaḥ sa prajā pṛthivī dhanyā sa śaila vana kānanā sa pura grāma nagarā catur varṇaiḥ alaṃkṛtā yatra tvam nṛpa śārdūla prajāḥ pālayitā prabhuḥ āvābhyām saha tiṣṭha tvam kathābhiḥ dharma saṃśritaḥ ayam mama sahāyaḥ tu āgataḥ śilpinām varaḥ viśvakarma samaḥ sākṣāt nipuṇaḥ sarva karmasu mayā uddiṣṭām tu pratimām karoti eṣa taṭam tyaja śrutvā evam vacanam tasya tadā rājā dvijanmanaḥ sāgarasya taṭam tyaktvā gatvā tasya samīpatas tasthau sa nṛpati śreṣṭhaḥ vṛkṣa chāye suśītale tatas tasmai sa viśvātmā dadau ājñām dvija ākṛtiḥ śilpi mukhyāya vipra indrāḥ kuruṣva pratimāḥ iti kṛṣṇa rūpam param śāntam padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇam gaura aṅgam kṣīra varṇa ābham dvitīyam svastika aṅkitam lāṅgala astra dharam devam ananta ākhyam mahā balam na vijñātaḥ hi tasya antaḥ tena anantaḥ iti smṛtaḥ bhaginīm vāsudevasya rukma varṇām su śobhanām tṛtīyām vai subhadrām ca sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣitām tad kṣaṇāt kārayām āsa pratimāḥ śubha lakṣaṇāḥ prathamam śukla varṇa ābham śārada indu sama prabham ārakta akṣam mahā kāyam sphaṭa a vikaṭa mastakam kuṇḍala eka dharam divyam gadā muśala dhāriṇam dvitīyam puṇḍarīkākṣam nīla jīmūta saṃnibham atasī puṣpa saṃkāśam padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇam pīta vāsasam ati ugram śubham śrīvatsa lakṣaṇam cakra pūrṇa karam divyam sarva pāpa haram harim tṛtīyām svarṇa varṇa ābhām padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇām vicitra vastra saṃchannām hāra keyūra bhūṣitām vicitra ābharaṇa upetām ratna hāra avalambitām pīna unnata kucām ramyām viśvakarmā vinirmame sa tu rāja adbhutam dṛṣṭvā kṣaṇena ekena nirmitāḥ divya vastra yuga channāḥ nānā ratnaiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpannāḥ pratimāḥ su manoharāḥ ubhau ca adbhuta karmāṇau deva vṛttau amānuṣau devau vā mānuṣau vā api yakṣa vidyādharau yuvām kim nu brahma hṛṣīkeśau kim vasū kim uta aśvinau yuvām gataḥ asmi śaraṇam ātmā tu me prakāśyatām śrī bhagavān uvāca na aham devaḥ na yakṣaḥ vā na daityaḥ na ca devarāj ārādhanīyaḥ bhūtānām antaḥ yasya na vidyate paṭhyate sarva śāstreṣu vedānteṣu nigadyate aham eva svayam brahmā aham viṣṇuḥ śivaḥ api aham pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni tretāgniḥ hutabhuj nṛpa varuṇaḥ apām patiḥ ca aham dharitrī ca mahīdharaḥ carācaram ca yat viśvam mad anyat na asti kiṃcana prītaḥ aham te nṛpa śreṣṭha varam varaya suvrata mad darśanam apuṇyānām svapna ante api na jāyate tvam punar dṛḍha bhakti tvāt pratyakṣam dṛṣṭavān asi romāñcita tanuḥ bhūtvā idam stotram jagau nṛpaḥ rājā uvāca śriyaḥ kānta namaḥ te astu śrīpate pīta vāsase śrīda śrīśa śrīnivāsa namaḥ te śrīniketana ādyam puruṣam īśānam sarva īśam sarvatomukham niṣkalam paramam devam praṇataḥ asmi sanātanam śabda atītam guṇa atītam bhāva abhāva vivarjitam nirlepam nirguṇam sūkṣmam sarvajñam sarva bhāvanam prāvṛṣ megha pratīkāśam go brāhmaṇa hite ratam sarveṣām eva goptāram vyāpinam sarva bhāvinam śaṅkha cakra dharam devam gadā muśala dhāriṇam nāga paryaṅka śayanam kṣīroda arṇava śāyinam namasye aham hṛṣīkeśam sarva pāpa haram harim sarva loka īśvaram viṣṇum mokṣa kāraṇam avyayam evam stutvā tu tam devam praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ uvāca praṇataḥ bhūtvā nipatya dharaṇī tale rājā uvāca deva asurāḥ sa gandharvāḥ yakṣa rakṣaḥ mahā uragāḥ siddha vidyādharāḥ sādhyāḥ kiṃnarāḥ guhyakāḥ tathā ṛṣayaḥ ye mahābhāgāḥ nānā śāstra viśāradāḥ parivrāj yoga yuktāḥ ca veda tattva artha cintakāḥ nirguṇam nirmalam śāntam yat paśyanti manīṣinaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca bhaviṣyati yathākāmam mad prasādāt na saṃśayaḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi tathā nava śatāni ca avicchinnam mahā rājyam kuru tvam nṛpa sattama parāt parataram sūkṣmam nirlepam niṣkalam dhruvam cintā śoka vinirmuktam kriyā kāraṇa varjitam tat aham darśayiṣyāmi jñeya ākhyam paramam padam yam prāpya parama ānandam prāpsyasi paramām gatim yāvat samudrāḥ sapta eva yāvat meru ādi parvatāḥ tiṣṭhanti divi devāḥ ca tāvat sarvatra ca avyayā indradyumnasaraḥ nāma tīrtham yajña aṅga saṃbhavam yatra snātvā sakṛt lokaḥ śakra lokam avāpnuyāt dāpayiṣyati yaḥ piṇḍān taṭe asmin sarasaḥ śubhe kula ekaviṃśam uddhṛtya śakra lokam gamiṣyati sarasaḥ dakṣiṇe bhāge nairṛtyām tu samāśrite ketakī vana saṃchannaḥ nānā pādapa saṃkulaḥ aśokaiḥ karṇikāraiḥ ca puṃnāgaiḥ nāgakesaraiḥ pāṭalā āmrāta saralaiḥ candanaiḥ devadārubhiḥ nyagrodha aśvattha khadiraiḥ pārijātaiḥ saha arjunaiḥ hintālaiḥ ca eva tālaiḥ ca śiṃśapaiḥ badaraiḥ tathā anyaiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ śobhitaḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ āṣāḍhasya site pakṣe pañcamyām pitṛ daivate ṛkṣe neṣyanti naḥ tatra nītvā sapta dināni vai maṇḍape sthāpayiṣyanti su veśyābhiḥ su śobhanaiḥ krīḍā viśeṣa bahulaiḥ nṛtya gīta manoharaiḥ cāmaraiḥ svarṇa daṇḍaiḥ ca vyajanaiḥ ratna bhūṣaṇaiḥ vījayantaḥ tathā asmabhyam sthāpayiṣyanti maṅgalāḥ brahmacārī yatiḥ ca eva snātakāḥ ca dvijottamāḥ vānaprasthāḥ gṛhasthāḥ ca siddhāḥ ca anye ca brāhmaṇāḥ nānā varṇa padaiḥ stotraiḥ ṛk yajuḥ sāma nisvanaiḥ kariṣyanti stutim rājan rāma keśavayoḥ punar tatas stutvā ca dṛṣṭvā ca saṃpraṇamya ca bhaktitaḥ naraḥ varṣa ayutam divyam śrīmat haripure vaset vimānena arka varṇena ratna hāreṇa bhrājatā tapaḥ kṣayāt iha āgatya manuṣyaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ bhavet koṭīdhanapatiḥ śrīmān caturvedī bhavet dhruvam evam tasmai varam dattvā kṛtvā ca samayam hariḥ jagāma adarśanam viprāḥ sahitaḥ viśvakarmaṇā sa tu rājā tadā hṛṣṭaḥ romāñcita tanūruhaḥ kṛtakṛtyam iva ātmānam mene saṃdarśanāt dhareḥ tatas kṛṣṇam ca rāmam ca subhadrām ca vara pradām rathaiḥ vimāna saṃkāśaiḥ maṇi kāñcana citritaiḥ saṃvāhya tāḥ tadā rājā mahā maṅgala niḥsvanaiḥ ānayām āsa matimān sa amātyaḥ sa purohitaḥ nānā vāditra nirghoṣaiḥ nānā veda svanaiḥ śubhaiḥ tatas śubha tithau kāle nakṣatre śubha lakṣaṇe pratiṣṭhām kārayām āsa su muhūrte dvijaiḥ saha yathā uktena vidhānena vidhi dṛṣṭena karmaṇā ācārya anumatena eva sarvam kṛtvā mahīpatiḥ ācāryāya tadā dattvā dakṣiṇām vidhivat prabhuḥ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhām vidhivat prāsāde bhavana uttame sthāpayām āsa tān sarvān vidhi dṛṣṭena karmaṇā tatas saṃpūjya vidhinā nānā puṣpaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ suvarṇa maṇi muktā ādyaiḥ nānā vastraiḥ su śobhanaiḥ dadau ca anyān sa viṣayān purāṇi nagarāṇi ca evam bahuvidham dattvā rājyam kṛtvā yathocitam iṣṭvā ca vividhaiḥ yajñaiḥ dattvā dānāni anekaśas jagāma paramam sthānam tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam evam mayā muni śreṣṭhāḥ kathitaḥ vaḥ nṛpa uttamaḥ viṣṇuḥ uvāca āścaryam menire viprāḥ papracchuḥ ca punar mudā munayaḥ ūcuḥ devatā prekṣaṇe ca eva brūhi sarvam pṛthak pṛthak dṛṣṭvā sadā jyeṣṭha śukla dvādaśyām puruṣottamam tasmāt jyeṣṭhe muni śreṣṭhāḥ prayatnena su saṃyataiḥ pañcatīrtham tu vidhivat kṛtvā jyeṣṭhe narottamaḥ śukla pakṣasya dvādaśyām paśyet tam puruṣottamam ye paśyanti avyayam devam dvādaśyām puruṣottamam kṛtvā tasmin pañcatīrtham draṣṭavyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ahani ahani śuddha ātmā saḥ api viṣṇu puram vrajet yātrām karoti kṛṣṇasya śraddhayā yaḥ samāhitaḥ cakram dṛṣṭvā hareḥ dūrāt prāsāda upari saṃsthitam āsīt kalpe muni śreṣṭhāḥ saṃpravṛtte mahā kṣaye naṣṭe arka candre pavane naṣṭe sthāvara jaṅgame tatas saṃvartakaḥ vahniḥ vāyunā saha bho dvijāḥ paścāt sa pṛthivīm bhittvā praviśya ca rasātalam deva dānava yakṣāṇām bhayam janayate mahat adhastāt muni śārdūlāḥ sarvam nāśayate kṣaṇāt tatas yojana viṃśānām sahasrāṇi śatāni ca nirdahati āśu gaḥ vāyuḥ sa ca saṃvartakaḥ analaḥ pradīptaḥ asau mahā raudraḥ kalpa agniḥ iti saṃśrutaḥ mahā jvālaḥ mahā arciṣmān saṃpradīpta mahā svanaḥ sūrya koṭi pratīkāśaḥ jvalan iva sa tejasā trailokyam ca adahat tūrṇam sa sura asura mānuṣam ṛṣiḥ parama dharma ātmā dhyāna yoga paraḥ abhavat ekaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate viprāḥ mārkaṇḍeya iti viśrutaḥ moha pāśaiḥ nibaddhaḥ asau kṣudh tṛṣṇā ākulita indriyāḥ sa dṛṣṭvā tam mahā vahnim śuṣka kaṇṭha oṣṭha tālukaḥ tṛṣṇā ārtaḥ praskhalan viprāḥ tadā asau bhaya vihvalaḥ babhrāma pṛthivīm sarvām kāṃdiśīkaḥ vicetanaḥ trātāram na adhigacchan vai itas ca itas ca dhāvati na lebhe ca tadā śarma yatra viśrāmyatā dvijāḥ karomi kim na jānāmi yasya aham śaraṇam vraje katham paśyāmi tam devam puruṣa īśam sanātanam prāptavān tat padam divyam mahāpralaya kāraṇam puruṣeśam iti khyātam vaṭa rājam sanātanam āsādya tam muni śreṣṭhāḥ tasya mūle samāviśat na kālāgni bhayam tatra na ca aṅgāra pravarṣaṇam tatas gaja kula prakhyāḥ taḍit mālā vibhūṣitāḥ kecid nīlotpala śyāmāḥ kecid kumuda saṃnibhāḥ kecid kiñjalka saṃkāśāḥ kecid pītāḥ payodharāḥ kecid dharita saṃkāśāḥ kākāṇḍa saṃnibhāḥ tathā kecid kamala pattra ābhāḥ kecid hiṅgula saṃnibhāḥ kecid puravara ākārāḥ kecid giri vara upamāḥ kecid añjana saṃkāśāḥ kecid marakata prabhāḥ vidyut mālā pinaddha aṅgāḥ samuttasthuḥ mahā ghanāḥ ghora rūpāḥ mahābhāgāḥ ghora svana nināditāḥ taiḥ iyam pṛthivī sarvā sa parvata vana ākarā āpūritāḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ salila ogha pariplutāḥ tatas te jaladāḥ ghorāḥ vāriṇā muni sattamāḥ sarvatas plāvayām āsuḥ coditāḥ parameṣṭhinā varṣamāṇāḥ mahā toyam pūrayantaḥ vasuṃdharām su ghoram aśivam raudram nāśayanti sma pāvakam tatas dvādaśa varṣāṇi payodāḥ samupaplave dhārābhiḥ pūrayantaḥ vai codyamānāḥ mahātmanā tatas samudrāḥ svām velām atikrāmanti bho dvijāḥ parvatāḥ ca vyaśīryanta mahī ca apsu nimajjati saṃveṣṭayitvā naśyanti vāyu vega samāhatāḥ tatas tam mārutam ghoram sa viṣṇuḥ muni sattamāḥ ādipadma ālayaḥ devaḥ pītvā svapiti bho dvijāḥ tasmin ekārṇave ghore naṣṭe sthāvara jaṅgame naṣṭe deva asura nare yakṣa rākṣasa varjite tatas muniḥ sa viśrāntaḥ dhyātvā ca puruṣottamam dadarśa cakṣuḥ unmīlya jala pūrṇām vasuṃdharām na apaśyat tam vaṭam na urvīm na diś ādi na bhāskaram babhrāma asau muniḥ ca ārtaḥ itas ca itas ca saṃplavan nimamajja tadā viprāḥ trātāram na adhigacchati evam tam vihvalam dṛṣṭvā kṛpayā puruṣottamaḥ provāca muni śārdūlāḥ tadā dhyānena toṣitaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca āgaccha āgaccha śīghram tvam mārkaṇḍeya mama antikam mārkaṇḍeya mune dhīra bālaḥ tvam śrama pīḍitaḥ uvāca sa tadā viprāḥ vismitaḥ ca abhavat muhur mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca na hi eṣa samudācāraḥ deveṣu api samāhitaḥ mām brahmā sa ca deveśaḥ dīrgha āyuḥ iti bhāṣate evam uktvā tadā viprāḥ cintā āviṣṭaḥ abhavat muniḥ kim svapnaḥ ayam mayā dṛṣṭaḥ kim vā mohaḥ ayam āgataḥ vrajāmi śaraṇam devam bhaktyā aham puruṣottamam sa gatvā śaraṇam devam muniḥ tad gata mānasaḥ dadarśa tam vaṭam bhūyas viśālam salila upari śākhāyām tasya sauvarṇam vistīrṇāyām mahā adbhutam ruciram divya paryaṅkam racitam viśvakarmaṇā padmarāga ādibhiḥ juṣṭam ratnaiḥ anyaiḥ alaṃkṛtam nānā āstaraṇa saṃvītam nānā ratna upaśobhitam nānā āścarya samāyuktam prabhā maṇḍala maṇḍitam tasya upari sthitam devam kṛṣṇam bāla vapuḥ dharam sūrya koṭi pratīkāśam dīpyamānam su varcasam catur bhujam sundara aṅgam padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇam śrīvatsa vakṣasam devam śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam vanamālā vṛta uraskam divya kuṇḍala dhāriṇam hāra bhāra arpita grīvam divya ratna vibhūṣitam dṛṣṭvā tadā muniḥ devam vismaya utphulla locanaḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyam ca jānan api mahā muniḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca vṛthā me tapasaḥ vīryam vṛthā jñānam vṛthā kriyā vṛthā me jīvitam dīrgham vṛthā mānuṣyam eva ca yaḥ aham suptam na jānāmi paryaṅke divya bālakam trāṇa artham vihvalaḥ ca asau nirvedam gatavān tadā tatas bāla arka saṃkāśam sva mahimnā vyavasthitam sarva tejaḥ mayam viprāḥ na śaśāka abhivīkṣitum dṛṣṭvā tam munim āyāntam sa bālaḥ prahasan iva provāca muni śārdūlāḥ tadā megha ogha nisvanaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca vatsa jānāmi śrāntam tvām trāṇa artham mām upasthitam śarīram viśa me kṣipram viśrāmaḥ te mayā uditaḥ śrutvā sa vacanam tasya kiṃcid na uvāca mohitaḥ viveśa vadanam tasya vivṛtam ca avaśaḥ muniḥ dadarśa pṛthivīm kṛtsnām nānā janapadaiḥ vṛtām dadarśa tān samudrān ca jambu plakṣam ca śālmalam kuśam krauñcam ca śākam ca puṣkaram ca dadarśa saḥ bhārata ādīni varṣāṇi tathā sarvān ca parvatān merum ca sarva ratna āḍhyam apaśyat kanakācalam nānā ratna anvitaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ bhūṣitam bahu kandaram nānā muni jana ākīrṇam nānā vṛkṣa vana ākulam nānā sattva samāyuktam nānā āścarya samanvitam vyāghraiḥ siṃhaiḥ varāhaiḥ ca cāmaraiḥ mahiṣaiḥ gajaiḥ mṛgaiḥ śākhāmṛgaiḥ ca anyaiḥ bhūṣitam su manoharam muni yakṣa apsarobhiḥ ca vṛtaiḥ ca anyaiḥ surālayaiḥ evam sumerum śrīmantam apaśyat muni sattamaḥ himavantam hemakūṭam niṣadham gandhamādanam śvetam ca durdharam nīlam kailāsam mandaram girim mahendram malayam vindhyam pāriyātram tathā arbudam etāḥ ca anyāḥ ca bahavaḥ yāvantaḥ pṛthivīdharāḥ tatas tān tu muni śreṣṭhāḥ saḥ apaśyat ratna bhūṣitān kurukṣetram ca pāñcālān matsyān madrān sa kekayān vāhlīkān śūrasenān ca kāśmīrān taṅgaṇān khasān pārvatīyān kirātān ca karṇaprāvaraṇān marūn antyajān antya jātīn ca saḥ apaśyat tasya ca udare mṛgān śākhāmṛgān siṃhān varāhān sṛmarān śaśān gajān ca anyān tathā sattvān saḥ apaśyat tasya ca udare pṛthivyām yāni tīrthāni grāmāḥ ca nagarāṇi ca kṛṣi gorakṣa vāṇijyam kraya vikrayaṇam tathā śakra ādīn vibudhān śreṣṭhān tathā anyān ca divaukasaḥ gandharva apsarasaḥ yakṣān ṛṣīn ca eva sanātanān daitya dānava saṃghān ca nāgān ca muni sattamāḥ siṃhikā tanayān ca eva ye ca anye sura śatravaḥ yat kiṃcid tena loke asmin dṛṣṭa pūrvam carācaram athavā kim bahu uktena kīrtitena punar punar pātālam sutalam ca eva vitalam ca rasātalam mahā talam ca brahmāṇḍam apaśyat tasya ca udare avyāhatā gatiḥ tasya tadā abhūt dvijasattamāḥ bhramamāṇaḥ tadā kukṣau kṛtsnam jagat idam dvijāḥ na antam jagāma dehasya tasya viṣṇoḥ kadācana yadā asau na āgataḥ ca antam tasya dehasya bho dvijāḥ tadā tam vara dam devam śaraṇam gatavān muniḥ tatas asau sahasā viprāḥ vāyu vegena niḥsṛtaḥ mahātmanaḥ mukhāt tasya vivṛtāt puruṣasya saḥ punar ca eka arṇavām urvīm apaśyat jana varjitām pūrva dṛṣṭam ca tam devam dadarśa śiśu rūpiṇam śākhāyām vaṭa vṛkṣasya paryaṅka upari saṃsthitam śrīvatsa vakṣasam devam pīta vastram catur bhujam jagat ādāya tiṣṭhantam padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇam dṛṣṭvā mukhāt viniṣkrāntam provāca prahasan iva śrī bhagavān uvāca bhramamāṇaḥ ca kim tatra āścaryam dṛṣṭavān asi bhaktaḥ asi me muni śreṣṭha śrāntaḥ asi ca mama āśritaḥ tena tvām upakārāya saṃbhāṣe paśya mām iha śrutvā sa vacanam tasya saṃprahṛṣṭa tanūruhaḥ dadarśa tam su duṣprekṣam ratnaiḥ divyaiḥ alaṃkṛtam prasannā nirmalā dṛṣṭiḥ muhūrtāt tasya bho dvijāḥ prasādāt tasya devasya prādurbhūtā punar navā praṇamya śirasā viprāḥ harṣa gadgadayā girā kṛtāñjaliḥ tadā hṛṣṭaḥ vismitaḥ ca punar punar dṛṣṭvā tam paramātmānam saṃstotum upacakrame mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca trāhi mām cāru padma akṣa duḥkhitam śaraṇa āgatam saṃtaptaḥ asmi suraśreṣṭha saṃvarta ākhyena vahninā aṅgāra varṣa bhītam ca trāhi mām puruṣottama śoṣitaḥ ca pracaṇḍena vāyunā jagadāyunā vihvalaḥ aham tathā śrāntaḥ trāhi mām puruṣottama tāpitaḥ ca taśa amātyaiḥ pralaya āvartaka ādibhiḥ na śāntim adhigacchāmi trāhi mām puruṣottama tṛṣitaḥ ca kṣudhā āviṣṭaḥ duḥkhitaḥ ca jagatpate trātāram na atra paśyāmi trāhi mām puruṣottama na ca antam adhigacchāmi trāhi mām puruṣottama tava udare ca deveśa mayā dṛṣṭam carācaram vismitaḥ aham viṣaṇṇaḥ ca trāhi mām puruṣottama prasīda vibudhām nātha prasīda vibudha ālaya prasīda sarva loka īśa jagat kāraṇa kāraṇa prasīda kamalā kānta prasīda tridaśeśvara prasīda kaṃsa keśī ghna prasīda ariṣṭa nāśana prasīda kṛṣṇa daitya ghna prasīda danuja antaka tvam mahī tvam jalam deva tvam agniḥ tvam samīraṇaḥ puruṣaḥ tvam jagat vyāpī puruṣāt api ca uttamaḥ tvam indriyāṇi sarvāṇi śabda ādyāḥ viṣayāḥ prabho tvam dikpālāḥ ca dharmāḥ ca vedāḥ yajñāḥ sa dakṣiṇāḥ tvam indraḥ tvam śivaḥ devaḥ tvam haviḥ tvam hutāśanaḥ tvam yamaḥ pitṛ rāj deva tvam rakṣaḥ adhipatiḥ svayam varuṇaḥ tvam apām nātha tvam vāyuḥ tvam dhana īśvaraḥ tvam īśānaḥ tvam anantaḥ tvam gaṇeśaḥ ca ṣaṇmukhaḥ vasavaḥ tvam tathā rudrāḥ tvam ādityāḥ ca khecarāḥ dānavāḥ tvam tathā yakṣāḥ tvam daityāḥ sa marut gaṇāḥ siddhāḥ ca apsarasaḥ nāgāḥ gandharvāḥ tvam sa cāraṇāḥ pitaraḥ vālakhilyāḥ ca prajānām patayaḥ acyuta munayaḥ tvam ṛṣi gaṇāḥ tvam aśvinau niśācarāḥ anyāḥ ca jātayaḥ tvam hi yat kiṃcid jīva saṃjñitam bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyam ca tvam jagat sacarācaram avyaktaḥ śāśvataḥ anantaḥ sarvavyāpī maheśvaraḥ tvam ākāśaḥ paraḥ śāntaḥ ajaḥ tvam vibhuḥ avyayaḥ evam tvām nirguṇam stotum kaḥ śaknoti nirañjanam ittham stutaḥ tadā tena mārkaṇḍeyena bho dvijāḥ prītaḥ provāca bhagavān megha gambhīrayā girā śrī bhagavān uvāca brūhi kāmam muni śreṣṭha yat te manasi vartate śrutvā sa vacanam viprāḥ śiśoḥ tasya mahātmanaḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca jñātum icchāmi deva tvām māyām vai tava ca uttamām icchāmi puṇḍarīkākṣa jñātum tvām aham avyayam iha bhūtvā śiśuḥ sākṣāt kim bhavān avatiṣṭhate jñātum icchāmi deveśa brūhi sarvam aśeṣatas mahat etat acintyam ca yat aham dṛṣṭavān prabho sāntvayan sa tadā vākyam uvāca vadatām varaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca kāmam devāḥ ca mām vipra nahi jānanti tattvataḥ tava prītyā pravakṣyāmi yathā idam visṛjāmi aham pitṛ bhaktaḥ asi viprarṣe mām eva śaraṇam gataḥ tatas dṛṣṭaḥ asmi te sākṣāt brahmacaryam ca te mahat āpaḥ nārāḥ iti purā saṃjñā karma kṛtam mayā tena nārāyaṇaḥ asmi uktaḥ mama tāḥ tu ayanam sadā aham nārāyaṇaḥ nāma prabhavaḥ śāśvataḥ avyayaḥ vidhātā sarva bhūtānām saṃhartā ca dvijottama aham viṣṇuḥ aham brahmā śakraḥ ca api sura adhipaḥ aham vaiśravaṇaḥ rājā yamaḥ preta adhipaḥ tathā aham śivaḥ ca somaḥ ca kaśyapaḥ ca prajāpatiḥ aham dhātā vidhātā ca yajñaḥ ca aham dvijottama dyauḥ mūrdhā kham diśaḥ śrotre tathā apaḥ sveda saṃbhavāḥ sadiśam ca nabhaḥ kāyaḥ vāyuḥ manasi me sthitaḥ mayā kratu śataiḥ iṣṭam bahubhiḥ ca āpta dakṣiṇaiḥ pṛthivyām kṣatriya indrāḥ ca pārthivāḥ svarga kāṅkṣiṇaḥ yajante mām tathā vaiśyāḥ svarga loka jigīṣavaḥ catur samudra paryantām meru mandara bhūṣaṇām śeṣaḥ bhūtvā aham ekaḥ hi dhārayāmi vasuṃdharām vārāham rūpam āsthāya mama iyam jagatī purā majjamānā jale vipra vīryeṇa asmi samuddhṛtā agniḥ ca vāḍavaḥ vipra bhūtvā aham dvijasattama pibāmi apaḥ samāviṣṭaḥ tāḥ ca eva visṛjāmi aham brahma vaktram bhujau kṣatram ūrū me saṃśritāḥ viśaḥ pādau śūdrāḥ bhavanti ime vikrameṇa krameṇa ca ṛgvedaḥ sāmavedaḥ ca yajurvedaḥ tu atharvaṇaḥ yatayaḥ śānti paramāḥ yata ātmānaḥ bubhutsavaḥ kāma krodha dveṣa muktāḥ niḥsaṅgāḥ vīta kalmaṣāḥ sattva sthāḥ nirahaṃkārāḥ nityam adhyātma kovidāḥ aham saṃvartakaḥ sūryaḥ tu aham saṃvartakaḥ anilaḥ tārā rūpāṇi dṛśyante yāni etāni nabhastale ratna ākarāḥ samudrāḥ ca sarve eva caturdiśaḥ mama eva viddhi rūpāṇi sarvāṇi etāni sattama satyam dānam tapaḥ ca ugram ahiṃsām sarva jantuṣu mayā abhibhūta vijñānāḥ ceṣṭayanti na kāmatas śānta ātmānaḥ jita krodhāḥ prāpnuvanti dvijātayaḥ prāptum śakyaḥ na ca eva aham naraiḥ duṣkṛta karmabhiḥ lobha abhibhūtaiḥ kṛpaṇaiḥ anāryaiḥ akṛtātmabhiḥ tat mām mahā phalam viddhi narāṇām bhāvitātmanām su duṣprāpam vimūḍhānām mām ku yoga niṣeviṇām daityāḥ hiṃsā anuraktāḥ ca avadhyāḥ sura sattamaiḥ rākṣasāḥ ca api loke asmin yadā utpatsyanti dāruṇāḥ tadā aham saṃprasūyāmi gṛheṣu puṇya karmaṇām praviṣṭaḥ mānuṣam deham sarvam praśamayāmi aham sṛṣṭvā deva manuṣyān ca gandharva uraga rākṣasān sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni saṃharāmi ātma māyayā āviśya mānuṣam deham maryādā bandha kāraṇāt śvetaḥ kṛta yuge dharmaḥ śyāmaḥ tretā yuge mama raktaḥ dvāparam āsādya kṛṣṇaḥ kali yuge tathā antakāle ca saṃprāpte kālaḥ bhūtvā ati dāruṇaḥ trailokyam nāśayāmi ekaḥ sarvam sthāvara jaṅgamam aham tri dharmā viśva ātmā sarva loka sukha āvahaḥ abhinnaḥ sarvagaḥ anantaḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ urukramaḥ śamanam sarva bhūtānām sarva bhūta kṛta udyamam evam praṇihitaḥ samyak mama ātmā muni sattama sarva loke ca mām bhaktāḥ pūjayanti ca sarvaśas yat ca kiṃcid tvayā prāptam mayi kleśa ātmakam dvija yat ca kiṃcid tvayā loke dṛṣṭam sthāvara jaṅgamam vihitaḥ sarvaḥ eva asau mayā ātmā bhūta bhāvanaḥ aham nārāyaṇaḥ nāma śaṅkha cakra gadā dharaḥ yāvat yugānām viprarṣe sahasram parivartate tāvat svapimi viśvātmā sarva viśvāni mohayan aśiśuḥ śiśu rūpeṇa yāvat brahmā na budhyate asakṛt parituṣṭena vipra ṛṣi gaṇa pūjita sarvam ekārṇavam kṛtvā naṣṭe sthāvara jaṅgame abhyantaram śarīrasya praviṣṭaḥ asi yadā mama dṛṣṭvā lokam samastam hi vismitaḥ na avabudhyase tatas asi vaktrāt viprarṣe drutam niḥsāritaḥ mayā ākhyātaḥ te mayā ca ātmā durjñeyaḥ hi sura asuraiḥ yāvat sa bhagavān brahmā na budhyeta mahā tapāḥ ekaḥ bhūtāni srakṣyāmi śarīrāṇi dvijottama ākāśam pṛthivīm jyotiḥ vāyuḥ salilam eva ca evam uktvā tadā viprāḥ punar tam prāha mādhavaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca mune brūhi yad artham mām stutavān paramārthataḥ varam vṛṇīṣva yat śreṣṭham dadāmi nacirāt aham āyuṣmān asi devānām mad bhaktaḥ asi dṛḍha vrataḥ śrutvā vāṇīm śubhām tasya vilokya sa tadā punar mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca dṛṣṭam param hi deveśa tava rūpam dvijottama mohaḥ ayam vigataḥ satyam tvayi dṛṣṭe tu me hare lokānām ca hita arthāya nānābhāva praśāntaye śaiva bhāgavatānām ca vāda artha pratiṣedhakam tatas jñāsyanti loke asmin eka mūrtī hari īśvarau śrī bhagavān uvāca yat etat paramam devam kāraṇam bhuvana īśvaram liṅgam ārādhana arthāya nānā bhāva praśāntaye mama ādiṣṭena vipra indra kuru śīghram śiva ālayam tad prabhāvāt śiva loke tiṣṭha tvam ca tathā akṣayam na āvayoḥ antaram kiṃcid eka bhāvau dvidhā kṛtau yaḥ rudraḥ sa svayam viṣṇuḥ yaḥ viṣṇuḥ sa maheśvaraḥ tava nāma aṅkitam tasmāt kuru vipra śiva ālayam mārkaṇḍeyahradaḥ nāma nara lokeṣu viśrutaḥ bhaviṣyati dvijaśreṣṭha sarva pāpa praṇāśanaḥ mārkaṇḍeyam muni śreṣṭhāḥ sarvavyāpī janārdanaḥ atas param pravakṣyāmi pañcatīrtha vidhim dvijāḥ yat phalam snāna dānena devatā prekṣaṇena ca mārkaṇḍeya hradam gatvā naraḥ ca udak mukhaḥ śuciḥ namaḥ śivāya śāntāya sarva pāpa harāya ca nābhi mātre jale snātvā vidhivat devatāḥ ṛṣīn tila udakena matimān pitṝn ca anyān ca tarpayet praviśya devatāgāram kṛtvā tam tris pradakṣiṇam mūlamantreṇa saṃpūjya mārkaṇḍeyasya ca īśvaram trāhi mām tvam virūpākṣa mahādeva namaḥ astu te mārkaṇḍeya hrade tu evam snātvā dṛṣṭvā ca śaṃkaram daśānām aśvamedhānām phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ tatra bhuktvā varān bhogān yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam śāṃkaram yogam āsādya tatas mokṣam avāpnuyāt kalpavṛkṣam tatas gatvā kṛtvā tam tris pradakṣiṇam pūjayet parayā bhaktyā mantreṇa anena tam vaṭam om namaḥ vyakta rūpāya mahāpralaya kāriṇe amaraḥ tvam sadā kalpe hareḥ ca āyatanam vaṭa bhaktyā pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā natvā kalpavaṭam naraḥ sahasā mucyate pāpāt jīrṇa tvacaḥ iva uragaḥ chāyām tasya samākramya kalpavṛkṣasya bho dvijāḥ brahmahatyām naraḥ jahyāt pāpeṣu anyeṣu kā kathā dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇa aṅga saṃbhūtam brahma tejaḥ mayam param nyagrodha ākṛtikam viṣṇum praṇipatya ca bho dvijāḥ rājasūya aśvamedhābhyām phalam prāpnoti ca adhikam tathā sva vaṃśam uddhṛtya viṣṇu lokam sa gacchati dṛṣṭvā vaṭam vainateyam yaḥ paśyet puruṣottamam saṃkarṣaṇam subhadrām ca sa yāti paramām gatim praviśya āyatanam viṣṇoḥ kṛtvā tam tris pradakṣiṇam saṃkarṣaṇam sva mantreṇa bhaktyā āpūjya prasādayet namaḥ te balinām śreṣṭha namaḥ te dharaṇīdhara pralambāre namaḥ te astu trāhi mām kṛṣṇa pūrvaja evam prasādya ca anantam ajeyam tridaśa arcitam kailāsa śikhara ākāram candrāt kāntatara ānanam nīla vastra dharam devam phaṇā vikaṭa mastakam mahābalam haladharam kuṇḍala eka vibhūṣitam ābhūtasaṃplavam yāvat bhuktvā tatra sukham naraḥ puṇya kṣayāt iha āgatya pravare yoginām kule brāhmaṇa pravaraḥ bhūtvā sarva śāstra artha pāragaḥ jñānam tatra samāsādya muktim prāpnoti durlabhām evam abhyarcya halinam tatas kṛṣṇam vicakṣaṇaḥ dvādaśa akṣara mantreṇa pūjayet su samāhitaḥ pūjayanti sadā dhīrāḥ te mokṣam prāpnuvanti vai na tām gatim surāḥ yānti yoginaḥ na eva soma pāḥ yām gatim yānti bho viprāḥ dvādaśa akṣara tatparāḥ tasmāt tena eva mantreṇa bhaktyā kṛṣṇam jagadgurum saṃpūjya gandha puṣpa ādyaiḥ praṇipatya prasādayet jaya kṛṣṇa jagannātha jaya sarva agha nāśana jaya cāṇūra keśi ghna jaya kaṃsa niṣūdana saṃsāra sāgare ghore niḥsāre duḥkha phenile nimagnaḥ aham suraśreṣṭha trāhi mām puruṣottama pīna aṃsam dvi bhujam kṛṣṇam padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇam mahā uraskam mahā bāhum pīta vastram śubha ānanam śaṅkha cakra gadā pāṇim mukuṭa aṅgada bhūṣaṇam sarva lakṣaṇa saṃyuktam vanamālā vibhūṣitam dṛṣṭvā naraḥ añjalim kṛtvā daṇḍa vat praṇipatya ca aśvamedha sahasrāṇām phalam prāpnoti vai dvijāḥ naraḥ tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam praṇamya ca naraḥ tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam praṇamya ca tat phalam samavāpnoti naraḥ kṛṣṇam praṇamya ca naraḥ tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam praṇamya ca naraḥ tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam praṇamya ca naraḥ tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam praṇamya ca naraḥ tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam praṇamya ca naraḥ tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam praṇamya ca naraḥ tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam praṇamya ca dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam naraḥ bhaktyā mokṣam prāpnoti durlabham pāpaiḥ vimuktaḥ śuddha ātmā kalpa koṭi samudbhavaiḥ śriyā paramayā yuktaḥ sarvaiḥ samuditaḥ guṇaiḥ gandharva apsarasaiḥ sārdham yathā viṣṇuḥ catur bhujaḥ cyutaḥ tasmāt iha āyātaḥ viprāṇām pravare kule svadharma nirataḥ śāntaḥ dātā bhūta hite rataḥ āsādya vaiṣṇavam jñānam tatas muktim avāpnuyāt tatas saṃpūjya mantreṇa subhadrām bhakta vatsalām prasādayet tatas viprāḥ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ trāhi mām padma pattra akṣi kātyāyani namaḥ astu te evam prasādya tām devīm jagaddhātrīm jagat hitām baladevasya bhaginīm subhadrām vara dām śivām ābhūtasaṃplavam yāvat krīḍitvā tatra deva vat iha mānuṣa tām prāptaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ veda vid bhavet evam dṛṣṭvā balam kṛṣṇam subhadrām praṇipatya ca dharmam ca artham ca kāmam ca mokṣam ca labhate dhruvam niṣkramya devatāgārāt kṛtakṛtyaḥ bhavet naraḥ praṇamya āyatanam paścāt vrajet tatra samāhitaḥ indranīla mayaḥ viṣṇuḥ yatra āste vālukā vṛtaḥ antardhāna gatam natvā tatas viṣṇu puram vrajet saḥ āste tatra bho viprāḥ siṃha ardha kṛta vigrahaḥ bhaktyā dṛṣṭvā tu tam devam praṇamya narakesarīm na teṣām duṣkṛtam kiṃcid phalam syāt yat yat īpsitam dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām phalam yasmāt prayacchati munayaḥ ūcuḥ śrotum icchāmahe brūhi param kautūhalam hi naḥ brūhi tāḥ kuru ca asmākam prasādam prapitāmaha śṛṇudhvam tasya bho viprāḥ prabhāvam gadataḥ mama kaḥ śaknoti guṇān vaktum samastān tasya bho dvijāḥ siṃha ardha kṛta dehasya pravakṣyāmi samāsatas yāḥ kāścid siddhayaḥ ca atra śrūyante daiva mānuṣāḥ prasādāt tasya tāḥ sarvāḥ sidhyanti na atra saṃśayaḥ vidhānam tasya vakṣyāmi bhaktānām upakārakam śṛṇudhvam muni śārdūlāḥ kalpa rājam sanātanam narasiṃhasya tattvam ca yat na jñātam sura asuraiḥ śāka yāvaka mūlaiḥ tu phala piṇyāka saktukaiḥ kośa kaupīna vāsāḥ ca dhyāna yuktaḥ jita indriyaḥ ūṣare siddha kṣetre ca narasiṃha āśrame tathā pratiṣṭhāpya svayam vā api pūjām kṛtvā vidhānataḥ dvādaśyām śukla pakṣasya upoṣya muni puṃgavāḥ japet lakṣāṇi vai viṃśat manasā saṃyata indriyaḥ upapātaka yuktaḥ ca mahāpātaka saṃyutaḥ muktaḥ bhavet tatas viprāḥ sādhakaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam tatra narasiṃham prapūjayet puṇya gandha ādibhiḥ dhūpaiḥ praṇamya śirasā prabhum karpūra candana aktāni jātī puṣpāṇi mastake tejaḥ soḍhum na śaktāḥ syuḥ brahma rudra ādayaḥ surāḥ kim punar dānavāḥ loke siddha gandharva mānuṣāḥ vidyādharāḥ yakṣa gaṇāḥ sa kiṃnara mahā uragāḥ mantram yān āsurān hantum japanti eke anya sādhakāḥ te sarve pralayam yānti dṛṣṭvā āditya agni varcasaḥ gandharvāḥ kiṃnarāḥ yakṣāḥ vidyādhara mahā uragāḥ bhūtāḥ piśācāḥ rakṣāṃsi ye ca anye paripanthinaḥ dvādaśa abhyantare ca eva yojanānām dvijottamāḥ palāśa kāṣṭhaiḥ prajvālya bhagavantam hutāśanam dve śate dvija śārdūlāḥ vaṣaṭkāreṇa sādhakaḥ tatas vivara dvāram tu prakaṭam jāyate kṣaṇāt tatas viśet tu niḥśaṅkam kavacī vivaram budhaḥ gacchataḥ saṃkaṭam tasya tamaḥ mohaḥ ca naśyati rājamārgaḥ su vistīrṇaḥ dṛśyate bhramara ajitaḥ narasiṃham smaran tatra pātālam viśate dvijāḥ tatas strīṇām sahasrāṇi vīṇā vādana karmaṇām praveśayanti tāḥ haste gṛhītvā sādhaka īśvaram tatas rasāyanam divyam pāyayanti dvijottamāḥ krīḍate saha kanyābhiḥ yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam bhinna dehaḥ vāsudeve līyate na atra saṃśayaḥ paṭṭam śūlam ca khaḍgam ca rocanām ca maṇim tathā rasam rasāyanam ca eva pādukā añjanam eva ca kṛṣṇājinam muni śreṣṭhāḥ guṭikām ca manoharām kamaṇḍalum ca akṣa sūtram yaṣṭim saṃjīvanīm tathā siddha vidyām ca śāstrāṇi gṛhītvā sādhaka īśvaraḥ jvalat vahni sphuliṅga ūrmi veṣṭitam tri śikham hṛdi viṣe nyastam viṣam hanyāt kuṣṭham hanyāt tanau sthitam sva dehe bhrūṇahatyā ādi kṛtvā divyena śudhyati mahā graha gṛhīteṣu jvalamānam vicintayet hṛd ante vai tatas śīghram naśyeyuḥ dāruṇāḥ grahāḥ bālānām kaṇṭhake baddham rakṣā bhavati nityaśas gaṇḍa piṇḍaka lūtānām nāśanam kurute dhruvam vyādhi jāte samidbhiḥ ca ghṛta kṣīreṇa homayet trisaṃdhyam māsam ekam tu sarva rogān vināśayet yām yām kāmayate siddhim tām tām prāpnoti sa dhruvam aṣṭottaraśatam tu eke pūjayitvā mṛgādhipam mṛttikāḥ sapta valmīke śmaśāne ca catuṣpathe raktacandana saṃmiśrāḥ gavām kṣīreṇa loḍayet siṃhasya pratimām kṛtvā pramāṇena ṣaṣ aṅgulām japet saṃkhyā vihīnam tu pūjayitvā jalāśaye jala ākīrṇā muhūrtena jāyate sarva medinī athavā śuṣka vṛkṣa agre narasiṃham tu pūjayet japtvā ca aṣṭaśatam tattvam varṣantam vinivārayet mahā vātaḥ muhūrtena āgacchet na atra saṃśayaḥ punar ca dhārayet kṣipram saptasaptena vāriṇā atha tām pratimām dvāri nikhanet yasya sādhakaḥ tasmāt tam muni śārdūlāḥ bhaktyā saṃpūjayet sadā mṛgarājam mahā vīryam sarva kāma phala pradam brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ striyaḥ śūdra antya jātayaḥ saṃpūjya tam suraśreṣṭham bhaktyā siṃha vapuḥ dharam saṃpūjya tam suraśreṣṭham prāpnuvanti abhivāñchitam yakṣa vidyādhara tvam ca tathā anyat ca abhivāñchitam dṛṣṭvā stutvā namaskṛtvā saṃpūjya narakesarīm prāpnuvanti narāḥ rājyam svargam mokṣam ca durlabham narasiṃham naraḥ dṛṣṭvā labhet abhimatam phalam sakṛt dṛṣṭvā tu tam devam bhaktyā siṃha vapuḥ dharam saṃgrāme saṃkaṭe durge cora vyāghra ādi pīḍite kāntāre prāṇa saṃdehe viṣa vahni jaleṣu ca rāja ādibhyaḥ samudrebhyaḥ graha roga ādi pīḍite smṛtvā tam puruṣaḥ sarvaiḥ rāja grāmaiḥ vimucyate tathā saṃdarśane tasya vināśam yānti upadravāḥ guṭikā añjana pātāla pāduke ca rasāyanam narasiṃhe prasanne tu prāpnoti anyān ca vāñchitān yān yān kāmān abhidhyāyan bhajate narakesarīm tān tān kāmān avāpnoti naraḥ na asti atra saṃśayaḥ dṛṣṭvā tam devadeveśam bhaktyā āpūjya praṇamya ca daśānām aśvamedhānām phalam daśaguṇam labhet pāpaiḥ sarvaiḥ vinirmuktaḥ guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ alaṃkṛtaḥ sarva kāma samṛddha ātmā jarā maraṇa varjitaḥ sauvarṇena vimānena kiṅkiṇī jāla mālinā taruṇa āditya varṇena muktā hāra avalambinā stūyamānaḥ apsarobhiḥ ca viṣṇu lokam vrajet naraḥ bhuktvā tatra varān bhogān viṣṇu loke dvijottamāḥ manaḥ hlāda karam saukhyam yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam puṇya kṣayāt iha āyātaḥ pravare yoginām kule vaiṣṇavam yogam āsthāya tatas mokṣam avāpnuyāt ananta ākhyam vāsudevam dṛṣṭvā bhaktyā praṇamya ca mayā ca ārādhitaḥ ca asau śakreṇa tad anantaram vibhīṣaṇena rāmeṇa kaḥ tam na ārādhayet pumān śvetagaṅgām naraḥ snātvā yaḥ paśyet śvetamādhavam matsya ākhyam mādhavam ca eva śvetadvīpam sa gacchati munayaḥ ūcuḥ śveta mādhava māhātmyam vaktum arhasi aśeṣatas śveta ākhyam mādhavam devam kaḥ tam sthāpitavān purā abhūt kṛta yuge viprāḥ śvetaḥ nāma nṛpaḥ balī matimān dharma vid śūraḥ satya saṃdhaḥ dṛḍha vrataḥ yasya rājye tu varṣāṇām sahasram daśa mānavāḥ vartamāne tadā rājye kiṃcid kāle gate dvijāḥ kapālagautamaḥ nāma ṛṣiḥ parama dhārmikaḥ sutaḥ asya ajāta dantaḥ ca mṛtaḥ kāla vaśāt dvijāḥ tam ādāya ṛṣiḥ dhīmān nṛpasya antikam ānayat dṛṣṭvā evam nṛpatiḥ suptam kumāram gata cetasam pratijñām akarot viprāḥ jīvana artham śiśoḥ tadā rājā uvāca na ānaye sapta rātreṇa citām dīptām samāruhe evam uktvā asitaiḥ padmaiḥ śataiḥ daśa śata ādikaiḥ saṃpūjya ca mahādevam rājā vidyām punar japet atibhaktim tu saṃcintya nṛpasya jagat īśvaraḥ sāṃnidhyam agamat tuṣṭaḥ śmi iti uvāca saha umayā śārdūla carma vasanam śaśāṅka aṅkita mūrdhajam mahīm nipatya sahasā praṇamya sa tadā bravīt śvetaḥ uvāca kāruṇyam yadi me dṛṣṭvā prasannaḥ asi prabho yadi yathā ukta āyuṣya saṃyuktam kṣemam kuru maheśvara śvetasya etat vacaḥ śrutvā mudam prāpa haraḥ tadā kālam ājñāpayām āsa sarva bhūta bhayaṃkaram niyamya kālam durdharṣam yamasya ājñā karam dvijāḥ bālam saṃjīvayām āsa mṛtyoḥ mukha gatam punar kṛtvā kṣemam jagat sarvam muneḥ putram sa tam dvijāḥ evam saṃjīvayām āsa muneḥ putram nṛpa uttamaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ brūhi naḥ paramam tathyam śveta ākhyasya ca sāṃpratam śṛṇudhvam muni śārdūlāḥ sarva sattva hita āvaham pravakṣyāmi yathātathyam yat pṛcchatha mama anaghāḥ mādhavasya ca māhātmyam sarva pāpa praṇāśanam yat śrutvā abhimatān kāmān dhruvam prāpnoti mānavaḥ śrutavān ṛṣibhiḥ pūrvam mādhava ākhyasya bho dvijāḥ śṛṇudhvam tām kathām divyām bhaya śoka ārti nāśinīm sa kṛtvā rājyam ekāgryam varṣāṇām ca sahasraśas vicārya laukikān dharmān vaidikān niyamān tathā keśava ārādhane viprāḥ niścitam vratam āsthitaḥ sa gatvā paramam kṣetram sāgaram dakṣiṇa āśrayam taṭe tasmin śubhe ramye deśe kṛṣṇasya ca antike śvetaḥ atha kārayām āsa prāsādam śubha lakṣaṇam tatas śvetena vipra indrāḥ śvetaśaila mayena ca kṛtaḥ sa bhagavān śvetaḥ mādhavaḥ candra saṃnibhaḥ pratiṣṭhām vidhivat cakre yathā uddiṣṭām svayam tu saḥ dattvā dānam dvijātibhyaḥ dīna anātha tapasvinām mahīm nipatya sahasā oṃkāram dvādaśa akṣaram japan sa maunam āsthāya māsam ekam samādhinā nirāhāraḥ mahābhāgaḥ samyak viṣṇu pade sthitaḥ śvetaḥ uvāca om namaḥ vāsudevāya namaḥ saṃkarṣaṇāya ca pradyumnāya aniruddhāya namaḥ nārāyaṇāya ca nirguṇāya apratarkyāya śucaye śukla karmaṇe om namaḥ puṣkarākṣāya sahasrākṣāya mīḍhuṣe variṣṭhāya vareṇyāya śaraṇyāya acyutāya ca om namaḥ bāla rūpāya bāla padma prabhāya ca bāla arka soma netrāya muñjakeśāya dhīmate keśavāya namaḥ nityam namaḥ nārāyaṇāya ca mādhavāya variṣṭhāya govindāya namaḥ namaḥ madhusūdanāya namaḥ śuddhāya aṃśudharāya ca namaḥ anantāya sūkṣmāya namaḥ śrīvatsa dhāriṇe namaḥ astu guṇa bhūtāya nirguṇāya namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ vāmana rūpāya namaḥ vāmana karmaṇe saṃsāra arṇava potāya praśāntāya svarūpiṇe śivāya saumya rūpāya rudrāya uttāraṇāya ca bhava saṃghāta rūpāya bhava sṛṣṭi kṛte namaḥ om namaḥ divya rūpāya soma agni śvasitāya ca soma sūrya aṃśu keśāya go brāhmaṇa hitāya ca om namaḥ ṛk svarūpāya padakrama svarūpiṇe ṛk stutāya namaḥ tubhyam namaḥ ṛk sādhanāya ca om namaḥ yajuṣām dhātre yajuḥ rūpa dharāya ca yajuḥ yājyāya juṣṭāya yajuṣām pataye namaḥ om namaḥ śrīpate deva śrīdharāya varāya ca śriyaḥ kāntāya dāntāya yogi cintyāya yogine om namaḥ sāma rūpāya sāma dhvani varāya ca om namaḥ sāma saumyāya sāma yoga vide namaḥ sāmne ca sāma gītāya om namaḥ sāma dhāriṇe om namaḥ vajraśīrṣāya madhu kaiṭabha ghātine namaḥ dīpta svarūpāya hṛṣīkeśāya vai namaḥ om namaḥ moha nāśāya bhava bhaṅga karāya ca yogi īśvarāya śuddhāya rāmāya uttaraṇāya ca sukhāya sukha netrāya namaḥ sukṛta dhāriṇe vāsudevāya vandyāya vāmadevāya vai namaḥ namaḥ vāsa nivāsāya vāsa vyavaharāya ca namaḥ yajña svarūpāya yajñeśāya ca yogine yati yoga kara īśāya namaḥ yajña aṅga dhāriṇe saṃkarṣaṇāya ca namaḥ pralamba mathanāya ca megha ghoṣa svana uttīrṇa vega lāṅgala dhāriṇe namaḥ astu jñāninām jñāna nārāyaṇa parāyaṇa malam yat kāya jam vā api mānasam ca eva keśava na tasya anyaḥ asti deveśa kṣālakaḥ tvām ṛte acyuta saṃsargāṇi samastāni vihāya tvām upasthitaḥ saṅgaḥ me astu tvayā sārdham ātma lābhāya keśava kaṣṭam āpad su duṣpāram saṃsāram vedmi keśava tāpa traya parikliṣṭaḥ tena tvām śaraṇam gataḥ eṣaṇābhiḥ jagat sarvam mohitam māyayā tava ākarṣitam ca lobha ādyaiḥ atas tvām aham āśritaḥ na asti kiṃcid sukham viṣṇo saṃsāra sthasya dehinaḥ naṣṭaḥ viveka śūnyaḥ asmi dṛśyate jagat āturam uddhartā puṇḍarīkākṣa tvām ṛte anyaḥ na vidyate ittham stutaḥ tatas tena rājñā śvetena bho dvijāḥ ājagāma nṛpasya agre sarvaiḥ devaiḥ vṛtaḥ hariḥ nīla jīmūta saṃkāśaḥ padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇaḥ dadhat sudarśanam dhīmān kara agre dīpta maṇḍalam kṣīroda jala saṃkāśaḥ vimalaḥ candra saṃnibhaḥ rarāja vāma haste asya pāñcajanyaḥ mahā dyutiḥ pakṣirāja dhvajaḥ śrīmān gadā śārṅga asi dhṛk prabhuḥ praṇamya śirasā uvāca śvetaḥ tad gata mānasaḥ śvetaḥ uvāca ā brahma bhavanāt ūrdhvam vaiṣṇavam padam avyayam vimalam virajam śuddham saṃsāra asaṅga varjitam śrī bhagavān uvāca yāsyasi paramam sthānam rājya amṛtam upāsya ca kīrtiḥ tava atra rāja indra trīn lokān ca gamiṣyati śvetagaṅgā iti gāsyanti sarve te deva dānavāḥ kuśa agreṇa api rāja indra śveta gāṅgeyam ambu ca spṛṣṭvā svargam gamiṣyanti mad bhaktāḥ ye samāhitāḥ yaḥ tu imām pratimām gacchet mādhava ākhyām śaśiprabhām śaṅkha go kṣīra saṃkāśām aśeṣa agha vināśinīm tām praṇamya sakṛt bhaktyā puṇḍarīka nibha īkṣaṇām manvantarāṇi tatra eva deva kanyābhiḥ āvṛtaḥ bhunakti vipulān bhogān yatheṣṭam māmakaiḥ saha veda vedāṅga vid śrīmān bhogavān cira jīvitaḥ gaja aśva ratha yāna āḍhyaḥ dhana dhānya āvṛtaḥ śuciḥ puruṣottamam punar prāpya vaṭa mūle atha sāgare tyaktvā deham harim smṛtvā tatas śānta padam vrajet ekārṇava jale pūrvam rohitam rūpam āsthitam vedānām haraṇa arthāya rasātala tale sthitam ādya avataraṇam rūpam mādhavam matsya rūpiṇam kāle punar iha āyātaḥ rājā syāt pṛthivī tale vatsa mādhavam āsādya durādharṣaḥ bhavet naraḥ dātā bhoktā bhavet yajvā vaiṣṇavaḥ satya saṃgaraḥ yogam prāpya hareḥ paścāt tatas mokṣam avāpnuyāt matsya mādhava māhātmyam mayā saṃparikīrtitam yam dṛṣṭvā muni śārdūlāḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt munayaḥ ūcuḥ bhagavan śrotum icchāmaḥ mārjanam varuṇālaye kriyate snāna dāna ādi tasya aśeṣa phalam vada śṛṇudhvam muni śārdūlāḥ mārjanasya yathāvidhi bhaktyā tu tad manāḥ bhūtvā saṃprāpya puṇyam uttamam mārkaṇḍeyahrade snānam pūrva kāle praśasyate caturdaśyām viśeṣeṇa sarva pāpa praṇāśanam paurṇamāsyām viśeṣeṇa hayamedha phalam labhet mārkaṇḍeyam vaṭam kṛṣṇam rauhiṇeyam mahā udadhim indradyumna saraḥ ca eva pañca tīrthī vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ pūrṇimā jyeṣṭha māsasya jyeṣṭhāḥ ṛkṣam yadā bhavet tadā gacchet viśeṣeṇa tīrtha rājam param śubham kāya vāc mānasaiḥ śuddhaḥ tad bhāvaḥ na anya mānasaḥ kalpavṛkṣa vaṭam ramyam tatra snātvā janārdanam pradakṣiṇam prakurvīta tri vāram su samāhitaḥ yam dṛṣṭvā mucyate pāpāt sapta janma samudbhavāt puṇyam ca āpnoti vipulam gatim iṣṭām ca bho dvijāḥ tasya nāmāni vakṣyāmi pramāṇam ca yuge yuge yathāsaṃkhyam ca bho viprāḥ kṛta ādiṣu yathākramam vaṭam vaṭeśvaram kṛṣṇam purāṇapuruṣam dvijāḥ vaṭasya etāni nāmāni kīrtitāni kṛta ādiṣu yojanam pāda hīnam ca yojana ardham tad ardhakam pramāṇam kalpavṛkṣasya kṛta ādau parikīrtitam yatra asau dṛśyate viṣṇuḥ svarga dvāram manoramam sāgara ambhaḥ samākṛṣṭam kāṣṭham sarva guṇa anvitam ugrasenam purā dṛṣṭvā svargadvāreṇa sāgaram gatvā ācamya śuciḥ tatra dhyātvā nārāyaṇam param nyaset aṣṭa akṣaram mantram paścāt hasta śarīrayoḥ om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya iti yam vadanti manīṣiṇaḥ om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya iti mantraḥ sarva artha sādhakaḥ āpaḥ narasya sūnu tvāt nārāḥ iti iha kīrtitāḥ viṣṇoḥ tāḥ tu ayanam pūrvam tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ nārāyaṇa parāḥ vedāḥ nārāyaṇa parāḥ dvijāḥ nārāyaṇa parāḥ yajñāḥ nārāyaṇa parāḥ kriyāḥ nārāyaṇa parā pṛthvī nārāyaṇa param jalam nārāyaṇa paraḥ vahniḥ nārāyaṇa param nabhaḥ nārāyaṇa paraḥ vāyuḥ nārāyaṇa param manaḥ ahaṃkāraḥ ca buddhiḥ ca ubhe nārāyaṇa ātmake bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyam ca yat kiṃcid jīva saṃjñitam sthūlam sūkṣmam param ca eva sarvam nārāyaṇa ātmakam śabda ādyāḥ viṣayāḥ sarve śrotra ādīni indriyāṇi ca prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ ca eva sarve nārāyaṇa ātmakāḥ avaṣṭabhya idam sarvam āste nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ brahma ādi stamba paryantam sarvam nārāyaṇa ātmakam nārāyaṇāt param kiṃcid nā iha paśyāmi bho dvijāḥ tena vyāptam idam sarvam dṛśya adṛśyam carācaram āpaḥ hi āyatanam viṣṇoḥ sa ca eva ambhasām patiḥ tasmāt apsu smaret nityam nārāyaṇam agha apaham snāna kāle viśeṣeṇa ca upasthāya jale śuciḥ oṃkāram ca nakāram ca aṅguṣṭhe hastayoḥ nyaset oṃkāram vāma pāde tu nakāram dakṣiṇe nyaset mokāram vāma kaṭyām tu nākāram dakṣiṇe nyaset rākāram nābhi deśe tu yakāram vāma bāhuke ṇākāram dakṣiṇe nyasya yakāram mūrdhni vinyaset adhas ca ūrdhvam ca hṛdaye pārśvatas pṛṣṭhatas agratas dhyātvā nārāyaṇam paścāt ārabhet kavacam budhaḥ pūrve mām pātu govindaḥ dakṣiṇe madhusūdanaḥ pātu viṣṇuḥ tathā āgneye nairṛte mādhavaḥ avyayaḥ vāyavye tu hṛṣīkeśaḥ tathā īśāne ca vāmanaḥ kṛtvā evam kavacam paścāt ātmānam cintayet tatas aham nārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ śaṅkha cakra gadā dharaḥ evam dhyātvā tadā ātmānam imam mantram udīrayet tvam agniḥ dvipadām nātha retaḥ dhāḥ kāma dīpanaḥ pradhānaḥ sarva bhūtānām jīvānām prabhuḥ avyayaḥ amṛtasya araṇiḥ tvam hi deva yoniḥ apām pate anyathā bho dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ snānam tatra na śasyate antar jale japet paścāt tris āvṛttya aghamarṣaṇam hayamedhaḥ yathā viprāḥ sarva pāpa haraḥ kratuḥ tathā aghamarṣaṇam ca atra sūktam sarva agha nāśanam prāṇān āyamya ca ācamya saṃdhyām ca upāsya bhāskaram upatiṣṭhet tatas ca ūrdhvam kṣiptvā puṣpa jala añjalim upasthāya ūrdhva bāhuḥ ca tad liṅgaiḥ bhāskaram tatas gāyatrīm pāvanīm devīm japet aṣṭa uttaram śatam anyān ca saura mantrān ca japtvā tiṣṭhan samāhitaḥ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam sūryam namaskṛtya upaviśya ca svādhyāyam prāc mukhaḥ kṛtvā tarpayet daivatāni ṛṣīn manuṣyān ca pitṝn ca anyān nāma gotreṇa mantra vid tarpaṇam devatānām ca pūrvam kṛtvā samāhitaḥ adhikārī bhavet paścāt pitṝṇām tarpaṇe dvijaḥ tarpaṇe tu ubhayam kuryāt eṣaḥ eva vidhiḥ sadā anvārabdhena savyena pāṇinā dakṣiṇena tu tṛpyatām iti siñcet tu nāma gotreṇa vāgyataḥ bhūmyām yat dīyate toyam dātā ca eva jale sthitaḥ vṛthā tat muni śārdūlāḥ nā upatiṣṭhati kasyacid pitṝṇām na upatiṣṭheta salilam tat nirarthakam na udakeṣu na pātreṣu na kruddhaḥ na eka pāṇinā na upatiṣṭhati tat toyam yat bhūmyām na pradīyate pitṝṇām akṣayam sthānam mahī dattā mayā dvijāḥ tasmāt tatra eva dātavyam pitṝṇām prītim icchatā bhūmi pṛṣṭhe samutpannāḥ bhūmyām ca eva ca saṃsthitāḥ bhūmyām ca eva layam yātā bhūmau dadyāt tatas jalam āstīrya ca kuśān sāgrān tān āvāhya sva mantrataḥ prācīna agreṣu vai devān yāmya agreṣu tathā pitṝn devān pitṝn tathā ca anyān saṃtarpya ācamya vāgyataḥ hasta mātram catuṣkoṇam catur dvāram su śobhanam evam maṇḍalam ālikhya pūjayet tatra bho dvijāḥ aṣṭa akṣara vidhānena nārāyaṇam ajam vibhum atas param pravakṣyāmi kāya śodhanam uttamam akāram hṛdaye dhyātvā cakra rekhā samanvitam jvalantam triśikham ca eva dahantam pāpa nāśanam candra maṇḍala madhya stham rākāram mūrdhni cintayet śukla varṇam pravarṣantam amṛtam plāvayan mahīm aṣṭa akṣaram tatas mantram nyaset eva ātmanaḥ budhaḥ vāma pādam samārabhya kramaśas ca eva vinyaset pañca aṅgam vaiṣṇavam ca eva catur vyūham tathā eva ca kara śuddhim prakurvīta mūlamantreṇa sādhakaḥ ekaikam ca eva varṇam tu aṅgulīṣu pṛthak pṛthak oṃkāram pṛthivīm śuklām vāma pāde tu vinyaset nakāraḥ śāṃbhavaḥ śyāmaḥ dakṣiṇe tu vyavasthitaḥ mokāram kālam eva āhuḥ vāma kaṭyām nidhāpayet na ākāraḥ sarva bījam tu dakṣiṇasyām vyavasthitaḥ rākāraḥ tejaḥ iti āhuḥ nābhi deśe vyavasthitaḥ vāyavyaḥ ayam yakāraḥ tu vāma skandhe samāśritaḥ ṇākāraḥ sarva gaḥ jñeyaḥ dakṣiṇa aṃse vyavasthitaḥ yakāraḥ ayam śira sthaḥ ca yatra lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ om viṣṇave namaḥ śiraḥ om jvalanāya namaḥ śikhā om viṣṇave namaḥ kavacam om viṣṇave namaḥ sphuraṇam diśobandhāya om huṃ phaṭ astram om śirasi śuklaḥ vāsudevaḥ iti om ām lalāṭe raktaḥ saṃkarṣaṇaḥ garutmān vahniḥ tejaḥ ādityaḥ iti om ām grīvāyām pītaḥ pradyumnaḥ vāyu meghaḥ iti om āṃ hṛdaye kṛṣṇaḥ aniruddhaḥ sarva śakti samanvitaḥ iti evam catur vyūham ātmānam kṛtvā tatas karma samācaret mama agre avasthitaḥ viṣṇuḥ pṛṣṭhatas ca api keśavaḥ govindaḥ dakṣiṇe pārśve vāme tu madhusūdanaḥ upariṣṭāt tu vaikuṇṭhaḥ vārāhaḥ pṛthivī tale avāntara diśaḥ yāḥ tu tāsu sarvāsu mādhavaḥ gacchataḥ tiṣṭhataḥ vā api jāgrataḥ svapataḥ api vā evam viṣṇu mayaḥ bhūtvā tatas karma samārabhet tatas ca eva prakurvīta prokṣaṇam praṇavena tu phaṭkāra antam samuddiṣṭam sarva vighna haram śubham tatra arka candra vahnīnām maṇḍalāni vicintayet tatas vicintya hṛdaye oṃkāram jyotiḥ rūpiṇam karṇikāyām samāsīnam jyotiḥ rūpam sanātanam aṣṭa akṣaram tatas mantram vinyaset ca yathākramam dvādaśa akṣara mantreṇa yajet devam sanātanam tatas avadhārya hṛdaye karṇikāyām bahis nyaset cintayitvā mahā yogam jyotīḥ rūpam sanātanam tatas ca āvāhayet mantram krameṇa ācintya mānase āvāhana mantraḥ mīna rūpaḥ varāhaḥ ca narasiṃhaḥ atha vāmanaḥ āyātu devaḥ vara daḥ mama nārāyaṇaḥ agratas om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ karṇikāyām su pīṭhe atra padma kalpitam āsanam om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ argha mantraḥ om trailokya patīnām pataye devadevāya hṛṣīkeśāya viṣṇave namaḥ om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ pādya mantraḥ om pādyam pādayoḥ deva padmanābha sanātana viṣṇo kamala pattra akṣa gṛhāṇa madhusūdana om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ mayā niveditam bhaktyā gṛhāṇa puruṣottama om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ mandākinyāḥ sitam vāri sarva pāpa haram śivam gṛhāṇa ācamanīyam tvam mayā bhaktyā niveditam om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ snāna mantraḥ tvam āpaḥ pṛthivī ca eva jyotiḥ tvam vāyuḥ eva ca lokeśa vṛtti mātreṇa vāriṇā snāpayāmi aham om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ śarīram te na jānāmi ceṣṭām ca eva ca keśava om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ṛk yajuḥ sāma mantreṇa trivṛtam padmayoninā sāvitrī granthi saṃyuktam upavītam tava arpaye om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ alaṃkāra mantraḥ gātrāṇi tava śobhantu sa alaṃkārāṇi mādhava om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ dhūpa mantraḥ mayā niveditaḥ bhaktyā dhūpaḥ ayam pratigṛhyatām om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ dīpa mantraḥ tvam eva jyotiṣām deva dīpaḥ ayam pratigṛhyatām om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ om namaḥ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ pūrve dale vāsudevam yāmye saṃkarṣaṇam nyaset vārāham ca tathā āgneye narasiṃham ca nairṛte tathā aṣṭa akṣara devasya garuḍam puratas nyaset vāma pārśve tathā cakram śaṅkham dakṣiṇatas nyaset tathā mahāgadām ca eva nyaset devasya dakṣiṇe tatas śārṅgam dhanuḥ vidvān nyaset devasya vāmatas dakṣiṇena iṣudhī divye khaḍgam vāme ca vinyaset śriyam dakṣiṇatas sthāpya puṣṭim uttaratas nyaset vinyaset dhṛdaya ādīni pūrva ādiṣu caturdiśam indram agnim yamam ca eva nairṛtam varuṇam tathā vāyum dhana dam īśānam anantam brahmaṇā saha evam saṃpūjya deveśam maṇḍala stham janārdanam labhet abhimatān kāmān naraḥ na asti atra saṃśayaḥ pūjitam yaḥ saṃpaśyeta sa viśet viṣṇum avyayam janma mṛtyu jarām tīrtvā sa viṣṇoḥ padam āpnuyāt yaḥ smaret satatam bhaktyā nārāyaṇam atandritaḥ anvaham tasya vāsāya śvetadvīpaḥ prakalpitaḥ oṃkāra ādi samāyuktam namaḥkāra anta dīpitam aṣṭāviṃśatim aṣṭau vā śatam aṣṭa uttaram tathā kāmeṣu ca yathāproktam yathāśakti samāhitaḥ padmam śaṅkhaḥ ca śrīvatsaḥ gadāḥ garuḍaḥ eva ca cakram khaḍgaḥ ca śārṅgam ca aṣṭau mudrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ praṇamya śirasā paścāt sāgaram ca prasādayet prāṇaḥ tvam sarva bhūtānām yoniḥ ca saritām pate tīre ca abhyarcya vidhivat nārāyaṇam anāmayam rāmam kṛṣṇam subhadrām ca praṇipatya ca sāgaram śatānām aśvamedhānām phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ vṛndārakaḥ iva śrīmān rūpa yauvana garvitaḥ bhuktvā tatra varān bhogān krīḍitvā ca apsaraiḥ saha manvantara śatam sāgram jarā mṛtyu vivarjitaḥ puṇya kṣayāt iha āyātaḥ kule sarva guṇa anvite rūpavān subhagaḥ śrīmān satya vādī jita indriyaḥ veda śāstra artha vid vipraḥ bhavet yajvā tu vaiṣṇavaḥ yogam ca vaiṣṇavam prāpya tatas mokṣam avāpnuyāt graha uparāge saṃkrāntyām ayane viṣuve tathā yuga ādiṣu ṣaṣ aśītyām vyatīpāte dinakṣaye āṣāḍhyām ca eva kārttikyām māghyām vā anye śubhe tithau pitṝṇām ye prayacchanti piṇḍam tatra vidhānataḥ akṣayām pitaraḥ teṣām tṛptim saṃprāpnuvanti vai dānasya ca phalam viprāḥ piṇḍa dānasya ca eva hi bhukti mukti phalam nṝṇām dhanyam duḥsvapna nāśanam nāstikāya na vaktavyam purāṇam ca dvijottamāḥ tāvat garjanti tīrthāni māhātmyaiḥ svaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak yāvat na tīrtha rājasya māhātmyam varṇyate dvijāḥ bhū tale yāni tīrthāni saritaḥ ca sarāṃsi ca viśanti sāgare tāni tena asau śreṣṭha tām gataḥ rājā samasta tīrthānām sāgaraḥ saritām patiḥ tasmāt samasta tīrthebhyaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ asau sarva kāma daḥ tamaḥ nāśam yathā abhyeti bhāskare abhyudite dvijāḥ snānena tīrtha rājasya tathā pāpasya saṃkṣayaḥ tīrtharāja samam tīrtham na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati adhiṣṭhānam yadā yatra prabhoḥ nārāyaṇasya vai kaḥ śaknoti guṇān vaktum tīrtharājasya bho dvijāḥ tasmāt snānam ca dānam ca homam japyam sura arcanam tatas gacchet dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ tīrtham yajña aṅga saṃbhavam gatvā tatra śuciḥ dhīmān ācamya manasā harim aśvamedha aṅga saṃbhūta tīrtha sarva agha nāśana evam uccārya vidhivat snātvā devān ṛṣīn pitṝn tila udakena ca anyān ca saṃtarpya ācamya vāgyataḥ dattvā pitṝṇām piṇḍān ca saṃpūjya puruṣottamam daśāśvamedhikam samyak phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ sapta avarān sapta parān vaṃśān uddhṛtya deva vat evam kṛtvā pañcatīrthīm ekādaśyām upoṣitaḥ jyeṣṭha śukla pañcadaśyām yaḥ paśyet puruṣottamam sa pūrva uktam phalam prāpya krīḍitvā vā acyuta ālaye prayāti paramam sthānam yasmāt na āvartate punar munayaḥ ūcuḥ māsān anyān parityajya māgha ādīn prapitāmaha praśaṃsasi katham jyeṣṭham brūhi tad kāraṇam prabho śṛṇudhvam muni śārdūlāḥ pravakṣyāmi samāsatas jyeṣṭham māsam yathā tebhyaḥ praśaṃsāmi punar punar pṛthivyām yāni tīrthāni saritaḥ ca sarāṃsi ca puṣkariṇyaḥ taḍāgāni vāpyaḥ kūpāḥ tathā hradāḥ nānā nadyaḥ samudrāḥ ca sapta aham puruṣottame jyeṣṭha śukla daśamī ādi pratyakṣam yānti sarvadā snāna dāna ādikam tasmāt devatā prekṣaṇam dvijāḥ śuklapakṣasya daśamī jyeṣṭhe māsi dvijottamāḥ harate daśa pāpāni tasmāt daśaharā smṛtā yaḥ tasyām halinam kṛṣṇam paśyet bhadrām su saṃyataḥ dṛṣṭvā rāmam subhadrām ca viṣṇu lokam vrajet naraḥ naraḥ dolā gatam dṛṣṭvā govindam puruṣottamam viṣuvat divase prāpte pañcatīrthīm vidhānataḥ kṛtvā saṃkarṣaṇam kṛṣṇam dṛṣṭvā bhadrām ca bho dvijāḥ naraḥ samasta yajñānām phalam prāpnoti durlabham yaḥ paśyati tṛtīyāyām kṛṣṇam candana rūṣitam jyaiṣṭhyām jyeṣṭha ṛkṣa yuktāyām yaḥ paśyet puruṣottamam yadā bhavet mahājyaiṣṭhī rāśi nakṣatra yogataḥ kṛṣṇam dṛṣṭvā mahā jyaiṣṭhyām rāmam bhadrām ca bho dvijāḥ naraḥ dvādaśa yātrāyāḥ phalam prāpnoti ca adhikam gaṅgādvāre kuśāvarte gaṅgāsāgara saṃgame kokāmukhe śūkare ca mathurāyām maru sthale śālagrāme vāyutīrthe mandare sindhusāgare piṇḍārake citrakūṭe prabhāse kanakhale dvijāḥ śaṅkhoddhāre dvārakāyām tathā badarikāśrame lohakuṇḍe ca aśvatīrthe sarva pāpa pramocane kāmālaye koṭitīrthe tathā ca amarakaṇṭake ekāmrake ca kedāre kāśyām ca viraje dvijāḥ kālañjare ca gokarṇe śrīśaile gandhamādane gaṅgāyām sarva tīrtheṣu yāmuneṣu ca bho dvijāḥ godāvarī bhīmarathī tuṅgabhadrā ca narmadā tāpī payouṣṇī kāverī śiprā carmaṇvatī dvijāḥ vitastā candrabhāgā ca śatadruḥ bāhudā tathā ṛṣikulyā kumārī ca vipāśā ca dṛṣadvatī śarayūḥ nākagaṅgā ca gaṇḍakī ca mahā nadī kauśikī karatoyā ca trisrotāḥ madhuvāhinī mahā nadī vaitaraṇī yāḥ ca anyāḥ na anukīrtitāḥ athavā kim bahu uktena bhāṣitena dvijottamāḥ pṛthivyām sarva tīrtheṣu sarveṣu āyataneṣu ca sāgareṣu ca śaileṣu nadīṣu ca saraḥsu ca tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mahājyaiṣṭhyām labhet naraḥ mahājyaiṣṭhyām muni śreṣṭhā sarva kāma phala īpsubhiḥ dṛṣṭvā rāmam mahā jyeṣṭham kṛṣṇam subhadrayā saha viṣṇu lokam naraḥ yāti samuddhṛtya samam kulam bhuktvā tatra varān bhogān yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam svadharma nirataḥ śāntaḥ kṛṣṇa bhaktaḥ jita indriyaḥ vaiṣṇavam yogam āsthāya tatas mokṣam avāpnuyāt munayaḥ ūcuḥ śṛṇudhvam munayaḥ snānam kṛṣṇasya vadataḥ mama rāmasya ca subhadrāyāḥ puṇyam sarva agha nāśanam paurṇamāsyām tadā snānam sarvakālam hareḥ dvijāḥ sarva tīrtha mayaḥ kūpaḥ tatra āste nirmalaḥ śuciḥ tadā bhogavatī tatra pratyakṣā bhavati dvijāḥ tasmāt jyaiṣṭhyām samuddhṛtya haima āḍhyaiḥ kalaśaiḥ jalam kṛṣṇa rāma abhiṣeka artham subhadrāyāḥ ca bho dvijāḥ kṛtvā su śobhanam mañcam patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛtam su dṛḍham sukha saṃcāram vastraiḥ puṣpaiḥ alaṃkṛtam vistīrṇam dhūpitam dhūpaiḥ snāna artham rāma kṛṣṇayoḥ tatra nānāvidhaiḥ vādyaiḥ kṛṣṇam nīla ambaram dvijāḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiḥ ca anyaiḥ ca jātibhiḥ aneka śata sāhasraiḥ vṛtam strī puruṣaiḥ dvijāḥ gṛhasthāḥ snātakāḥ ca eva yatayaḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ snāpayanti tadā kṛṣṇam mañca stham sahalāyudham tathā samasta tīrthāni pūrva uktāni dvijottamāḥ sva udakaiḥ puṣpa miśraiḥ ca snāpayanti pṛthak pṛthak paścāt paṭaha śaṅkha ādyaiḥ bherī muraja nisvanaiḥ kāhalaiḥ tāla śabdaiḥ ca mṛdaṅgaiḥ jharjharaiḥ tathā anyaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ vādyaiḥ ghaṇṭā svana vibhūṣitaiḥ strīṇām maṅgala śabdaiḥ ca stuti śabdaiḥ manoharaiḥ jaya śabdaiḥ tathā stotraiḥ vīṇā veṇu nināditaiḥ śrūyate su mahān śabdaḥ sāgarasya iva garjataḥ munīnām veda śabdena mantra śabdaiḥ tathā aparaiḥ nānā stotra ravaiḥ puṇyaiḥ sāma śabda upabṛṃhitaiḥ snāna kāle suraśreṣṭha stuvanti parayā mudā śyāmaiḥ veśyā janaiḥ ca eva kuca bhāra avanāmibhiḥ pīta rakta ambarābhiḥ ca mālya dāma avanāmibhiḥ cāmaraiḥ ratna daṇḍaiḥ ca vījyete rāma keśavau yakṣa vidyādharaiḥ siddhaiḥ kiṃnaraiḥ ca apsaraḥ gaṇaiḥ ādityāḥ vasavaḥ rudrāḥ sādhyāḥ viśve marut gaṇāḥ trailokya dhāriṇam devam brahmaṇyam mokṣa kāraṇam stutvā evam vibudhāḥ kṛṣṇam rāmam ca eva mahā balam subhadrām ca muni śreṣṭhāḥ tad ākāśe vyavasthitāḥ deva tūryāṇi avādyanta vātāḥ vānti suśītalāḥ puṣpa miśram tadā meghāḥ varṣanti ākāśa gocarāḥ jaya śabdam ca kurvanti munayaḥ siddha cāraṇāḥ śakra ādyāḥ vibudhāḥ sarve ṛṣayaḥ pitaraḥ tathā prajānām patayaḥ nāgāḥ ye ca anye svarga vāsinaḥ ābhiṣecanikam dravyam gṛhītvā devatā gaṇāḥ indraḥ viṣṇuḥ mahā vīryaḥ sūryācandramasau tathā dhātā ca eva vidhātā ca tathā ca eva anila analau pūṣā bhagaḥ aryamā tvaṣṭā aṃśunā eva vivasvatā patnībhyām sahitaḥ dhīmān mitreṇa varuṇena ca rudraiḥ vasubhiḥ ādityaiḥ aśvibhyām ca vṛtaḥ prabhuḥ vaikhānasaiḥ vālakhilyaiḥ vāyu āhāraiḥ marīcipaiḥ bhṛgubhiḥ ca aṅgirobhiḥ ca sarva vidyā su niṣṭhitaiḥ pitāmahaḥ pulastyaḥ ca pulahaḥ ca mahā tapāḥ aṅgirāḥ kaśyapaḥ atriḥ ca marīciḥ bhṛguḥ eva ca ṛtavaḥ ca grahāḥ ca eva jyotīṃṣi ca dvijottamāḥ mūrtimatyaḥ ca saritaḥ devāḥ ca eva sanātanāḥ samudrāḥ ca hradāḥ ca eva tīrthāni vividhāni ca pṛthivī dyauḥ diśaḥ ca eva pādapāḥ ca dvijottamāḥ aditiḥ deva mātā ca hrīḥ śrīḥ svāhā sarasvatī umā śacī sinīvālī tathā ca anumatiḥ kuhūḥ rākā ca dhiṣaṇā ca eva patnyaḥ ca anyāḥ divaukasām himavān ca eva vindhyaḥ ca meruḥ ca aneka śṛṅgavān airāvataḥ sa anucaraḥ kalā kāṣṭhāḥ tathā eva ca māsa ardham māsa ṛtavaḥ tathā rātri ahanī samāḥ uccaiḥśravāḥ haya śreṣṭhaḥ nāga rājaḥ ca vāmanaḥ aruṇaḥ garuḍaḥ ca eva vṛkṣāḥ ca oṣadhibhiḥ saha dharmaḥ ca bhagavān devaḥ samājagmuḥ hi saṃgatāḥ kālaḥ yamaḥ ca mṛtyuḥ ca yamasya anucarāḥ ca ye bahula tvāt ca na uktāḥ ye vividhāḥ devatā gaṇāḥ te devasya abhiṣeka artham samāyānti tatas tatas gṛhītvā te tadā viprāḥ sarve devāḥ divaukasaḥ ābhiṣecanikam dravyam maṅgalāni ca sarvaśas divya saṃbhāra saṃyuktaiḥ kalaśaiḥ kāñcanaiḥ dvijāḥ sārasvatībhiḥ puṇyābhiḥ divya toyābhiḥ eva ca toyena ākāśagaṅgāyāḥ kṛṣṇam rāmeṇa saṃgatam sa puṣpaiḥ kāñcanaiḥ kumbhaiḥ snāpayanti avani sthitāḥ saṃcaranti vimānāni devānām ambare tathā uccāvacāni divyāni kāmagāni sthirāṇi ca gītaiḥ vādyaiḥ patākābhiḥ śobhitāni samantataḥ evam tadā muni śreṣṭhāḥ kṛṣṇam rāmeṇa saṃgatam snāpayitvā subhadrām ca saṃstuvanti mudā anvitāḥ jaya kṛṣṇa jagannātha jaya saṃkarṣaṇa anuja jaya padma palāśa akṣa jaya vāñchā phala prada evam stutvā tadā devāḥ śakra ādyāḥ hṛṣṭa mānasāḥ siddha cāraṇa saṃghāḥ ca ye ca anye svarga vāsinaḥ munayaḥ vālakhilyāḥ ca kṛṣṇam rāmeṇa saṃgatam subhadrām ca muni śreṣṭhāḥ praṇipatya ambare sthitāḥ dṛṣṭvā stutvā namaskṛtvā tadā te tridivaukasaḥ kṛṣṇam rāmam subhadrām ca yānti svam svam niveśanam saṃcaranti vimānāni devānām ambare tadā uccāvacāni divyāni kāmagāni sthirāṇi ca gītaiḥ vādyaiḥ patākābhiḥ śobhitāni samantataḥ dṛṣṭvā nirāmayam sthānam yānti na asti atra saṃśayaḥ kapilā śata dānena yat phalam puṣkare smṛtam tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham sahalāyudham subhadrām ca muni śreṣṭhāḥ prāpnoti śubha kṛt naraḥ kanyā śata pradānena yat phalam samudāhṛtam tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ suvarṇa śata niṣkāṇām dānena yat phalam smṛtam tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ vṛṣotsargeṇa vidhivat yat phalam samudāhṛtam tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ gaja aśva ratha dānena yat phalam samudāhṛtam tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ suvarṇaśṛṅgī dānena yat phalam samudāhṛtam tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ dānena ghṛtadhenvāḥ ca phalam yat samudāhṛtam tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ cāndrāyaṇena cīrṇena yat phalam samudāhṛtam tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham labhate naraḥ tat phalam kṛṣṇam ālokya mañca stham sa halāyudham subhadrām ca muni śreṣṭhāḥ prāpnoti śubha kṛt naraḥ tasmāt naraḥ athavā nārī paśyet tam puruṣottamam tatas samasta tīrthānām labhet snāna ādikam phalam snāna śeṣeṇa kṛṣṇasya toyena ātmā abhiṣicyate vandhyā mṛta prajā yā tu durbhagā graha pīḍitā rākṣasa ādyaiḥ gṛhītāḥ vā tathā rogaiḥ ca saṃhatāḥ sadyas tāḥ snāna śeṣeṇa udakena abhiṣecitāḥ prāpnuvanti īpsitān kāmān yān yān vāñchanti ca īpsitān putra arthinī labhet putrān saubhāgyam ca sukha arthinī roga ārtā mucyate rogāt dhanam ca dhana kāṅkṣiṇī puṇyāni yāni toyāni tiṣṭhanti dharaṇī tale tāni snāna avaśeṣasya kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśīm tasmāt snāna avaśeṣam yat kṛṣṇasya salilam dvijāḥ tena abhiṣiñcet gātrāṇi sarva kāma pradam hi tat snātam paśyanti ye kṛṣṇam vrajantam dakṣiṇā mukham śāstreṣu yat phalam proktam pṛthiv yaḥ tri pradakṣiṇaiḥ dṛṣṭvā naraḥ labhet kṛṣṇam vrajantam dakṣiṇāmukham tīrtha yātrā phalam yat tu pṛthivyām samudāhṛtam dṛṣṭvā naraḥ labhet kṛṣṇam tat phalam dakṣiṇāmukham badaryām yat phalam proktam dṛṣṭvā nārāyaṇam naram dṛṣṭvā naraḥ labhet kṛṣṇam tat phalam dakṣiṇāmukham gaṅgādvāre kurukṣetre snāna dānena yat phalam dṛṣṭvā naraḥ labhet kṛṣṇam tat phalam dakṣiṇāmukham prayāge ca mahā māghyām yat phalam samudāhṛtam dṛṣṭvā naraḥ labhet kṛṣṇam tat phalam dakṣiṇāmukham śālagrāme mahācaitryām snāna dānena yat phalam dṛṣṭvā naraḥ labhet kṛṣṇam tat phalam dakṣiṇāmukham mahā abhidhāna kārttikyām puṣkare yat phalam smṛtam dṛṣṭvā naraḥ labhet kṛṣṇam tat phalam dakṣiṇāmukham yat phalam snāna dānena gaṅgā sāgara saṃgame dṛṣṭvā naraḥ labhet kṛṣṇam tat phalam dakṣiṇāmukham dṛṣṭvā naraḥ labhet kṛṣṇam tat phalam dakṣiṇāmukham gaṅgāyām sarva tīrtheṣu yāmuneṣu ca bho dvijāḥ sārasvateṣu tīrtheṣu tathā anyeṣu saraḥsu ca dṛṣṭvā naraḥ labhet kṛṣṇam tat phalam dakṣiṇāmukham puṣkare ca atha tīrtheṣu gaye ca amarakaṇṭake naimiṣa ādiṣu tīrtheṣu kṣetreṣu āyataneṣu ca dṛṣṭvā naraḥ labhet kṛṣṇam tat phalam dakṣiṇāmukham yat kiṃcid kathitam ca atra phalam puṇyasya karmaṇaḥ veda śāstre purāṇe ca bhārate ca dvijottamāḥ dharma śāstreṣu sarveṣu tathā anyatra manīṣibhiḥ dṛṣṭvā naraḥ labhet kṛṣṇam tat phalam sa halāyudham sakalam bhadrayā sārdham vrajantam dakṣiṇāmukham yāntam ye paśyanti rathe sthitam kṛṣṇam balam subhadrām ca te yānti bhavanam hareḥ ye paśyanti tadā kṛṣṇam sapta aham maṇḍape sthitam halinam ca subhadrām ca viṣṇu lokam vrajanti te munayaḥ ūcuḥ kena sā nirmitā yātrā dakṣiṇasyām jagatpate yātrā phalam ca kim tatra prāpyate brūhi mānavaiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ saṃkarṣaṇaḥ ca eva subhadrā ca rathena te śrī bhagavān uvāca guḍivā nāma yātrā me sarva kāma phala pradā ye mām tatra arcayiṣyanti śraddhayā maṇḍape sthitam saṃkarṣaṇam subhadrām ca vidhivat su samāhitāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ striyaḥ śūdrāḥ ca vai nṛpa upahāraiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ praṇipātaiḥ pradakṣiṇaiḥ na teṣām durlabham kiṃcid phalam yasya yat īpsitam bhaviṣyati nṛpa śreṣṭha mad prasādāt asaṃśayam sa tu rāja varaḥ śrīmān kṛtakṛtyaḥ abhavat tadā tasmāt sarva prayatnena guḍivāyām dvijottamāḥ āyuḥ kīrtim yaśaḥ medhām balam vidyām dhṛtim paśūn yān yān samīhate bhogān dṛṣṭvā tam puruṣottamam naraḥ vā api athavā nārī tān tān prāpnoti asaṃśayam yātrām kṛtvā guḍivā ākhyām vidhivat su samāhitaḥ āṣāḍhasya site pakṣe naraḥ yoṣit atha api vā dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam ca rāmam ca subhadrām ca dvijottamāḥ daśa pañca aśvamedhānām phalam prāpnoti ca adhikam sapta avarān sapta parān vaṃśān uddhṛtya ca ātmanaḥ rūpavān subhagaḥ śūraḥ naraḥ viṣṇu puram vrajet tatra bhuktvā varān bhogān yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam sarva kāma samṛddha ātmā jarā maraṇa varjitaḥ vaiṣṇavam yogam āsthāya tatas mokṣam avāpnuyāt munayaḥ ūcuḥ ekaikasyāḥ tu yātrāyāḥ phalam brūhi pṛthak pṛthak yat prāpnoti naraḥ kṛtvā nārī vā tatra saṃyatā pratiyātrā phalam viprāḥ śṛṇudhvam gadataḥ mama yat prāpnoti naraḥ kṛtvā tasmin kṣetre su saṃyataḥ guḍivāyām tathā utthāne phālgunyām viṣuve tathā yātrām kṛtvā vidhānena dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam praṇamya ca naraḥ gacchet viṣṇu loke yāvat indrāḥ caturdaśa yāvat yātrām jyeṣṭha māse karoti vidhivat naraḥ tāvat kalpam viṣṇu loke sukham bhuṅkte na saṃśayaḥ jyeṣṭhe yātrām naraḥ kṛtvā nārī vā saṃyata indriyaḥ pratiṣṭhām kurute yaḥ tu śāṭhya dambha vivarjitaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ śrotum icchāmahe deva pratiṣṭhām vadataḥ tava vidhānam ca arcanam dānam phalam tatra jagatpateḥ śṛṇudhvam muni śārdūlāḥ pratiṣṭhām vidhi coditām yām kṛtvā tu naraḥ bhaktyā nārī vā labhate phalam yātrā dvādaśa saṃpūrṇā yadā syāt tu dvijottamāḥ tadā kurvīta vidhivat pratiṣṭhām pāpa nāśinīm jyeṣṭhe māsi site pakṣe tu ekādaśyām samāhitaḥ gatvā jalāśayam puṇyam ācamya prayataḥ śuciḥ āvāhya sarva tīrthāni dhyātvā nārāyaṇam tathā tatas snānam prakurvīta vidhivat su samāhitaḥ yasya yaḥ vidhiḥ uddiṣṭaḥ ṛṣibhiḥ snāna karmaṇi snātvā samyak vidhānena tatas devān ṛṣīn pitṝn saṃtarpayet tathā anyān ca nāma gotra vidhāna vid upaspṛśya vidhānena bhāskara abhimukhaḥ tatas gāyatrīm pāvanīm devīm manasā vedamātaram sarva pāpa harām puṇyām japet aṣṭa uttaram śatam puṇyān ca saura mantrān ca śraddhayā su samāhitaḥ tris pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya bhāskaram praṇamet tatas veda uktam triṣu varṇeṣu snānam jāpyam udāhṛtam strī śūdrayoḥ snāna jāpyam veda ukta vidhi varjitam ghṛtena snāpayet devam kṣīreṇa tad anantaram tatas vastra yugam śreṣṭham bhaktyā tam paridhāpayet anyaiḥ ca vaiṣṇavaiḥ puṣpaiḥ arcayet mallikā ādibhiḥ dhūpam ca aguru saṃyuktam dahet devasya ca agratas dīpam prajvālayet bhaktyā yathāśaktyā ghṛtena vai anyān ca dīpakān dadyāt dvādaśa eva samāhitaḥ ghṛtena ca muni śreṣṭhāḥ tila tailena vā punar naivedye pāyasa apūpa śaṣkulī vaṭakam tathā modakam phāṇitam vā alpam phalāni ca nivedayet evam pañca upacāreṇa saṃpūjya puruṣottamam namaḥ puruṣottamāya iti japet aṣṭa uttaram śatam saṃsāra sāgare magnam trāhi mām puruṣottama yāḥ te mayā kṛtāḥ yātrāḥ dvādaśā eva jagatpate prasādāt tava govinda saṃpūrṇāḥ tāḥ bhavantu me evam prasādya tam devam daṇḍa vat praṇipatya ca nānā puṣpaiḥ muni śreṣṭhāḥ vicitram puṣpa maṇḍapam kṛtvā avadhāraṇam paścāt jāgaram kārayet niśi kathām ca vāsudevasya gītikām ca api kārayet dhyāyan paṭhan stuvan devam praṇayet rajanīm budhaḥ tatas prabhāte vimale dvādaśyām dvādaśa eva tu nimantrayet vrata snātān brāhmaṇān vedapāragān itihāsa purāṇa jñān śrotriyān saṃyata indriyān upacāraiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ praṇipātaiḥ pradakṣiṇaiḥ saṃpūjya evam jagannātham brāhmaṇān pūjayet tatas bhaktyā tu sa dhanam tebhyaḥ dadyāt vastra ādikam dvijāḥ ācāryāya tatas dadyāt go vastram kanakam tathā chattra upānah yugam ca anyat kāṃsya pātram ca bhaktitaḥ tatas tān anna tṛptān ca brāhmaṇān svastha mānasān dvādaśa eva uda kumbhān ca dadyāt tebhyaḥ sama udakān dakṣiṇām ca yathāśaktyā dadyāt tebhyaḥ vimatsaraḥ kumbham ca dakṣiṇām ca eva ācāryāya nivedayet evam saṃpūjya tān viprān gurum jñāna pradāyakam pūjayet parayā bhaktyā viṣṇu tulyam dvijottamāḥ saṃpūjya tam namaskṛtya imam mantram udīrayet an ādi nidhanaḥ devaḥ prīyatām puruṣottamaḥ iti uccārya tatas viprān tris kṛtvā ca pradakṣiṇām praṇamya śirasā bhaktyā ācāryam tu visarjayet tatas tān brāhmaṇān bhaktyā ca āsīmāntam anuvrajet anyaiḥ ca upāsakaiḥ dīnaiḥ bhikṣukaiḥ ca anna kāṅkṣibhiḥ evam kṛtvā naraḥ samyak nārī vā labhate phalam aśvamedha sahasrāṇām rājasūya śatasya ca atītam śatam ādāya puruṣāṇām nara uttamāḥ bhaviṣyam ca śatam viprāḥ svargatyāḥ divya rūpadhṛk sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpannaḥ sarva alaṃkāra bhūṣitaḥ rūpa yauvana saṃpannaḥ guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ alaṃkṛtaḥ stūyamānaḥ apsarobhiḥ ca gandharvaiḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ udyotayan diśaḥ sarvāḥ ākāśe vigata klamaḥ yuvā mahā balaḥ dhīmān viṣṇu lokam sa gacchati yathā devaḥ jagannāthaḥ śaṅkha cakra gadā dharaḥ tathā asau muditaḥ viprāḥ kṛtvā rūpam catur bhujam bhuktvā tatra varān bhogān krīḍām kṛtvā suraiḥ saha siddha vidyādharaiḥ ca api śobhitam sura kiṃnaraiḥ aneka śata sāhasraiḥ vimānaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam aśīti kalpa kālam tu tatra bhuktvā sukham naraḥ ṣaṣṭi kalpān sukham tatra bhuktvā nānāvidham mudā guhyaka apsarasaiḥ sādhyaiḥ vṛtaiḥ ca anyaiḥ sura uttamaiḥ āgatya tatra pañcāśat kalpān bhuktvā sukham naraḥ sura lokam tatas gatvā vimānaiḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ catvāriṃśat tu kalpān tu bhuktvā bhogān su durlabhān tatas bhogān varān bhuṅkte triṃśat kalpān yathā īpsitān tasmāt āgacchate lokam śaśāṅkasya dvijottamāḥ yatra asau tiṣṭhate somaḥ sarvaiḥ devaiḥ alaṃkṛtaḥ nānā āścarya mayam puṇyam gandharva apsaraḥ sevitam tatra bhuktvā śubhān bhogān daśa kalpān dvijottamāḥ tasmāt āyāti bhuvanam gandharvāṇām su durlabham bhuktvā ca āyāti medinyām rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ cakravartī mahā vīryaḥ guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ alaṃkṛtaḥ kṛtvā rājyam svadharmeṇa yajñaiḥ iṣṭvā su dakṣiṇaiḥ tad ante yoginām lokam gatvā mokṣa pradam śivam tatra bhuktvā varān bhogān yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam tasmāt āgacchate ca atra jāyate yoginām kule catur vedī vipra varaḥ yajñaiḥ iṣṭvā āpta dakṣiṇaiḥ vaiṣṇavam yogam āsthāya tatas mokṣam avāpnuyāt evam yātrā phalam viprāḥ mayā samyak udāhṛtam munayaḥ ūcuḥ pramāṇam tasya lokasya bhogam kāntim balam prabho karmaṇā kena gacchanti tatra dharma parāyaṇāḥ darśanāt sparśanāt vā api tīrtha snāna ādinā api vā śṛṇudhvam munayaḥ sarve yat param paramam padam bhaktānām īhitam dhanyam puṇyam saṃsāra nāśanam pravaram sarva lokānām viṣṇu ākhyam vadataḥ mama sarva āścarya mayam puṇyam sthānam trailokya pūjitam aśokaiḥ pārijātaiḥ ca mandāraiḥ campaka drumaiḥ pāṭalā cūta khadiraiḥ karṇikāra vana ujjvalaiḥ kapitthaiḥ nārikeraiḥ ca tālaiḥ śrīphala saṃbhavaiḥ saralaiḥ candanaiḥ nīpaiḥ devadāru śubhāñjanaiḥ jātī lavaṅga kaṅkolaiḥ karpūra āmoda vāsibhiḥ nānā jalāśayaiḥ puṇyaiḥ nānā pakṣi rutaiḥ varaiḥ dīrghikā śata saṃghātaiḥ toya pūrṇaiḥ manoharaiḥ rakta nīlotpalaiḥ kāntaiḥ kahlāraiḥ ca sugandhibhiḥ anyaiḥ ca jala jaiḥ puṣpaiḥ nānā varṇaiḥ su śobhanaiḥ haṃsa kāraṇḍava ākīrṇaiḥ cakravāka upaśobhitaiḥ koyaṣṭikaiḥ ca dātyūhaiḥ kāraṇḍava ravākulaiḥ cātakaiḥ priyaputraiḥ ca jīvaṃjīvaka jātibhiḥ evam nānāvidhaiḥ divyaiḥ nānā āścarya samanvitaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ jalāśayaiḥ puṇyaiḥ bhūṣitam su manoharaiḥ tatra divyaiḥ vimānaiḥ ca nānā ratna vibhūṣitaiḥ kāmagaiḥ kāñcanaiḥ śubhraiḥ divya gandharva nāditaiḥ taruṇa āditya saṃkāśaiḥ apsarobhiḥ alaṃkṛtaiḥ khecaraiḥ sa patākaiḥ ca muktā hāra avalambibhiḥ nānā varṇaiḥ asaṃkhyātaiḥ jātarūpa paricchadaiḥ nānā kusuma gandha āḍhyaiḥ candana aguru bhūṣitaiḥ manaḥ māruta tulyaiḥ ca kiṅkiṇī stabaka ākulaiḥ nānā aṅganābhiḥ satatam gandharva apsaras ādibhiḥ candra ānanābhiḥ kāntābhiḥ yoṣidbhiḥ su manoharaiḥ pīna unnata kuca agrābhiḥ sumadhyābhiḥ samantataḥ śyāma avadāta varṇābhiḥ matta mātaṅga gāmibhiḥ parivārya nara śreṣṭham vījayanti sma tāḥ striyaḥ cāmaraiḥ rukma daṇḍaiḥ ca nānā ratna vibhūṣitaiḥ gīta nṛtyaiḥ tathā vādyaiḥ modamānaiḥ mada alasaiḥ sura saṃghaiḥ ca ṛṣibhiḥ śuśubhe bhuvana uttamam tatra prāpya mahā bhogān prāpnuvanti manīṣiṇaḥ vaṭarāja samīpe tu dakṣiṇasya udadheḥ taṭe dṛṣṭaḥ yaiḥ bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ puṣkarākṣaḥ jagatpatiḥ krīḍanti apsarasaiḥ sārdham yāvat dyauḥ candra tārakam pratapta hema saṃkāśāḥ jarā maraṇa varjitāḥ sarva duḥkha vihīnāḥ ca tṛṣṇā glāni vivarjitāḥ catur bhujāḥ mahā vīryāḥ vanamālā vibhūṣitāḥ śrīvatsa lāñchanaiḥ yuktāḥ śaṅkha cakra gadā dharāḥ kecid nīlotpala śyāmāḥ kecid kāñcana saṃnibhāḥ śyāma varṇāḥ kuṇḍalinaḥ tathā anye vajra saṃnibhāḥ na tādṛś sarva devānām bhānti lokāḥ dvijottamāḥ yādṛś bhāti hareḥ lokaḥ sarva āścarya samanvitaḥ na tatra punarāvṛttiḥ gamanāt jāyate dvijāḥ kṛṣṇam rāmam subhadrām ca paśyanti puruṣottame pratapta hema saṃkāśam taruṇa āditya saṃnibham aneka śata sāhasraiḥ patākaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam yojana ayuta vistīrṇam hema prākāra veṣṭitam vibhāti śāradaḥ yadvat nakṣatraiḥ saha candramāḥ catur dvāram su vistīrṇam kañcukibhiḥ su rakṣitam indranīlam tṛtīyam tu mahānīlam tatas param puram tu pañcamam dīptam padmarāga mayam puram ṣaṣṭham vajra mayam viprāḥ vaidūryam saptamam puram nānā ratna mayaiḥ hema pravāla aṅkura bhūṣitaiḥ dṛśyante tatra siddhāḥ ca bhāsayanti diśaḥ daśa paurṇamāsyām sa nakṣatraḥ yathā bhāti niśākaraḥ ārūḍhaḥ tatra bhagavān salakṣmīkaḥ janārdanaḥ pīta ambara dharaḥ śyāmaḥ śrīvatsa lakṣma saṃyutaḥ ādāya tam muni śreṣṭhāḥ savya hastena keśavaḥ yasya śabdena sakalam saṃkṣobham jāyate jagat viśrutam pāñcajanya iti sahasra āvarta bhūṣitam duṣkṛta anta karīm raudrām daitya dānava nāśinīm jvalat vahni śikhā ākārām duḥsahām tridaśaiḥ api kaumodakīm gadām ca asau dhṛtavān dakṣiṇe kare śaraiḥ āditya saṃkāśaiḥ jvālā mālā ākulaiḥ varaiḥ sarva ānanda karaḥ śrīmān sarva śāstra viśāradaḥ sahasramūrdhā deveśaḥ sahasra caraṇa īkṣaṇaḥ sahasra ākhyaḥ sahasra aṅgaḥ sahasra bhujavān prabhuḥ siṃhāsana gataḥ devaḥ padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇaḥ vidyut vispaṣṭa saṃkāśaḥ jagannāthaḥ jagadguruḥ parītaḥ sura siddhaiḥ ca gandharva apsarasām gaṇaiḥ yakṣa vidyādharaiḥ nāgaiḥ muni siddhaiḥ sa cāraṇaiḥ tatrasthā satatam kīrtiḥ prajñā medhā sarasvatī gāyatrī ca eva sāvitrī maṅgalā sarva maṅgalā prabhā matiḥ tathā kāntiḥ tatra nārāyaṇī sthitā śraddhā ca kauśikī devī vidyut saudāminī tathā nidrā rātriḥ tathā māyā tathā anya amara yoṣitaḥ vāsudevasya sarvāḥ tāḥ bhavane saṃpratiṣṭhitāḥ ghṛtācī menakā rambhā sahajanyī tilottamā urvaśī ca eva nimlocā tathā anyā vāmanā parā mandodarī ca subhagā viśvācī vipula ānanā bhadrāṅgī citrasenā ca pramlocā sumanoharā muni saṃmohinī rāmā candra madhyā śubha ānanā sukeśī nīlakeśā ca tathā manmathadīpinī alambuṣā miśrakeśī tathā anyā muñjikasthalā kratusthalā varāṅgī ca pūrvacittiḥ tathā parā parāvatī mahārūpā śaśi lekhā śubha ānanā haṃsa līlā anugāminyaḥ matta vāraṇa gāminī bimbauṣṭhī navagarbhā ca vikhyātāḥ sura yoṣitaḥ etāḥ ca anyāḥ apsarasaḥ rūpa yauvana garvitāḥ su madhyāḥ cāru vadanāḥ sarva alaṃkāra bhūṣitāḥ gīta mādhurya saṃyuktāḥ sarva lakṣaṇa saṃyutāḥ gīta vādye ca kuśalāḥ sura gandharva yoṣitaḥ na kṣudh pipāsā na jarā na vairūpyam na ca asukham viṣṇu lokāt param lokam na atra paśyāmi bho dvijāḥ ye lokāḥ svarga loke tu śrūyante puṇya karmaṇām viṣṇu lokasya te viprāḥ kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśīm evam hareḥ pura sthānam sarva bhoga guṇa anvitam sarva saukhya karam puṇyam sarva āścarya mayam dvijāḥ na tatra nāstikāḥ yānti puruṣāḥ viṣaya ātmakāḥ na kṛtaghnāḥ na piśunāḥ no stenāḥ na ajita indriyāḥ te tatra vaiṣṇavāḥ yānti viṣṇu lokam na saṃśayaḥ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam ca rāmam ca subhadrām ca dvijottamāḥ te api tatra narāḥ yānti ye mṛtāḥ puruṣottame te api tatra param sthānam yānti na asti atra saṃśayaḥ evam mayā muni śreṣṭhāḥ viṣṇu lokaḥ sanātanaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ tyaktvā yatra naraḥ deham yāti sālokya tām hareḥ yatra sva deha saṃtyāgāt viṣṇu lokam vrajet naraḥ narāṇām upakārāya puruṣa ākhye na saṃśayaḥ anāyāsena deveśa deham tyaktvā nara uttamāḥ tasmin kṣetre param viṣṇoḥ padam yānti nirāmayam śrutvā kṣetrasya māhātmyam vismayaḥ naḥ mahān abhūt prayāga puṣkara ādīni kṣetrāṇi āyatanāni ca pṛthivyām sarva tīrthāni saritaḥ ca sarāṃsi ca na tathā tāni sarvāṇi praśaṃsasi sura uttama yathā praśaṃsasi kṣetram puruṣa ākhyam punar punar jñātaḥ asmābhiḥ abhiprāyaḥ tava idānīm pitāmaha puruṣa ākhya samam nūnam kṣetram nā asti mahī tale tena tvam vibudha śreṣṭha praśaṃsasi punar punar satyam satyam muni śreṣṭhāḥ bhavadbhiḥ samudāhṛtam puruṣa ākhya samam kṣetram na asti atra pṛthivī tale santi yāni tu tīrthāni puṇyāni āyatanāni ca tāni śrīpuruṣa ākhyasya kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśīm tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam ādityānām yathā viṣṇuḥ śreṣṭha tve samudāhṛtaḥ tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam nakṣatrāṇām yathā somaḥ sarasām sāgaraḥ yathā tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam vasūnām pāvakaḥ yadvat rudrāṇām śaṃkaraḥ yathā tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam varṇānām brāhmaṇaḥ yadvat vainateyaḥ ca pakṣiṇām tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam śikhariṇām yathā meruḥ parvatānām himālayaḥ tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam pramadānām yathā lakṣmīḥ saritām jāhnavī yathā tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam airāvataḥ gaja indrāṇām mahā ṛṣīṇām bhṛguḥ yathā tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam senā nīnām yathā skandaḥ siddhānām kapilaḥ yathā tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam uccaiḥśravāḥ yathā aśvānām kavīnām uśanā kaviḥ tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam munīnām ca yathā vyāsaḥ kuberaḥ yakṣa rakṣasām tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam indriyāṇām manaḥ yadvat bhūtānām avanī yathā tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam aśvatthaḥ sarva vṛkṣāṇām pavanaḥ plavatām yathā tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam bhūṣaṇānām tu sarveṣām yathā cūḍāmaṇiḥ dvijāḥ tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam gandharvāṇām citra rathaḥ śastrāṇām kuliśaḥ yathā tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam akāraḥ sarva varṇānām gāyatrī chandasām yathā tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam sarva aṅgebhyaḥ yathā śreṣṭham uttamāṅgam dvijottamāḥ tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam arundhatī yathā strīṇām satīnām śreṣṭha tām gatā tathā samasta tīrthānām śreṣṭham tat puruṣottamam yathā samasta vidyānām mokṣa vidyā parā smṛtā tathā samasta tīrthānām śreṣṭham tat puruṣottamam manuṣyāṇām yathā rājā dhenūnām api kāmadhuk tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham puruṣottamam suvarṇam sarva ratnānām sarpāṇām vāsukiḥ yathā tathā samasta tīrthānām variṣṭham
