durlabhān bhogān nānāvidhān viprāḥ ṛk dvi aṣṭaka samanvitān manvantarāṇām tatra eva bhuktvā kālam ca saptatim bhogān uccāvacān divyān manasaḥ prīti vardhanān bhuktvā tatra īpsitān bhogān sarva kāma guṇa anvitān tasmāt paitāmaham lokam yānti te vaiṣṇavāḥ dvijāḥ manvantarāṇām navati krīḍitvā tatra vai sukham iha āgatya punar tasmāt viprāṇām pravare kule jāyante yoginaḥ viprāḥ veda śāstra artha pāragāḥ saṃbhave saṃbhave te tu śata varṣam dvijottamāḥ bhuktvā yathā īpsitān bhogān yānti loka antaram tatas daśa janma yadā teṣām krameṇa evam prapūryate gatvā tatra akṣayān bhogān bhuktvā sarva guṇa anvitān manvantara śatam yāvat janma mṛtyu vivarjitāḥ gacchanti bhuvanam paścāt vārāhasya dvijottamāḥ divya dehāḥ kuṇḍalinaḥ mahā kāyāḥ mahā balāḥ krīḍanti tatra vipra indrāḥ kṛtvā rūpam catur bhujam daśa koṭi sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām dvijasattamāḥ tiṣṭhanti śāśvate bhāve sarvaiḥ devaiḥ namaskṛtāḥ tatas yānti tu te dhīrāḥ narasiṃha gṛham dvijāḥ krīḍante tatra muditāḥ varṣa koṭi ayutāni ca krīḍante tatra saukhyena varṣāṇām ayutāni ca tatra sthitvā ciram kālam varṣa koṭi śatān bahūn nārāyaṇa puram yānti tatas te sādhaka īśvarāḥ bhuktvā bhogān ca vividhān varṣa koṭi arbudāni ca aniruddhapuram paścāt divya rūpāḥ mahā balāḥ gacchanti sādhaka varāḥ stūyamānāḥ sura asuraiḥ tatra koṭi sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām ca caturdaśa tiṣṭhanti vaiṣṇavāḥ tatra jarā maraṇa varjitāḥ tatra tiṣṭhanti te viprāḥ lakṣa koṭi śata trayam svacchanda gāminaḥ hṛṣṭāḥ bala śakti samanvitāḥ gacchanti yoginaḥ paścāt yatra saṃkarṣaṇaḥ prabhuḥ tatra uṣitvā ciram kālam bhuktvā bhogān sahasraśas evam krameṇa bhuktim te prāpnuvanti manīṣiṇaḥ muktim ca muni śārdūlāḥ vāsudeva arcane ratāḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca ekādaśyām ubhe pakṣe nirāhāraḥ samāhitaḥ saṃpūjya vidhivat viṣṇum śraddhayā su samāhitaḥ daṇḍa vat praṇipātaiḥ ca jaya śabdaiḥ tathā uttamaiḥ evam saṃpūjya vidhivat rātrau kṛtvā prajāgaram kathām vā gītikām viṣṇoḥ gāyan viṣṇu parāyaṇaḥ yāti viṣṇoḥ param sthānam naraḥ na asti atra saṃśayaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ prajāgare gītikāyāḥ phalam viṣṇoḥ mahā mune brūhi tat śrotum icchāmaḥ param kautūhalam hi naḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca śṛṇudhvam muni śārdūlāḥ pravakṣyāmi anupūrvaśas gītikāyāḥ phalam viṣṇoḥ jāgare yat udāhṛtam avantī nāma nagarī babhūva bhuvi viśrutā tatra āste bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śaṅkha cakra gadā dharaḥ tasyāḥ nagaryāḥ paryante cāṇḍālaḥ gīti kovidaḥ sat vṛttyā utpādita dhanaḥ bhṛtyānām bharaṇe rataḥ viṣṇu bhaktaḥ sa cāṇḍālaḥ māsi māsi dṛḍha vrataḥ ekādaśyām samāgamya sa upavāsaḥ atha gāyati gītikāḥ viṣṇu nāma aṅkāḥ prādurbhāva samāśritāḥ gāndhāra ṣaḍja naiṣāda svara pañcama dhaivataiḥ rātri jāgaraṇe viṣṇum gāthābhiḥ upagāyati prabhāte ca praṇamya īśam dvādaśyām gṛham etya ca jāmātṛ bhāgineyān ca bhojayitvā sa kanyakāḥ tatas sa parivāraḥ tu paścāt bhuṅkte dvijottamāḥ evam tasya āsataḥ tatra kurvataḥ viṣṇu prīṇanam ekadā caitra māse tu kṛṣṇa ekādaśi gocare viṣṇu śuśrūṣaṇa arthāya yayau vanam anuttamam vana jātāni puṣpāṇi grahītum bhakti tatparaḥ kṣiprā taṭe mahā araṇye vibhītaka taroḥ adhas dṛṣṭaḥ sa rākṣasena atha gṛhītaḥ ca api bhakṣitum cāṇḍālaḥ tam atha uvāca na adya bhakṣyaḥ tvayā hi aham prātar bhokṣyasi kalyāṇa satyam eṣyāmi aham punar adya kāryam mama mahat tasmāt muñcasva rākṣasa śvas satyena sameṣyāmi tatas khādasi mām iti viṣṇu śuśrūṣaṇa arthāya rātrijāgaraṇam mayā vyāsaḥ uvāca tam rākṣasaḥ pratyuvāca daśa rātram abhojanam na mokṣye bhakṣayiṣyāmi kṣudhayā pīḍitaḥ bhṛśam niśācara vacaḥ śrutvā mātaṅgaḥ tam uvāca ha sāntvayan ślakṣṇayā vācā sa satya vacanaiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ mātaṅgaḥ uvāca satya mūlam jagat sarvam brahmarākṣasa tat śṛṇu satyena aham śapiṣyāmi punarāgamanāya ca ādityaḥ candramāḥ vahniḥ vāyuḥ bhūḥ dyauḥ jalam manaḥ para dāreṣu yat pāpam yat para dravya hāriṣu vandhyā pateḥ ca yat pāpam yat pāpam vṛṣalī pateḥ yat ca devalake pāpam matsya māṃsa āśinaḥ ca yat kroḍa māṃsa āśinaḥ yat ca kūrma māṃsa āśinaḥ ca yat vṛthā māṃsa āśinaḥ yat ca pṛṣṭha māṃsa āśinaḥ ca yat kṛtaghne mitra ghātake yat pāpam didhiṣū patau sūtakasya ca yat pāpam yat pāpam krūra karmaṇaḥ amāvāsyā aṣṭamī ṣaṣṭhī kṛṣṇa śukla caturdaśī rajasvalām tathā paścāt śrāddham kṛtvā striyam vrajet mitra bhāryām gacchatām ca yat pāpam piśunasya ca dambha māyā anurakte ca yat pāpam madhu ghātinaḥ yat ca kanyā anṛte pāpam yat ca gośvatara anṛte strī bāla hantuḥ yat pāpam yat ca mithyā abhibhāṣiṇaḥ yat ca nindayatām pāpam guru mithyā apacārataḥ tayoḥ dātṛ grahītroḥ ca yat pāpam bhrūṇa ghātinaḥ kim ca atra bahubhiḥ proktaiḥ śapathaiḥ tava rākṣasa śrūyatām śapatham bhīmam durvācyam api kathyate sva kanyā jīvinaḥ pāpam gūḍha satyena sākṣiṇaḥ a yājya yājake ṣaṇḍhe yat pāpam śravaṇe adhame vyāsaḥ uvāca mātaṅga vacanam śrutvā vismitaḥ brahmarākṣasaḥ iti uktaḥ kuṇa pāśena śvapākaḥ kusumāni tu samādāya agamat ca eva viṣṇoḥ sa nilayam gataḥ tāni prādāt brāhmaṇāya saḥ api prakṣālya ca ambhasā viṣṇum abhyarcya nilayam jagāma sa tapodhanāḥ saḥ api mātaṅga dāyādaḥ sa upavāsaḥ tu tām niśām gāyan hi bāhya bhūmiṣṭhaḥ prajāgaram upākarot prabhātāyām tu śarvaryām snātvā devam namasya ca dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām śarīram sādhanam yatas mahatā tu prayatnena śarīram pālayet budhaḥ mātaṅgaḥ tat vacaḥ śrutvā pratyuvāca atha hetumat mātaṅgaḥ uvāca bhadra satyam puraskṛtya gacchāmi śapathāḥ kṛtāḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca tam bhūyas pratyuvāca atha kim evam mūḍha dhīḥ bhavān kim na śrutam tvayā sādho manunā yat udīritam go strī dvijānām parirakṣaṇa artham prāṇa atyaye sarva dhana apahāre pañca anṛtāni āhuḥ a pātakāni dharma vākyam na ca strīṣu na vivāhe tathā ripau vañcane ca artha hānau ca sva nāśe anṛtake tathā evam tat vākyam ākarṇya mātaṅgaḥ pratyuvāca ha mātaṅgaḥ uvāca satyena arkaḥ pratapati satyena apaḥ rasa ātmikāḥ dharma artha kāma saṃprāptiḥ mokṣa prāptiḥ ca durlabhā satyena jāyate puṃsām tasmāt satyam na saṃtyajet satyam svarga samāyātam tasmāt satyam na saṃtyajet vyāsaḥ uvāca jagāma tatra yatra āste prāṇi hā brahma rākṣasaḥ tam āgatam samīkṣya asau cāṇḍālam brahmarākṣasaḥ brahmarākṣasaḥ uvāca sādhu sādhu mahābhāga satya vākya anupālaka karmaṇā anena manye tvām brāhmaṇam śucim avyayam kim tatra bhavatā rātrau kṛtam viṣṇu gṛhe vada vyāsaḥ uvāca tam abhyuvāca mātaṅgaḥ śṛṇu viṣṇu gṛhe mayā yat kṛtam rajanī bhāge yathātathyam vadāmi te viṣṇoḥ devakulasya adhas sthitena ānamra mūrtinā prajāgaraḥ kṛtaḥ rātrau gāyatā viṣṇugītikām tam brahma rākṣasaḥ prāha kiyantam kālam ucyatām prajāgaraḥ viṣṇu gṛhe kṛtam bhaktimatā vada tam abhyuvāca prahasan viṃśati abdāni rākṣasa ekādaśyām māsi māsi kṛtaḥ tatra prajāgaraḥ mātaṅga vacanam śrutvā provāca brahmarākṣasaḥ brahmarākṣasaḥ uvāca evam tvām mokṣayiṣyāmi mokṣayiṣyāmi na anyathā vyāsaḥ uvāca mātaṅgaḥ tam uvāca atha mayā ātmā te niśācara tam āha rākṣasaḥ bhūyas yāma dvaya prajāgaram mātaṅgaḥ rākṣasam prāha kim asaṃbaddham ucyate khādasva sva icchayā mām tvam na pradāsye prajāgaram mātaṅga vacanam śrutvā prāha tam brahmarākṣasaḥ brahmarākṣasaḥ uvāca dharṣayitum pīḍayitum rakṣitam dharma karmaṇā naraka ārtasya mūḍhasya sādhavaḥ syuḥ dayā anvitāḥ tat mama tvam mahābhāga kṛpām kṛtvā prajāgaram vyāsaḥ uvāca tam punar prāha cāṇḍālaḥ na yāsyāmi nijam gṛham na ca api tava dāsyāmi kathaṃcid yāma jāgaram tam prahasya atha cāṇḍālam provāca brahmarākṣasaḥ brahmarākṣasaḥ uvāca rātri avasāne yā gītā gītikā kautuka āśrayā vyāsaḥ uvāca mātaṅgaḥ uvāca kim pūrvam bhavatā karma vikṛtam kṛtam añjasā yena tvam doṣa jātena saṃbhūtaḥ brahmarākṣasaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca tasya tat vākyam ākarṇya mātaṅgam brahma rākṣasaḥ provāca duḥkha saṃtaptaḥ saṃsmṛtya sva kṛtam kṛtam brahmarākṣasaḥ uvāca śrūyatām yaḥ aham āsam vai pūrvam yat ca mayā kṛtam yasmin kṛte pāpa yonim gatavān asmi rākṣasīm somaśarmaḥ iti khyātaḥ pūrvam āsam aham dvijaḥ āgnīdhram ca akarot yajñe lobha moha prapīḍitaḥ yaṣṭum ārabdhavān asmi dvādaśa aham mahā kratum saṃpūrṇe daśa rātre tu na samāpte tathā kratau virūpākṣasya dīyantyām āhutyām rākṣase kṣaṇe mṛtaḥ aham tena doṣeṇa saṃbhūtaḥ brahmarākṣasaḥ a jānatā yajña vidyām yat iṣṭam yājitam ca yat tena karma vipākena saṃbhūtaḥ brahmarākṣasaḥ prajāgare gītikā ekām paścimām dātum arhasi vyāsaḥ uvāca tam uvāca atha cāṇḍālaḥ yadi prāṇi vadhāt bhavān nivṛttim kurute dadyām tatas paścima gītikām tasmin gīti phale datte mātaṅgam brahmarākṣasaḥ praṇamya prayayau hṛṣṭaḥ tīrtha varyam pṛthūdakam tatra anaśana saṃkalpam kṛtvā prāṇān jahau dvijāḥ rākṣasa tvāt vinirmuktaḥ gītikā phala bṛṃhitaḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi nirātaṅkaḥ avasat tatas tasya ante brāhmaṇaḥ jātaḥ babhūva smṛtimān vaśī tasya aham caritam bhūyas kathayiṣyāmi bho dvijāḥ mātaṅgasya kathā śeṣam śṛṇudhvam gadataḥ mama rākṣase tu gate dhīmān gṛham etya yata ātmavān tad vipracaritam smṛtvā nirviṇṇaḥ śuciḥ api asau putreṣu bhāryām nikṣipya dadau bhūmyāḥ pradakṣiṇām dṛṣṭvā skandam yayau dhārā cakre ca api pradakṣiṇam pāpapramocanam tīrtham āsasāda sa tu dvijāḥ snānam pāpa haram cakre sa tu cāṇḍāla vaṃśa jaḥ vimukta pāpaḥ sasmāra pūrva jātīḥ anekaśas sa pūrva janmani abhavat bhikṣuḥ saṃyata vāc manāḥ yata kāyaḥ ca matimān veda vedāṅga pāragaḥ ekadā goṣu nagarāt dhriyamāṇāsu taskaraiḥ bhikṣā avadhūtā rajasā muktā tena atha bhikṣuṇā sa tena adharma doṣeṇa cāṇḍālīm yonim āgataḥ pāpapramocane snātaḥ sa mṛtaḥ narmadā taṭe mūrkhaḥ abhūt brāhmaṇa varaḥ vārāṇasyām ca bho dvijāḥ tatra asya vasataḥ abdaiḥ tu triṃśadbhiḥ siddha pūruṣaḥ virūpa rūpī babhrāma yoga mālā bala anvitaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā sa upahāsa artham abhivādya abhyuvāca ha kuśalam siddha puruṣam kutas tu āgamyate tvayā vyāsaḥ uvāca evam saṃbhāṣitaḥ tena jñātaḥ aham iti cintya tu tam siddham prāha mūrkhaḥ asau kim tvam vetsi triviṣṭape nārāyaṇa uru prabhavām urvaśīm apsaraḥ varām siddhaḥ tam āha tām vedmi śakra cāmara dhāriṇīm svargasya ābharaṇam mukhyam urvaśīm sādhu saṃbhavām vipraḥ siddham uvāca atha ṛju mārga vivarjitaḥ tat mitra mad kṛte vārttām urvaśyāḥ bhavata ādarāt kathanīyā yat ca sā te brūyāt ākhyāsyate bhavān babhūva siddhaḥ api yayau meru pṛṣṭham surālayam sā prāha tam siddha varam na aham kāśi patim dvijam vārāṇasīm yayau siddhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ mūrkheṇa vai punar dṛṣṭaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kila bhūyas kim āha uru bhavā tava siddhaḥ abravīt na jānāmi mām uvāca urvaśī svayam siddha vākyam tatas śrutvā smita bhinna oṣṭha saṃpuṭaḥ punar prāha katham vetsi iti evam vācyā tvayā urvaśī bāḍham evam kariṣyāmi iti uktvā siddhaḥ divam gataḥ dadarśa śakra bhavanāt niṣkrāmantīm atha urvaśīm provāca tām siddha varaḥ sā ca tam siddham abravīt yena aham karmaṇā siddha tam jānāmi na ca anyathā iti uktaḥ prayayau siddhaḥ svarge dṛṣṭvā urvaśīm atha prāha asau śakaṭam bhokṣye na adya prabhṛti karhicit tam siddham urvaśī prāha jñātaḥ asau sāṃpratam mayā niyama grahaṇāt eva mūrkhaḥ mām upahāsakaḥ iti uktvā prayayau śīghram vāsam nārāyaṇa ātmajā siddhaḥ api vicacāra asau kāma cārī mahī talam urvaśī api vara ārohā gatvā vārāṇasīm purīm athā asau api mūrkhaḥ tu nadīm matsyodarīm mune jagāma atha dadarśa asau snāyamānām atha urvaśīm tām dṛṣṭvā vavṛdhe atha asya manmathaḥ kṣobha kṛt dṛḍham cakāra mūrkhaḥ ceṣṭāḥ ca tam viveda urvaśī svayam tam mūrkham siddha gaditam jñātvā sa smitam āha tam urvaśī uvāca kariṣyāmi vacaḥ tubhyam tvam viśrabdham kariṣyasi mūrkha brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca ātma pradānena mama prāṇān rakṣa śuci smite vyāsaḥ uvāca tam prāha atha urvaśī vipram niyama sthā asmi sāṃpratam tvam tiṣṭhasva kṣaṇam atha pratīkṣasva āgatam mama māsa mātreṇa sā āyātā dadarśa tam kṛśam dvijam sthitam māsam nadī tīre nirāhāram sura aṅganā tam dṛṣṭvā niścaya yutam bhūtvā vṛddha vapuḥ tatas sā cakāra nadī tīre śakaṭam śarkarā vṛtam ghṛtena madhunā ca eva nadīm matsyodarīm gatā snātvā atha bhūmau vasantī śakaṭam ca yathārthataḥ tam brāhmaṇam samāhūya vākyam āha su locanā urvaśī uvāca mayā tīvram vratam vipra cīrṇam saubhāgya kāraṇāt vrata ante niṣkṛtim dadyām pratigṛhṇīṣva bho dvija vyāsaḥ uvāca sa prāha kim idam loke dīyate śarkarā vṛtam kṣudh kṣāma kaṇṭhaḥ pṛcchāmi sādhu bhadre samīraya sā prāha śakaṭaḥ vipra śarkarā piṣṭa saṃyutaḥ imam tvam samupādāya prāṇam tarpaya mā ciram sa tat śrutvā atha saṃsmṛtya kṣudhayā pīḍitaḥ api san prāha bhadre na gṛhṇāmi niyamaḥ hi kṛtaḥ mayā sā bravīt niyamaḥ bhadra kṛtaḥ kāṣṭha maye tvayā na asau kāṣṭha mayaḥ bhuṅkṣva kṣudhayā ca atipīḍitaḥ tām brāhmaṇaḥ pratyuvāca na mayā tat viśeṣaṇam kṛtam bhadre atha niyamaḥ sāmānyena eva me kṛtaḥ tam bhūyas prāha sā tanvī na ced bhokṣyasi brāhmaṇa gṛham gṛhītvā gacchasva kuṭumbam tava bhokṣyati iha āyātā varārohā trailokye api adhikā guṇaiḥ sā mayā madana ārtena prārthitā āśvāsitaḥ tayā sthīyatām kṣaṇam iti evam sthāsyāmi iti mayā uditam tasya sā vacanam śrutvā kṛtvā svam rūpam uttamam urvaśī uvāca sādhu satyam tvayā vipra vratam niṣṭhita cetasā niṣpāditam haṭhāt eva mama darśanam icchatā aham eva urvaśī vipra tvām jijñāsā artham āgatā parīkṣitaḥ niścitavān bhavān satyatapāḥ ṛṣiḥ gaccha rūpatīrtha iti viśrutam vyāsaḥ uvāca iti uktvā divam utpatya sā jagāma urvaśī dvijāḥ tatra śānti paraḥ bhūtvā śuciḥ babhūva sukule rājā prajā rañjana tatparaḥ sa yajvā vividhaiḥ yajñaiḥ samāpta vara dakṣiṇaiḥ putreṣu rājyam nikṣipya yayau śaukaravam punar rūpatīrthe mṛtaḥ bhūyas śakra lokam upāgataḥ pratiṣṭhāne puravare budha putraḥ purūravāḥ babhūva tatra ca urvaśyāḥ saṃgamāya tapodhanāḥ evam purā satyatapāḥ dvijātiḥ ārādhya janmani atha ca arcya viṣṇum munayaḥ ūcuḥ śrutam phalam gītikāyāḥ asmābhiḥ su prajāgare kṛṣṇasya yena cāṇḍālaḥ gataḥ asau paramām gatim tapasā karmaṇā yena śrotum icchāma sāṃpratam vyāsaḥ uvāca śṛṇudhvam muni śārdūlāḥ pravakṣyāmi anupūrvaśas yathā kṛṣṇe bhavet bhaktiḥ puruṣasya mahā phalā mahā moha kare nṝṇām nānā duḥkha śata ākule tiryagyoni sahasreṣu jāyamānaḥ punar punar kathaṃcid labhate janma dehī mānuṣyakam dvijāḥ yāvat pāpa kṣayam puṃsām na bhavet janma saṃcitam tasmāt vakṣyāmi bho viprāḥ bhaktiḥ kṛṣṇe yathā bhavet karmaṇā manasā vācā tadgatena antarātmanā sa karoti tatas viprāḥ bhaktim ca agneḥ samāhitaḥ pūjām karoti satatam ādityasya tatas dvijāḥ pūjām karoti vidhivat sa tu śaṃbhoḥ prayatnataḥ saṃpūjya tam jagannātham vāsudeva ākhyam avyayam munayaḥ ūcuḥ avaiṣṇavāḥ narāḥ ye tu dṛśyante ca mahā mune kim te viṣṇum na arcayanti brūhi tad kāraṇam dvija vyāsaḥ uvāca āsuraḥ ca tathā daivaḥ purā sṛṣṭaḥ svayaṃbhuvā daivīm prakṛtim āsādya pūjayanti tatas acyutam āsurīm yonim āpannāḥ dūṣayanti narāḥ harim māyayā hata vijñānāḥ viṣṇoḥ te tu nara adhamāḥ a prāpya tam harim viprāḥ tatas yānti adhamām gatim tasya yā gahvarī māyā durvijñeyā sura asuraiḥ mahā moha karī nṝṇām dustarā ca akṛtātmabhiḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ icchāmaḥ tām mahā māyām jñātum viṣṇoḥ su dustarām vyāsaḥ uvāca svapna indrajāla saṃkāśā māyā sā loka karṣaṇī kaḥ śaknoti hareḥ māyām jñātum tām keśavāt ṛte yā vṛttā brāhmaṇasya āsīt māyā arthe nāradasya ca viḍambanām tu tām viprāḥ śṛṇudhvam gadataḥ mama prāk āsīt nṛpatiḥ śrīmān āgnīdhraḥ iti viśrutaḥ dharma ārāmaḥ kṣamā śīlaḥ pitṛ śuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ prajā anurañjakaḥ dakṣaḥ śruti śāstra kṛta śramaḥ sukha mūlāḥ hi dārāḥ ca tasmāt tam tvam samācara sa pituḥ vacanam śrutvā tūṣṇīm āste ca gauravāt muhur muhur tam ca pitā codayām āsa bho dvijāḥ atha asau pitaram prāha tāta nāma anurūpa tā mayā samāśritā vyaktā vaiṣṇavī paripālinī na vidhārayitavyā syāt puruṣeṇa vipaścitā mā nimajja kulam mahyam narake saṃtati kṣayāt sa hi tam pituḥ ādeśam śrutvā prāha sutaḥ vaśī prītaḥ saṃsmṛtya paurāṇīm saṃsārasya vicitra tām śṛṇu tāta vacaḥ mahyam tattva vākyam sa hetukam nāma anurūpam kartavyam satyam bhavati pārthiva mayā janma sahasrāṇi jarā mṛtyu śatāni ca prāptāni dāra saṃyoga viyogāni ca sarvaśas tṛṇa gulma latā vallī sarīsṛpa mṛga dvijāḥ paśu strī puruṣa ādyāni prāptāni śataśas mayā yakṣa guhyaka rakṣāṃsi dānava apsarasaḥ surāḥ nadīśvara sahasram ca prāptam tāta punar punar sṛṣṭaḥ tu bahuśas sṛṣṭau saṃhāre ca api saṃhṛtaḥ dāra saṃyoga yuktasya tāta īdṛś me viḍambanā itas tṛtīye yat vṛttam mama janmani tat śṛṇu kathayāmi samāsena tīrtha māhātmya saṃbhavam atītya janmāni bahūni tāta vidyādharāṇām khaga kiṃnarāṇām jātaḥ hi vaṃśe sutapāḥ mahā ṛṣiḥ saṃtoṣitaḥ cakra gadā astra dhārī tuṣṭaḥ abhyagāt pakṣi patim mahātmā prāha ucca śabdam vriyatām dvijāte varaḥ hi yam vāñchasi tam pradāsye tatas aham ūce harim īśitāram tuṣṭaḥ asi ced keśava tat vṛṇomi yā sā tvadīyā paramā hi māyā atha abravīt me madhukaiṭabhāriḥ kim te tayā brahman māyayā vai dharma artha kāmāni dadāni tubhyam mama adya tām darśaya puṣkarākṣa tatas abhyuvāca atha nṛsiṃha mukhyaḥ śrīśaḥ prabhuḥ viṣṇuḥ idam vacaḥ me viṣṇuḥ uvāca māyām madīyām nahi vetti kaścid pūrvam sura ṛṣiḥ dvija nārada ākhyaḥ nivāritaḥ mām ati mūḍha bhāvāt bhavān yathā evam vṛtavān varam ca māyām hi me vetsyasi saṃnimagnaḥ kanyā babhau kāśi pateḥ suśīlā tām yauvana āḍhyām atha cāru dharmiṇe siṣeva kāmān atulān mahā ṛṣiḥ rājyam krama āyātam avāpya hṛṣṭaḥ vidarbha rāṣṭram paripālayānaḥ atha abhavat bhūmipateḥ sudharmaṇaḥ kāśi īśvareṇa atha samam su yuddham vidarbha rāj kāśipatiḥ ca yuddhe tatas suśīlā pitaram sa putram jñātvā patim ca api sa putra pautram purāt viniḥsṛtya raṇa avanim gatā dṛṣṭvā suśīlā kadanam mahāntam duḥkha anvitā sā su ciram vilapya jagāma sā mātaram ārta rūpā bhrātṝn sutān bhrātṛ sutān sa pautrān bhartāram eṣā pitaram ca gṛhya mahā śmaśāne ca mahācitim sā kṛtvā hutāśam pradadau svayam ca tadā suśīlā praviveśa vegāt dhāḥ putra hā putra iti bruvāṇā tadā punar sā muniḥ nāradaḥ abhūt sa ca api vahniḥ sphaṭika amala ābhaḥ pūrṇam saraḥ abhūt atha ca uttatāra mṛtam ca kam śocasi naṣṭa buddhiḥ vrīḍā anvitaḥ abhūt atha nāradaḥ asau iti īdṛśā nārada kaṣṭa rūpā māyā madīyā kamalāsana ādyaiḥ sa vākyam ākarṇya mahā mahā ṛṣiḥ uvāca bhaktim mama dehi viṣṇo sadā ca saṃdarśanam īśa te astu yatra aham ārtaḥ citim adya rūḍhaḥ sthāsyāmi aham ca atra sadā eva viṣṇuḥ khyātam pṛthivyām ca bhaviṣyate tat yadā na amara ari hantā tīrtham stutam puṇya dam avyaya ākhyam kṛtvā tu pāpāni naraḥ mahānti tasmin praviṣṭaḥ śuciḥ apramādī yadā tu mām cintayate sa śuddhaḥ prayāti mokṣam bhagavat prasādāt bhūtvā tasmin rudra piśāca saṃjñaḥ māyā madīyā nahi śakyate sā cāṇḍāla veśmani abhavat dvijaḥ saḥ rūpa anvitā śīla guṇa upapannā avāpa sā yauvanam āsasāda cāṇḍāla putreṇa subāhunā api kanyā ca paścāt badhirā tathā anyā gatā kadācid kalaśam gṛhītvā sā antar jalam snātum atha praviṣṭā jātaḥ kriyā yoga rataḥ su śīlaḥ draṣṭum jagāma atha nadīm su puṇyām dadarśa kumbham na ca tām taṭa sthām duḥkha anvitā asau samupājagāma te vai rudantam pitaram ca dṛṣṭvā duḥkha anvitāḥ vai ruruduḥ bhṛśa ārtāḥ dṛṣṭā tu toya artham upādravantī ākhyāta te procuḥ imām praviṣṭā etāvat eva iha samīhitam naḥ ruroda śoka aśru paripluta akṣaḥ dṛṣṭvā aham ārtaḥ sutarām babhūva ārtiḥ ca me abhūt atha saṃsmṛtiḥ ca cāṇḍāla yoṣā aham iti kṣitīśa tatas abravam tam nṛpate mataṅgam ākranditena iha vṛthā hi kim te āśvāsayiṣye api atha poṣayiṣye sva vaṃśa vṛttāntam atha ācacakṣe saṃviveśa kokāmukham ārta rūpaḥ tīrtha prabhāvāt ca vimukta pāpaḥ vimānam āruhya śaśi prakāśam mama ārtiḥ āsīt ati moha kartrī tatas ati nirviṇṇa manāḥ gataḥ aham kokāmukham saṃyata vākya cittaḥ vratam samāsthāya kalevaram svam saṃśoṣayitvā divam āruroha saḥ aham samārādhya murāri devam kokāmukhe tyakta śubha aśubha icchaḥ viṣṇum samārādhya varāha rūpam tyaktvā tanum doṣa mayīm tatas tu māyā surāṇām api durvicintyā munayaḥ ūcuḥ asmābhiḥ tu śrutam vyāsa yat tvayā samudāhṛtam prādurbhāva āśritam puṇyam māyā viṣṇoḥ ca durvidā mahāpralaya saṃjñām ca kalpa ante ca mahā mune vyāsaḥ uvāca śrūyatām bho muni śreṣṭhāḥ yathāvat anusaṃhṛtiḥ ahorātram pitṝṇām tu māsaḥ abdam tridivaukasām kṛtam tretā dvāparam ca kaliḥ ca iti caturyugam caturyugāṇi aśeṣāṇi sadṛśāni svarūpataḥ ādyam kṛta yugam proktam munayaḥ antyam tathā kalim munayaḥ ūcuḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca kali svarūpam bho viprāḥ yat pṛcchadhvam mama anaghāḥ varṇa āśrama ācāravatī pravṛttiḥ na kalau nṛṇām vivāhāḥ na kalau dharmāḥ na śiṣyāḥ guru saṃsthitāḥ devatāḥ ca kalau sarvāḥ sarvaḥ sarvasya ca āśramaḥ dharmaḥ yathā abhirucitaiḥ anuṣṭhānaiḥ anuṣṭhitaḥ strīṇām rūpa madaḥ ca eva keśaiḥ eva bhaviṣyati kalau striyaḥ bhaviṣyanti tadā keśaiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ parityakṣyanti bhartāram vitta hīnam tathā striyaḥ yaḥ yaḥ dadāti bahulam sa sa svāmī tadā nṛṇām gṛha antāḥ dravya saṃghātāḥ dravya antā ca tathā matiḥ arthāḥ ca atha upabhoga antāḥ bhaviṣyanti tadā kalau anyāya avāpta vitteṣu puruṣeṣu spṛhālavaḥ abhyarthitaḥ api suhṛdā sva artha hānim tu mānavaḥ paṇasya ardha ardha mātre api kariṣyati tadā dvijāḥ kṣīra pradāna saṃbandhi bhāti goṣu ca gauravam anāvṛṣṭi bhayāt prāyas prajāḥ kṣudh bhaya kātarāḥ bhaviṣyanti tadā sarvāḥ gagana āsakta dṛṣṭayaḥ mūla parṇa phala āhārāḥ tāpasāḥ iva mānavāḥ ātmānam ghātayiṣyanti tadā avṛṣṭyā abhiduḥkhitāḥ durbhikṣam eva satatam sadā kleśam anīśvarāḥ prāpsyanti vyāhata sukham pramādāt mānavāḥ kalau lolupāḥ hrasva dehāḥ ca bahu anna adana tatparāḥ ubhābhyām atha pāṇibhyām śiraḥ kaṇḍūyanam striyaḥ kurvatyaḥ guru bhartṝṇām ājñām bhetsyanti anāvṛtāḥ sva poṣaṇa parāḥ kruddhāḥ deha saṃskāra varjitāḥ paruṣa anṛta bhāṣiṇyaḥ bhaviṣyanti kalau striyaḥ duḥśīlāḥ duṣṭa śīleṣu kurvatyaḥ satatam spṛhām asat vṛttāḥ bhaviṣyanti puruṣeṣu kula aṅganāḥ veda ādānam kariṣyanti vaḍavāḥ ca tathāvratāḥ bhaveyuḥ vana vāsāḥ vai grāmya āhāra parigrahāḥ bhikṣavaḥ ca api putrāḥ hi sneha saṃbandha yantrakāḥ arakṣitāraḥ hartāraḥ śulka vyājena pārthivāḥ hāriṇaḥ jana vittānām saṃprāpte ca kalau yuge yaḥ yaḥ aśva ratha nāga āḍhyaḥ sa sa rājā bhaviṣyati yaḥ ca yaḥ ca abalaḥ sarvaḥ sa sa bhṛtyaḥ kalau yuge vaiśyāḥ kṛṣi vaṇijya ādi saṃtyajya nija karma yat śūdra vṛttyāḥ bhaviṣyanti kāru karma upajīvinaḥ bhaikṣya vratāḥ tathā śūdrāḥ pravrajyā liṅginaḥ adhamāḥ pākhaṇḍa saṃśrayām vṛttim āśrayiṣyanti asaṃskṛtāḥ durbhikṣa kara pīḍābhiḥ atīva upadrutāḥ janāḥ godhūma anna yava annādyān deśān yāsyanti duḥkhitāḥ veda mārge pralīne ca pākhaṇḍa āḍhye tatas jane adharma vṛddhyā lokānām alpam āyuḥ bhaviṣyati a śāstra vihitam ghoram tapyamāneṣu vai tapaḥ nareṣu nṛpa doṣeṇa bāla mṛtyuḥ bhaviṣyati bhavitrī yoṣitām sūtiḥ pañca ṣaṣ sapta vārṣikī nava aṣṭa daśa varṣāṇām manuṣyāṇām tathā kalau palita udgamaḥ ca bhavitā tadā dvādaśa vārṣikaḥ na jīviṣyati vai kaścid kalau varṣāṇi viṃśatim alpa prajñāḥ vṛthāliṅgāḥ duṣṭa antaḥkaraṇāḥ kalau yatas tatas vinaśyanti kālena alpena mānavāḥ yadā yadā hi pākhaṇḍa vṛttiḥ atra upalakṣyate tadā tadā kaleḥ vṛddhiḥ anumeyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ yadā yadā satām hāniḥ veda mārga anusāriṇām tadā tadā kaleḥ vṛddhiḥ anumeyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ prārambhāḥ ca avasīdanti yadā dharma kṛtām nṛṇām tadā anumeyam prādhānyam kaleḥ viprāḥ vicakṣaṇaiḥ yadā yadā na yajñānām īśvaraḥ puruṣottamaḥ na prītiḥ veda vādeṣu pākhaṇḍeṣu yadā ratiḥ kaleḥ vṛddhiḥ tadā prājñaiḥ anumeyā dvijottamāḥ kalau jagatpatim viṣṇum sarva sraṣṭāram īśvaram na arcayiṣyanti bho viprāḥ pākhaṇḍa upahatāḥ narāḥ kim devaiḥ kim dvijaiḥ vedaiḥ kim śaucena ambu jalpanā iti evam pralapiṣyanti pākhaṇḍa upahatāḥ narāḥ alpa vṛṣṭiḥ ca parjanyaḥ su alpam sasya phalam tathā phalam tathā alpa sāram ca viprāḥ prāpte kalau yuge jānu prāyāṇi vastrāṇi śamī prāyāḥ mahīruhāḥ śūdra prāyāḥ tathā varṇāḥ bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge aṇu prāyāṇi dhānyāni āja prāyam tathā payaḥ bhaviṣyati kalau prāpte auśīram ca anulepanam śvaśrū śvaśura bhūyiṣṭhāḥ guravaḥ ca nṛṇām kalau śāla ādi āhāri bhāryāḥ ca suhṛdaḥ muni sattamāḥ kasya mātā pitā kasya yadā karma ātmakaḥ pumān iti ca udāhariṣyanti śvaśura anugatāḥ narāḥ vāc manaḥ kāya jaiḥ doṣaiḥ abhibhūtāḥ punar punar narāḥ pāpāni anudinam kariṣyanti alpa medhasaḥ niḥsatyānām aśaucānām nirhrīkāṇām tathā dvijāḥ niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkāre svadhā svāhā vivarjite munayaḥ ūcuḥ vaktum arhasi aśeṣeṇa śrotum vāñchā pravartate vyāsaḥ uvāca tathā bhavetām strī śūdrau dhanyau ca anyat nibodhata yat kṛte daśabhiḥ varṣaiḥ tretāyām hāyanena tat dhyāyan kṛte yajan yajñaiḥ tretāyām dvāpare arcayan su alpa āyāsena dharma jñāḥ tena tuṣṭaḥ asmi aham kalau vrata caryā paraiḥ grāhyāḥ vedāḥ pūrvam dvijātibhiḥ vṛthā kathā vṛthā bhojyam vṛthā svam ca dvijanmanām asamyakkaraṇe doṣāḥ teṣām sarveṣu vastuṣu bhojya peya ādikam ca eṣām na icchā prāpti karam dvijāḥ pāratantryāt samasteṣu teṣām kāryeṣu vai tatas lokān kleśena mahatā yajanti vinaya anvitāḥ dvija śuśrūṣaṇena eva pākayajña adhikāravān bhakṣya abhakṣyeṣu na āśā asti yeṣām pāpeṣu vā yatas niyamaḥ muni śārdūlāḥ tena asau sādhu iti īritam pratipādanīyam pātreṣu yaṣṭavyam ca yathāvidhi tasya arjane mahān kleśaḥ pālanena dvijottamāḥ tathā sat viniyogāya vijñeyam gahanam nṛṇām ebhiḥ anyaiḥ tathā kleśaiḥ puruṣāḥ dvijasattamāḥ nijān jayanti vai lokān prājāpatya ādikān kramāt yoṣit śuśrūṣaṇāt bhartuḥ karmaṇā manasā girā etat viṣayam āpnoti tad sālokyam yatas dvijāḥ na ati kleśena mahatā tān eva puruṣaḥ yathā tṛtīyam vyāhṛtam tena mayā sādhu iti yoṣitaḥ etat vaḥ kathitam viprāḥ yad nimittam iha āgatāḥ tat pṛcchadhvam yathākāmam aham vakṣyāmi vaḥ sphuṭam naraiḥ ātma guṇa ambhobhiḥ kṣālita akhila kilbiṣaiḥ śūdraiḥ ca dvija śuśrūṣā tad paraiḥ muni sattamāḥ tathā strībhiḥ anāyāsāt pati śuśrūṣayā eva hi dharma saṃrādhane kleśaḥ dvijātīnām kṛta ādiṣu tathā su alpena tapasā siddhim yāsyanti mānavāḥ a pṛṣṭena api dharma jñāḥ kim anyat kriyatām dvijāḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ āsannam viprakṛṣṭam vā yadi kālam na vidmahe tatas dvāpara vidhvaṃsam yuga antam spṛhayāmahe prāptāḥ vayam hi tat kālam anayā dharma tṛṣṇayā ādadyāma param dharmam sukham alpena karmaṇā vyāsaḥ uvāca arakṣitāraḥ hartāraḥ balibhāgasya pārthivāḥ yuga ante prabhaviṣyanti sva rakṣaṇa parāyaṇāḥ a kṣatriyāḥ ca rājānaḥ viprāḥ śūdra upajīvinaḥ śūdrāḥ ca brāhmaṇa ācārāḥ bhaviṣyanti yuga kṣaye śrotriyāḥ kāṇḍapṛṣṭhāḥ ca niṣkarmāṇi havīṃṣi ca eka paṅktyām aśiṣyanti yuga ante muni sattamāḥ a śiṣṭavantaḥ artha parāḥ narāḥ madya āmiṣa priyāḥ mitra bhāryām bhajiṣyanti yuga ante puruṣa adhamāḥ rāja vṛtti sthitāḥ caurāḥ rājānaḥ caura śīlinaḥ dhanāni ślāghanīyāni satām vṛttam a pūjitam pranaṣṭa nāsāḥ puruṣāḥ mukta keśāḥ virūpiṇaḥ ūna ṣoḍaśa varṣāḥ ca prasoṣyanti tathā striyaḥ aṭṭa śūlāḥ janapadāḥ śiva śūlāḥ catuṣpathāḥ pramadāḥ keśa śūlāḥ ca bhaviṣyanti yuga kṣaye śūdra ābhāḥ vādinaḥ ca eva brāhmaṇāḥ ca antyavāsinaḥ śukla dantāḥ jita akṣāḥ ca muṇḍāḥ kāṣāya vāsasaḥ śūdrāḥ dharmam vadiṣyanti śāṭhya buddhyā upajīvinaḥ śvāpada pracura tvam ca gavām ca eva parikṣayaḥ sādhūnām parivṛttiḥ ca vidyāt anta gate yuge nirhrīkāḥ ca prajāḥ sarvāḥ naṣṭāḥ tatra yuga kṣaye tapaḥ yajña phalānām ca vikretāraḥ dvijottamāḥ ṛtavaḥ viparītāḥ ca bhaviṣyanti yuga kṣaye tathā dvi hāyanāḥ damyāḥ kalau lāṅgala dhāriṇaḥ citra varṣī ca parjanyaḥ yuge kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati sarve śūra kule jātāḥ kṣamā nāthāḥ bhavanti hi yathā nimnāḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ bhaviṣyanti yuga kṣaye pitṛ deyāni dattāni bhaviṣyanti tathā sutāḥ ūṣarā bahulā bhūmiḥ panthānaḥ taskara āvṛtāḥ sarve vāṇikāḥ ca eva bhaviṣyanti yuga kṣaye pitṛ dāyāda dattāni vibhajanti tathā sutāḥ bhaviṣyanti yugasya ante nāryaḥ keśaiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ yuga ante samanuprāpte na anyā bhāryā samā ratiḥ kuśīla anārya bhūyiṣṭhāḥ vṛthā rūpa samanvitāḥ puruṣa alpam bahu strīkam tat yuga antasya lakṣaṇam rāja caura agni daṇḍa ādi kṣīṇaḥ kṣayam upaiṣyati aphalāni ca sasyāni taruṇāḥ vṛddha śīlinaḥ aśīlāḥ sukhinaḥ loke bhaviṣyanti yuga kṣaye varṣāsu paruṣāḥ vātāḥ nīcāḥ śarkara varṣiṇaḥ vaiśyāḥ iva ca rājanyāḥ dhana dhānya upajīvinaḥ yuga apakramaṇe pūrvam bhaviṣyanti na bāndhavāḥ apravṛttāḥ prapaśyanti samayāḥ śapathāḥ tathā ṛṇam sa vinaya bhraṃśam yuge kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati bhaviṣyati aphalaḥ harṣaḥ krodhaḥ ca sa phalaḥ nṛṇām apramāṇam kariṣyanti narāḥ paṇḍita māninaḥ śāstra uktasya a pravaktāraḥ bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ sarvaḥ sarvam vijānāti vṛddhān an upasevya vai nakṣatrāṇi viyogāni na karma sthāḥ dvijātayaḥ caura prāyāḥ ca rājānaḥ yuga ante samupasthite kuṇḍīvṛṣāḥ naikṛtikāḥ surāpāḥ brahma vādinaḥ yājayiṣyanti a yājyān tu tathā abhakṣyasya bhakṣiṇaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ dhana tṛṣṇā ārtāḥ yuga ante samupasthite ekaśaṅkhāḥ tathā nāryaḥ gavedhu kapinaddhakāḥ nakṣatrāṇi vivarṇāni viparitāḥ diśaḥ daśa saṃdhyā rāgaḥ vidagdha aṅgaḥ bhaviṣyati yuga kṣaye preṣayanti pitṝn putrāḥ vadhūḥ śvaśrūḥ sva karmasu a kṛtvā agrāṇi bhokṣyanti dvijāḥ ca eva a huta agnayaḥ bhikṣām balim a dattvā ca bhokṣyanti puruṣāḥ svayam na vyādhitān na api arūpān na udyatān na api asūyakān kṛte na pratikartā ca yuge kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati munayaḥ ūcuḥ evam vilambite dharme mānuṣāḥ kara pīḍitāḥ kutra deśe nivatsyanti kimāhāra vihāriṇaḥ kiṃkarmāṇaḥ kim īhantaḥ kiṃpramāṇāḥ kim āyuṣaḥ kām ca kāṣṭhām samāsādya prapatsyanti kṛtam yugam vyāsaḥ uvāca atas ūrdhvam cyute dharme guṇa hīnāḥ prajāḥ tathā śīla vyasanam āsādya prāpsyanti hrāsam āyuṣaḥ āyuḥ ha anyāḥ balagnā aniḥ balagnā anyāḥ vivarṇa tā vaivarṇyāt vyādhi saṃpīḍā nirvedaḥ vyādhi pīḍanāt nirvedāt ātma saṃbodhaḥ saṃbodhāt dharma śīla tā evam gatvā parām kāṣṭhām prapatsyanti kṛtam yugam uddeśataḥ dharma śīlāḥ kecid madhyastha tām gatāḥ kiṃdharma śīlāḥ kecid tu kecid atra kutūhalāḥ pratyakṣam anumānam ca pramāṇam iti niścitāḥ apramāṇam kariṣyanti sarvam iti apare janāḥ nāstikya paratāḥ ca api kecid dharma vilopakāḥ bhaviṣyanti narāḥ mūḍhāḥ dvijāḥ paṇḍita māninaḥ tadātva mātra śraddheyā śāstra jñāna bahiṣkṛtāḥ dāmbhikāḥ te bhaviṣyanti narāḥ jñāna vilopitāḥ tathā vilulite dharme janāḥ śreṣṭha puraskṛtāḥ śubhān samācariṣyanti dāna śīla parāyaṇāḥ sarva bhakṣāḥ svayaṃguptāḥ nirghṛṇāḥ nirapatrapāḥ bhaviṣyanti tadā loke tat kaṣāyasya lakṣaṇam kaṣāya upaplave kāle jñāna niṣṭhā praṇāśane viprāṇām śāśvatīm vṛttim yadā varṇa avare janāḥ saṃśrayiṣyanti bho viprāḥ tat kaṣāyasya lakṣaṇam mahā yuddham mahā varṣam mahā vātam mahā tapaḥ bhaviṣyati yuge kṣīṇe tat kaṣāyasya lakṣaṇam vipra rūpeṇa yakṣāṃsi rājānaḥ karṇa vedinaḥ niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkārāḥ ku netāraḥ abhimāninaḥ kravyādāḥ brahma rūpeṇa sarva bhakṣyāḥ vṛthāvratāḥ mūrkhāḥ ca artha parāḥ lubdhāḥ kṣudrāḥ kṣudra paricchadāḥ vyavahāra upavṛttāḥ ca cyutāḥ dharmāḥ ca śāśvatāt hartāraḥ para ratnānām para dāra pradharṣakāḥ kāma ātmānaḥ durātmānaḥ sa upadhāḥ priya sāhasāḥ teṣu prabhavamāṇeṣu janeṣu api ca sarvaśas kalau yuge samutpannāḥ pradhāna puruṣāḥ ca ye kathā yogena tān sarvān pūjayiṣyanti mānavāḥ sasya caurāḥ bhaviṣyanti tathā caila apahāriṇaḥ bhokṣya bhojya harāḥ ca eva karaṇḍānām ca hāriṇaḥ cauraiḥ caura kṣaye ca api kṛte kṣemam bhaviṣyati narāḥ vanam śrayiṣyanti kara bhāra prapīḍitāḥ yajña karmaṇi uparate rakṣāṃsi śvāpadāni ca kīṭa mūṣika sarpāḥ ca dharṣayiṣyanti mānavān kṣemam subhikṣam ārogyam sāmagryam ca eva bandhuṣu uddeśeṣu narāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ bhaviṣyanti yuga kṣaye svayaṃpālāḥ svayam caurāḥ plava saṃbhāra saṃbhṛtāḥ maṇḍalaiḥ saṃbhaviṣyanti deśe deśe pṛthak pṛthak sva deśebhyaḥ paribhraṣṭāḥ niḥsārāḥ saha bandhubhiḥ narāḥ sarve bhaviṣyanti tadā kāla parikṣayāt tatas sarve samādāya kumārān pradrutāḥ bhayāt kauśikīm saṃtariṣyanti narāḥ kṣudh bhaya pīḍitāḥ aṅgān vaṅgān kaliṅgān ca kāśmīrān atha kośalān ṛṣikānta giri droṇīḥ saṃśrayiṣyanti mānavāḥ kṛtsnam ca himavat pārśvam kūlam ca lavaṇāmbhasaḥ vividham jīrṇa pattram ca valkalāni ajināni ca na eva śūnyā nava araṇyā bhaviṣyati vasuṃdharā a goptāraḥ ca goptāraḥ bhaviṣyanti narādhipāḥ mṛgaiḥ matsyaiḥ vihaṃgaiḥ ca śvāpadaiḥ sarpa kīṭakaiḥ madhu śāka phalaiḥ mūlaiḥ vartayiṣyanti mānavāḥ śīrṇa parṇa phala āhārāḥ valkalāni ajināni ca bījānām a kṛta snehāḥ āhatāḥ kāṣṭha śaṅkubhiḥ aja eḍakam khara uṣṭram ca pālayiṣyanti nityaśas nadī srotāṃsi rotsyanti toya artham kūlam āśritāḥ tanūruhaiḥ yathā jātaiḥ sa mala antara saṃbhṛtaiḥ bahu apatyāḥ prajā hīnāḥ kula śīla vivarjitāḥ evam bhaviṣyanti tadā narāḥ ca adharma jīvinaḥ hīnā hīnam tathā dharmam prajā samanuvatsyati āyuḥ tatra ca martyānām param triṃśat bhaviṣyati durbalāḥ viṣaya glānāḥ jarā śokaiḥ abhiplutāḥ bhaviṣyanti tadā teṣām rogaiḥ indriya saṃkṣayaḥ āyuḥ pratyaya saṃrodhāt viṣayāt uparaṃsyate śuśrūṣavaḥ bhaviṣyanti sādhūnām darśane ratāḥ bhaviṣyanti ca kāmānām alābhāt dharma śīlinaḥ kariṣyanti ca saṃskāram svayam ca kṣaya pīḍitāḥ evam śuśrūṣavaḥ dāne satye prāṇi abhirakṣaṇe teṣām labdha anumānānām guṇeṣu parivartatām svādu kim tu iti vijñāya dharmaḥ eva ca dṛśyate yathā hāni kramam prāptāḥ tathā ṛddhi kramam gatāḥ sādhu vṛttiḥ kṛta yuge kaṣāye hāniḥ ucyate ekaḥ eva tu kālaḥ ayam hīna varṇaḥ yathā śaśī arthavādaḥ param brahma veda arthaḥ iti tam viduḥ a viviktam a vijñātam dāyādyam iha dhāryate iṣṭa vādaḥ tapaḥ nāma tapaḥ hi sthavirīkṛtaḥ guṇaiḥ karma abhinirvṛttiḥ guṇāḥ śudhyanti karmaṇā āśīḥ tu puruṣam dṛṣṭvā deśa kāla anuvartinī yuge yuge yathākālam ṛṣibhiḥ samudāhṛtā dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām devānām ca pratikriyā āśiṣaḥ ca śivāḥ puṇyāḥ tathā eva āyuḥ yuge yuge tathā yugānām parivartanāni kṣaṇam na saṃtiṣṭhati jīva lokaḥ kṣaya udayābhyām parivartamānaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca sarveṣām eva bhūtānām trividhaḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ brāhmaḥ naimittikaḥ teṣām kalpa ante pratisaṃcaraḥ ātyantikaḥ vai mokṣaḥ ca prākṛtaḥ dviparārdhikaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ parārdha saṃkhyām bhagavan tvam ācakṣva yathā uditām dviguṇīkṛta yat jñeyaḥ prākṛtaḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca sthānāt sthānam daśaguṇam ekaikam gaṇyate dvijāḥ tatas aṣṭādaśame bhāge parārdham abhidhīyate parārdham dviguṇam yat tu prākṛtaḥ sa layaḥ dvijāḥ nimeṣaḥ mānuṣaḥ yaḥ ayam mātrā mātra pramāṇataḥ taiḥ pañcadaśabhiḥ kāṣṭhā triṃśat kāṣṭhāḥ tathā kalā nāḍikā tu pramāṇena kalā ca daśa pañca ca unmānena ambhasaḥ sā tu palāni ardha trayodaśa hema māṣaiḥ kṛta chidrā caturbhiḥ catur aṅgulaiḥ nāḍikābhyām atha dvābhyām muhūrtaḥ dvijasattamāḥ ahorātram muhūrtāḥ tu triṃśat māsaḥ dinaiḥ tathā tribhiḥ varṣa śataiḥ varṣam ṣaṣṭyā ca eva asuradviṣām taiḥ tu dvādaśa sāhasraiḥ caturyugam udāhṛtam śṛṇudhvam prākṛtam bhūyas tatas vakṣyāmi aham layam caturyuga sahasra ante kṣīṇa prāye mahī tale anāvṛṣṭiḥ atīva ugrā jāyate śata vārṣikī tatas yāni alpa sārāṇi tāni sattvāni anekaśas kṣayam yānti muni śreṣṭhāḥ pārthivāni atipīḍanāt tatas sa bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ rudra rūpī tathā avyayaḥ kṣayāya yatate kartum ātma sthāḥ sakalāḥ prajāḥ tatas sa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ bhānoḥ saptasu raśmiṣu sthitaḥ pibati aśeṣāṇi jalāni muni sattamāḥ pītvā ambhāṃsi samastāni prāṇi bhūta gatāni vai śoṣam nayati bho viprāḥ samastam pṛthivī talam samudrān saritaḥ śailān śaila prasravaṇāni ca pātāleṣu ca yat toyam tat sarvam nayati kṣayam tatas tasya api abhāvena toya āhāra upabṛṃhitāḥ adhas ca ūrdhvam ca te dīptāḥ tatas sapta divākarāḥ dahanti aśeṣam trailokyam sa pātāla talam dvijāḥ sa adri naga arṇava ābhogam niḥsneham abhijāyate bhavati eṣā ca vasudhā kūrma pṛṣṭha upama ākṛtiḥ śeṣa ahi śvāsa saṃtāpāt pātālāni dahati adhas pātālāni samastāni sa dagdhvā jvalanaḥ mahān bhuvaḥ lokam tatas sarvam svarga lokam ca dāruṇaḥ ambarīṣam iva ābhāti trailokyam akhilam tadā jvālā āvarta parīvāram upakṣīṇa balāḥ tatas hṛta avakāśāḥ gacchanti mahar lokam dvijāḥ tadā tasmāt api mahā tāpa taptāḥ lokāḥ tatas param gacchanti jana lokam te daśa āvṛtyā para eṣiṇaḥ mukha niḥśvāsa jān meghān karoti muni sattamāḥ uttiṣṭhanti tadā vyomni ghorāḥ saṃvartakāḥ ghanāḥ kecid añjana saṃkāśāḥ kecid kumuda saṃnibhāḥ dhūma varṇāḥ ghanāḥ kecid kecid pītāḥ payodharāḥ kecid dharidrā varṇa ābhāḥ lākṣā rasa nibhāḥ tathā kecid vaidūrya saṃkāśāḥ indranīla nibhāḥ tathā śaṅkha kunda nibhāḥ ca anye jātī kunda nibhāḥ tathā indragopa nibhāḥ kecid manaḥśilā nibhāḥ tathā padma pattra nibhāḥ kecid uttiṣṭhanti ghana aghanāḥ kecid puravara ākārāḥ kecid parvata saṃnibhāḥ kūṭāgāra nibhāḥ ca anye kecid sthala nibhāḥ ghanāḥ mahā kāyāḥ mahā rāvā pūrayanti nabhastalam naṣṭe ca agnau śatam te api varṣāṇām adhikam ghanāḥ dhārābhiḥ akṣa mātrābhiḥ plāvayitvā akhilām bhuvam andhakārīkṛte loke naṣṭe sthāvara jaṅgame varṣanti te mahā meghāḥ varṣāṇām adhikam śatam vyāsaḥ uvāca atha niḥśvāsa jaḥ viṣṇoḥ vāyuḥ tān jaladān tatas nāśam nayati bho viprāḥ varṣāṇām adhikam śatam anādiḥ ādiḥ viśvasya pītvā vāyum aśeṣatas ekārṇave tatas tasmin śeṣa śayyā sthitaḥ prabhuḥ brahma rūpa dharaḥ śete bhagavān ādi kṛt hariḥ ātma māyā mayīm divyām yoganidrām samāsthitaḥ ātmānam vāsudeva ākhyam cintayan parameśvaraḥ eṣa naimittikaḥ nāma vipra indrāḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ yadā jāgarti sarva ātmā sa tadā ceṣṭate jagat nimīlati etat akhilam māyā śayyā āśaye acyute eka arṇava kṛte loke tāvatī rātriḥ ucyate tatas prabuddhaḥ rātri ante punar sṛṣṭim karoti ajaḥ brahma sva rūpa dhṛk viṣṇuḥ yathā vaḥ kathitam purā naimittikaḥ vaḥ kathitaḥ śṛṇudhvam prākṛtam param avṛṣṭi agni ādibhiḥ samyak kṛte śayyā ālaye dvijāḥ samasteṣu eva lokeṣu pātāleṣu akhileṣu ca mahat ādeḥ vikārasya viśeṣāt tatra saṃkṣaye kṛṣṇa icchā kārite tasmin pravṛtte pratisaṃcare āpaḥ grasanti vai pūrvam bhūmeḥ gandha ādikam guṇam āpaḥ tadā pravṛttāḥ tu vegavatyaḥ mahā svanāḥ sarvam āpūrayanti idam tiṣṭhanti vicaranti ca apām api guṇaḥ yaḥ tu jyotiṣā pīyate tu saḥ naśyanti āpaḥ su taptāḥ ca rasa tanmātra saṃkṣayāt tatas ca āpaḥ amṛta rasāḥ jyotiḥ tvam prāpnuvanti vai sa ca agniḥ sarvatas vyāpya ādatte tat jalam tadā sarvam ca ābhiḥ tadā jagat idam śanais jyotiṣaḥ api param rūpam vāyuḥ atti prabhākaram pranaṣṭe rūpa tanmātre kṛta rūpaḥ vibhāvasuḥ praśāmyati tadā jyotiḥ vāyuḥ dodhūyate mahān tatas pralayam āsādya vāyu saṃbhavam ātmanaḥ ūrdhvam ca vāyuḥ tiryak ca dodhavīti diśaḥ daśa vāyoḥ tu api guṇam sparśam ākāśam grasate tatas praśāmyati tadā vāyuḥ kham tu tiṣṭhati anāvṛtam parimaṇḍalataḥ tat tu ākāśam śabda lakṣaṇam śabda mātram tathā ākāśam sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati tatas śabda guṇam tasya bhūtādiḥ grasate punar abhimāna ātmakaḥ hi eṣa bhūtādiḥ tāmasaḥ smṛtaḥ bhūtādim grasate ca api mahā buddhiḥ vicakṣaṇā urvī mahān ca jagataḥ prānte antar bāhyatas tathā pratyāhāraiḥ tu tāḥ sarvāḥ praviśanti parasparam yena idam āvṛtam sarvam aṇḍam apsu pralīyate udaka āvaraṇam hi atra jyotiṣā pīyate tu tat jyotiḥ vāyau layam yāti yāti ākāśe samīraṇaḥ ākāśam ca eva bhūtādiḥ grasate tam tathā mahān guṇa sāmyam an udriktam anyūnam ca dvijottamāḥ procyate prakṛtiḥ hetuḥ pradhānam kāraṇam param iti eṣā prakṛtiḥ sarvā vyakta avyakta svarūpiṇī ekaḥ śuddhaḥ akṣaraḥ nityaḥ sarvavyāpī tathā punar saḥ api aṃśaḥ sarva bhūtasya dvijendrāḥ paramātmanaḥ naśyanti sarvāḥ yatra api nāma jāti ādi kalpanāḥ sattā mātra ātmake jñeye jñāna ātmani ātmanaḥ pare sa brahma tat param dhāma paramātmā para īśvaraḥ sa viṣṇuḥ sarvam eva idam yatas na āvartate punar prakṛtiḥ yā mayā ākhyātā vyakta avyakta svarūpiṇī puruṣaḥ ca api ubhau etau līyete paramātmani paramātmā ca sarveṣām ādhāraḥ parameśvaraḥ viṣṇu nāmnā sa vedeṣu vedānteṣu ca gīyate tābhyām ubhābhyām puruṣaiḥ yajña mūrtiḥ saḥ ijyate yajñeśvaraḥ yajñapumān puruṣaiḥ puruṣottamaḥ jñāna ātmā jñāna yogena jñāna mūrtiḥ saḥ ijyate yat ca vācām aviṣayaḥ tat sarvam viṣṇuḥ avyayaḥ paramātmā ca viśvātmā viśva rūpa dharaḥ hariḥ vyakta avyakta ātmikā tasmin prakṛtiḥ sā vilīyate puruṣaḥ ca api bho viprāḥ yaḥ tat avyākṛta ātmani dvi parārdha ātmakaḥ kālaḥ kathitaḥ yaḥ mayā dvijāḥ vyakte tu prakṛtau līne prakṛtyām puruṣe tathā tatra āsthite niśā tasya tad pramāṇā tapodhanāḥ iti eṣa muni śārdūlāḥ kathitaḥ prākṛtaḥ layaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca ādhyātmika ādi bho viprāḥ jñātvā tāpa trayam budhaḥ utpanna jñāna vairāgyaḥ prāpnoti ātyantikam layam ādhyātmikaḥ api dvividhaḥ śārīraḥ mānasaḥ tathā śārīraḥ bahubhiḥ bhedaiḥ bhidyate śrūyatām ca saḥ śiraḥ roga pratiśyāya jvara śūla bhagaṃdaraiḥ gulma arśaḥ śvayathu śvāsa chardi ādibhiḥ anekadhā tathā akṣi roga atīsāra kuṣṭha aṅga āmaya saṃjñakaiḥ śoka asūyā avamāna īrṣyā mātsarya abhibhavaḥ tathā mānasaḥ api dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ tāpaḥ bhavati na ekadhā iti evamādibhiḥ bhedaiḥ tāpaḥ hi ādhyātmikaḥ smṛtaḥ mṛga pakṣi manuṣya ādyaiḥ piśāca uraga rākṣasaiḥ sarīsṛpa ādyaiḥ ca nṛṇām janyate ca ādhibhautikaḥ śīta uṣṇa vāta varṣa ambu vaidyuta ādi samudbhavaḥ tāpaḥ dvijavara śreṣṭhāḥ kathyate ca ādhidaivikaḥ garbha janma jarā jñāna mṛtyu nāraka jam tathā ulba saṃveṣṭitaḥ bhagna pṛṣṭha grīvā asthi saṃhatiḥ ati amla kaṭu tīkṣṇa uṣṇa lavaṇaiḥ mātṛ bhojanaiḥ prasāraṇa ākuñcana ādau nāgānām prabhuḥ ātmanaḥ śakṛt mūtra mahā paṅka śāyī sarvatra pīḍitaḥ jāyamānaḥ purīṣa asṛj mūtra śukra āvila ānanaḥ prājāpatyena vātena pīḍyamāna asthi bandhanaḥ kleśaiḥ niṣkrāntim āpnoti jaṭharāt mātuḥ āturaḥ mūrchām avāpya mahatīm saṃspṛṣṭaḥ bāhya vāyunā vijñāna bhraṃśam āpnoti jātaḥ tu muni sattamāḥ kaṇṭakaiḥ iva tunna aṅgaḥ krakacaiḥ iva dāritaḥ pūti vraṇāt nipatitaḥ dharaṇyām krimikaḥ yathā kaṇḍūyane api ca aśaktaḥ parivarte api anīśvaraḥ stana pāna ādika āhāram avāpnoti para icchayā aśuci srastare suptaḥ kīṭa daṃśa ādibhiḥ tathā bhakṣyamāṇaḥ api na eva eṣām samarthaḥ vinivāraṇe bāla bhāve yat āpnoti ādhibhūta ādikāni ca ajñāna tamasā channaḥ mūḍha antaḥkaraṇaḥ naraḥ na jānāti kutas kaḥ aham kutra gantā kimātmakaḥ kena bandhena baddhaḥ aham kāraṇam kim akāraṇam kim kāryam kim akāryam vā kim vācyam kim na ca ucyate kim kartavyam akartavyam kim vā kim guṇa doṣavat evam paśu samaiḥ mūḍhaiḥ ajñāna prabhavam mahat avāpyate naraiḥ duḥkham śiśna udara parāyaṇaiḥ ajñānam tāmasaḥ bhāvaḥ kārya ārambha pravṛttayaḥ ajñāninām pravartante karma lopaḥ tatas dvijāḥ narakam karmaṇām lopāt phalam āhuḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ tasmāt ajñāninām duḥkham iha ca amutra ca uttamam jarā jarjara dehaḥ ca śithila avayavaḥ pumān vicalat śīrṇa daśanaḥ vali snāyu sirā vṛtaḥ dūra pranaṣṭa nayanaḥ vyoma antargata tārakaḥ nāsā vivara niryāta roma puñjaḥ calat vapuḥ prakaṭībhūta sarva asthiḥ nata pṛṣṭha asthi saṃhatiḥ utsanna jaṭhara agni tvāt alpa āhāraḥ alpa ceṣṭitaḥ kṛcchra caṅkramaṇa utthāna śayana āsana ceṣṭitaḥ tad kṣaṇe api anubhūtānām asmartā akhila vastunām sakṛt uccārite vākye samudbhūta mahā śramaḥ śvāsa kāsa āmaya āyāsa samudbhūta prajāgaraḥ bhṛtya ātma putra dārāṇām apamāna parākṛtaḥ prakṣīṇa akhila śaucaḥ ca vihāra āhāra saṃspṛhaḥ hāsyaḥ parijanasya api nirviṇṇa aśeṣa bāndhavaḥ anubhūtam iva anyasmin janmani ātma viceṣṭitam evamādīni duḥkhāni jarāyām anubhūya ca maraṇe yāni duḥkhāni prāpnoti śṛṇu tāni api ślatha grīvā aṅghri hastaḥ atha prāptaḥ vepathunā naraḥ muhur glāni paraḥ ca asau muhur jñāna bala anvitaḥ hiraṇya dhānya tanaya bhāryā bhṛtya gṛha ādiṣu ete katham bhaviṣyanti iti atīva mamatā ākulaḥ parivartamāna tārā akṣi hasta pādam muhur kṣipan saṃśuṣyamāṇa tālu oṣṭha kaṇṭhaḥ ghuraghurāyate niruddha kaṇṭha deśaḥ api udāna śvāsa pīḍitaḥ tāpena mahatā vyāptaḥ tṛṣā vyāptaḥ tathā kṣudhā kleśāt utkrāntim āpnoti yāmya kiṃkara pīḍitaḥ etāni anyāni ca ugrāṇi duḥkhāni maraṇe nṛṇām śṛṇudhvam narake yāni prāpyante puruṣaiḥ mṛtaiḥ yāmya kiṃkara pāśa ādi grahaṇam daṇḍa tāḍanam karambha vālukā vahni yantra śastra ādi bhīṣaṇe pratyekam yātanāyāḥ ca yātanā ādi dvijottamāḥ krakacaiḥ pīḍyamānānām mṛṣāyām ca api kuṭhāraiḥ pāṭyamānānām bhūmau ca api nikhanyatām śūleṣu āropyamāṇānām vyāghra vaktre praveśyatām gṛdhraiḥ saṃbhakṣyamāṇānām dvīpibhiḥ uccān nipātyamānānām kṣipyatām kṣepa yantrakaiḥ narake yāni duḥkhāni pāpa hetu udbhavāni vai prāpyante nārakaiḥ viprāḥ teṣām saṃkhyā na vidyate na kevalam dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ narake duḥkha paddhatiḥ svarge api pāta bhītasya kṣayiṣṇoḥ nā asti nirvṛtiḥ yat yat prīti karam puṃsām vastu viprāḥ prajāyate kriyate na tathā bhūri sukham puṃsām yathāsukham iti saṃsāra duḥkha arka tāpa tāpita cetasām vimukti pādapa chāyām ṛte kutra sukham nṛṇām nirasta atiśaya āhlādam sukha bhāva eka lakṣaṇam bheṣajam bhagavat prāptiḥ ekā ca ātyantikī matā tad prāpti hetuḥ jñānam ca karma ca uktam dvijottamāḥ āgama uttham vivekāt ca dvidhā jñānam tathā ucyate yathā sūryaḥ tathā jñānam yat vai viprāḥ viveka jam manuḥ api āha veda artham smṛtvā yat muni sattamāḥ śabdabrahmaṇi niṣṇātaḥ param brahma adhigacchati parayā hi akṣara prāptiḥ ṛgveda ādi mayā aparā anirdeśyam arūpam ca pāṇi pāda ādi asaṃyutam vittam sarva gatam nityam bhūta yonim akāraṇam vyāpyam vyāptam yatas sarvam tat vai paśyanti sūrayaḥ tat brahma paramam dhāma tat dheyam mokṣa kāṅkṣibhiḥ śruti vākya uditam sūkṣmam tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam utpattim pralayam ca eva bhūtānām āgatim gatim jñāna śakti bala aiśvarya vīrya tejāṃsi aśeṣatas bhūteṣu ca sa sarva ātmā vāsudevaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ uvāca idam mahā ṛṣibhyaḥ purā pṛṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ dhātā vidhātā jagatām vāsudevaḥ tatas prabhuḥ sa sarva bhūta prakṛtiḥ guṇān ca doṣān ca sarvān sa guṇaḥ hi atītaḥ atīta sarva āvaraṇaḥ akhila ātmā tena āvṛtam yat bhuvana antarālam samasta kalyāṇa guṇa ātmakaḥ hi sva śakti leśa ādṛta bhūta sargaḥ icchā gṛhīta abhimata uru dehaḥ saṃsādhita aśeṣa jagat hitaḥ asau sva vīrya śakti ādi guṇa eka rāśiḥ paraḥ parāṇām sakalāḥ na yatra kleśa ādayaḥ santi para apara īśe saḥ īśvaraḥ vyaṣṭi samaṣṭi rūpaḥ saṃjñāyate yena tat asta doṣam saṃdṛśyate vā api atha gamyate vā munayaḥ ūcuḥ idānīm brūhi yogam ca duḥkha saṃyoga bheṣajam yam viditvā avyayam tatra yuñjāmaḥ puruṣottamam śrutvā sa vacanam teṣām kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ tadā abravīt parama prītaḥ yogī yoga vidām varaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca yogam vakṣyāmi bho viprāḥ śṛṇudhvam bhava nāśanam śrutvā ādau yoga śāstrāṇi gurum ārādhya bhaktitaḥ itihāsam purāṇam ca vedān ca eva vicakṣaṇaḥ āhāram yoga doṣān ca deśa kālam ca buddhimān jñātvā samabhyaset yogam nirdvaṃdvaḥ niṣparigrahaḥ bhuñjan saktum yavāgūm ca takra mūla phalam payaḥ yāvakam kaṇa piṇyākam āhāram yoga sādhanam na dvaṃdve na ca śīte ca na ca uṣṇe na anila ātmake sa śabde na jala abhyāse jīrṇa goṣṭhe catuṣpathe sarīsṛpe śmaśāne ca na nadyante agni saṃnidhau na śuṣka parṇa nicaye yogam yuñjīta karhicit deśān etān an ādṛtya mūḍha tvāt yaḥ yunakti vai pravakṣye tasya ye doṣāḥ jāyante vighna kārakāḥ bādhiryam jaḍa tā lopaḥ smṛteḥ mūka tvam andha tā tasmāt sarva ātmanā kāryā rakṣā yoga vidā sadā dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām śarīram sādhanam yatas śūnya āgāre śucau ramye ca ekānte devatālaye rajanyāḥ paścime yāme pūrve ca su samāhitaḥ pūrvāhṇe madhyame ca ahni yukta āhāraḥ jita indriyaḥ āsīnaḥ prāc mukhaḥ ramye āsane sukha niścale na ati nīce na ca ucchrite niḥspṛhaḥ satya vāc śuciḥ sarva dvaṃdva sahaḥ dhīraḥ sama kāya aṅghri mastakaḥ nābhau nidhāya hastau dvau śāntaḥ padmāsane sthitaḥ saṃsthāpya dṛṣṭim nāsā agre prāṇān āyamya vāgyataḥ samāhṛtya indriya grāmam manasā hṛdaye muniḥ praṇavam dīrgham udyamya saṃvṛta āsyaḥ su niścalaḥ saṃchādya nirmale śānte sthitaḥ saṃvṛta locanaḥ hṛd padma koṭare līnam sarva vyāpi nirañjanam yuñjīta satatam yogī mukti dam puruṣottamam saṃtyajya viṣayān tasya yoga siddhiḥ prakāśitā yadā nirviṣayam cittam pare brahmaṇi līyate bhavati ānandam āsādya tadā nirvāṇam ṛcchati śuddham dhāma traya atītam turya ākhyam puruṣottamam prāpya yoga balāt yogī mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ niḥspṛhaḥ sarva kāmebhyaḥ sarvatra priya darśanaḥ sadā ca abhyāsa yogena mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ na ca padmāsanāt yogaḥ na nāsā agra nirīkṣaṇāt manasaḥ ca indriyāṇām ca saṃyogaḥ yogaḥ ucyate evam mayā muni śreṣṭhāḥ yogaḥ proktaḥ vimukti daḥ lomaharṣaṇaḥ uvāca vyāsam praśasya saṃpūjya punar praṣṭum samudyatāḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ tava vaktra abdhi saṃbhūtam amṛtam vāc mayam mune pibatām naḥ dvijaśreṣṭha na tṛptiḥ iha dṛśyate sāṃkhyam ca dvipadām śreṣṭha śrotum icchāmahe vayam prajñāvān śrotriyaḥ yajvā khyātaḥ prājñaḥ anasūyakaḥ sāṃkhye vā yadi vā yoge etat pṛṣṭaḥ vadasva naḥ manasaḥ ca indriyāṇām ca yathā aikāgryam avāpyate vyāsaḥ uvāca mahābhūtāni sarvāṇi pūrva sṛṣṭiḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ bhūyiṣṭham prāṇabhṛt grāme niviṣṭāni śarīriṣu bhūmeḥ dehaḥ jalāt snehaḥ jyotiṣaḥ cakṣuṣī smṛte prāṇa apāna āśrayaḥ vāyuḥ koṣṭha ākāśam śarīriṇām karṇayoḥ pradiśaḥ śrotre jihvāyām vāc sarasvatī karṇau tvac cakṣuṣī jihvā nāsikā ca eva pañcamī daśa tāni indriya uktāni dvārāṇi āhāra siddhaye śabda sparśau tathā rūpam rasam gandham ca pañcamam indriyāṇi manaḥ yuṅkte avaśyān iva rājinaḥ manaḥ ca api sadā yuṅkte bhūtātmā hṛdaya āśritaḥ indriyāṇām tathā eva eṣām sarveṣām īśvaram manaḥ indriyāṇi indriya arthāḥ ca svabhāvaḥ cetanā manaḥ prāṇa apānau ca jīvaḥ ca nityam deheṣu dehinām āśrayaḥ na asti sattvasya guṇa śabdaḥ na cetanāḥ sattvam hi tejaḥ sṛjati na guṇān vai kathaṃcana evam saptadaśam deham vṛtam ṣoḍaśabhiḥ guṇaiḥ manīṣī manasā viprāḥ paśyati ātmānam ātmani na hi ayam cakṣuṣā dṛśyaḥ na ca sarvaiḥ api indriyaiḥ manasā tu pradīptena mahān ātmā prakāśate a śabda sparśa rūpam tat ca arasa agandham avyayam aśarīram śarīre sve nirīkṣeta nirindriyam śuni ca eva śvapāke ca paṇḍitāḥ sama darśinaḥ sa hi sarveṣu bhūteṣu jaṅgameṣu dhruveṣu ca sarva bhūteṣu ca ātmānam sarva bhūtāni ca ātmani yadā paśyati bhūtātmā brahma saṃpadyate tadā yāvān ātmani veda ātmā tāvān ātmā parātmani śakuntānām iva ākāśe matsyānām iva ca udake yathā gatiḥ na dṛśyeta tathā jñāna vidām gatiḥ kālaḥ pacati bhūtāni sarvāṇi eva ātmanā ātmani sarve tad sthāḥ ime lokāḥ bāhyam eṣām na kiṃcana na eva antam kāraṇasya īyāt yadi api syāt manojavaḥ tasmāt sūkṣmataram na asti na asti sthūlataram tathā sarvatas pāṇi pādam tat sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukham sarvatas śrutimat loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati tat antar sarva bhūtānām dhruvam tiṣṭhat na dṛśyate akṣaram ca kṣaram ca eva dvedhā bhāvaḥ ayam ātmanaḥ kṣaraḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu divyam tu amṛtam akṣaram nava dvāram puram kṛtvā haṃsaḥ hi niyataḥ vaśī īdṛśaḥ sarva bhūtasya sthāvarasya carasya ca hānena abhivikalpānām narāṇām saṃcayena ca śarīrāṇām ajasya āhuḥ haṃsa tvam pāra darśinaḥ haṃsa uktam ca kṣaram ca eva kūṭastham yat tat akṣaram tat vidvān akṣaram prāpya jahāti prāṇa janmanī vyāsaḥ uvāca bhavatām pṛcchatām viprāḥ yathāvat iha tattvataḥ sāṃkhyam jñānena saṃyuktam yat etat kīrtitam mayā yoga kṛtyam tu bho viprāḥ kīrtayiṣyāmi atas param eka tvam buddhi manasoḥ indriyāṇām ca sarvaśas ātmanaḥ vyāpinaḥ jñānam jñānam etat anuttamam tat etat upaśāntena dāntena adhyātma śīlinā ātma ārāmeṇa buddhena boddhavyam śuci karmaṇā kāmam krodham ca lobham ca bhayam svapnam ca pañcamam krodham śamena jayati kāmam saṃkalpa varjanāt dhṛtyā śiśna udaram rakṣet pāṇi pādam ca cakṣuṣā cakṣuḥ śrotram ca manasā manaḥ vācam ca karmaṇā apramādāt bhayam jahyāt dambham prājña upasevanāt agnīn ca brāhmaṇān ca atha devatāḥ praṇamet sadā varjayet uddhatām vācam hiṃsā yuktām manonugām etasya bhūta bhūtasya dṛṣṭam sthāvara jaṅgamam dhyānam adhyayanam dānam satyam hrīḥ ārjavam kṣamā śaucam ca eva ātmanaḥ śuddhiḥ indriyāṇām ca nigrahaḥ etaiḥ vivardhate tejaḥ pāpmānam ca apakarṣati dhūta pāpmā tu tejasvī laghu āhāraḥ jita indriyaḥ kāma krodhau vaśe kṛtvā niṣevet brahmaṇaḥ padam manasaḥ ca indriyāṇām ca kṛtvā aikāgryam samāhitaḥ pūrvarātre para ardhe ca dhārayet manaḥ ātmanaḥ manasaḥ pūrvam ādadyāt kūrmāṇām iva matsya hā tatas śrotram tatas cakṣuḥ jihvā ghrāṇam ca yoga vid pañca indriyāṇi manasi hṛdi saṃsthāpayet yadi yadā etāni avatiṣṭhante manaḥ ṣaṣṭhāni ca ātmani prasīdanti ca saṃsthāyām tadā brahma prakāśate vidhūmaḥ iva dīpta arciḥ ādityaḥ iva dīptimān vaidyutaḥ agniḥ iva ākāśe paśyanti ātmānam ātmani tam paśyanti mahātmānaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ye manīṣiṇaḥ dhṛtimantaḥ mahā prājñāḥ sarva bhūta hite ratāḥ evam parimitam kālam ācaran saṃśita vrataḥ pramohaḥ bhramaḥ āvartaḥ ghrāṇam śravaṇa darśane adbhutāni rasaḥ sparśaḥ śīta uṣṇa māruta ākṛtiḥ pratibhān upasargāḥ ca pratisaṃgṛhya yogataḥ giri śṛṅge tathā caitye vṛkṣa mūleṣu yojayet saṃniyamya indriya grāmam koṣṭhe bhāṇḍa manāḥ iva yena upāyena śakyeta niyantum cañcalam manaḥ śūnya āgārāṇi ca ekāgraḥ nivāsa artham upakramet na ativrajet param vācā karmaṇā manasā api vā na prahṛṣyeta lābheṣu na alābheṣu ca cintayet samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu sadharmā mātariśvanaḥ evam svastha ātmanaḥ sādhoḥ sarvatra sama darśinaḥ vedanā ārtān parān dṛṣṭvā sama loṣṭa aśma kāñcanaḥ api varṇa avakṛṣṭaḥ tu nārī vā dharma kāṅkṣiṇī tau api etena mārgeṇa gacchetām paramām gatim ajam purāṇam ajaram sanātanam avekṣya ca imām parameṣṭhi sāmyatām prayānti anāvṛtti gatim manīṣiṇaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ kām diśam vidyayā yānti kām ca gacchanti karmaṇā vyāsaḥ uvāca śṛṇudhvam muni śārdūlāḥ yat pṛcchadhvam samāsatas karma vidyā mayau ca ubhau vyākhyāsyāmi kṣara akṣarau yām diśam vidyayā yānti yām gacchanti ca karmaṇā śṛṇudhvam sāṃpratam viprāḥ gahanam hi etat uttaram yakṣasya sādṛśyam idam yakṣasya idam bhavet atha dvau imau atha panthānau yatra vedāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ pravṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ dharmaḥ nivṛttaḥ vā vibhāṣitaḥ karmaṇā jāyate pretya mūrtimān ṣoḍaśa ātmakaḥ ye tu buddhim parām prāptāḥ dharma naipuṇya darśinaḥ na te karma praśaṃsanti kūpam nadyām piban iva avyākṛtam anāyāmam amṛtam ca adhiyoga vid samāḥ sarvatra maitrāḥ ca sarva bhūta hite ratāḥ vidyā mayaḥ anyaḥ puruṣaḥ dvijāḥ karma mayaḥ aparaḥ viprāḥ candra sama sparśaḥ sūkṣmayā kalayā sthitaḥ tat etat ṛṣiṇā proktam vistareṇa anugīyate ekādaśa vikāra ātmā kalā saṃbhāra saṃbhṛtaḥ mūrtimān iti tam vidyāt viprāḥ karma guṇa ātmakam kṣetrajñam tam vijānīyāt nityam yoga jita ātmakam tamaḥ rajaḥ ca sattvam ca jñeyam jīva guṇa ātmakam jīvam ātma guṇam vidyāt ātmānam paramātmanaḥ sa cetanam jīva guṇam vadanti sa ceṣṭate jīva guṇam ca sarvam vyāsaḥ uvāca prakṛtyāḥ tu vikārāḥ ye kṣetrajñāḥ te pariśrutāḥ taiḥ ca eva kurute kāryam manaḥ ṣaṣṭhaiḥ iha indriyaiḥ su dāntaiḥ iva saṃyantā dṛḍhaḥ parama vājibhiḥ amṛtāt na param kiṃcid sā kāṣṭhā paramā gatiḥ evam sarveṣu bhūteṣu gūḍha ātmā na prakāśate dṛśyate tu agryayā buddhyā sūkṣmayā sūkṣma darśibhiḥ antarātmani saṃlīya manaḥ ṣaṣṭhāni medhayā dhyāne api paramam kṛtvā vidyā saṃpāditam manaḥ anīśvaraḥ praśānta ātmā tatas gacchet param padam indriyāṇām tu sarveṣām vaśya ātmā calita smṛtiḥ ātmanaḥ saṃpradānena martyaḥ mṛtyum upāśnute citta prasādena yatiḥ jahāti iha śubha aśubham nirvāte vā yathā dīpaḥ dīpyamānaḥ na kampate evam pūrva apare rātre yuñjan ātmānam ātmanā laghu āhāraḥ viśuddha ātmā paśyati ātmānam ātmani ātma pratyāyakam śāstram idam putra anuśāsanam dharma ākhyāneṣu sarveṣu satya ākhyāneṣu yat vasu daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi nirmathya amṛtam uddhṛtam navanītam yathā dadhnaḥ kāṣṭhāt agniḥ yathā eva ca tathā eva viduṣām jñānam mukti hetoḥ samuddhṛtam snātakānām idam śāstram vācyam putra anuśāsanam tat idam na a praśāntāya na a dāntāya tapasvine na a veda viduṣe vācyam tathā na anugatāya ca na asūyakāya anṛjave na ca anirdiṣṭa kāriṇe ślāghine ślāghanīyāya praśāntāya tapasvine idam priyāya putrāya śiṣyāya anugatāya tu yat api asya mahīm dadyāt ratna pūrṇām imām naraḥ yat tat mahā ṛṣibhiḥ dṛṣṭam vedānteṣu ca gīyate tat yuṣmabhyam prayacchāmi yat mām pṛcchata sattamāḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca adhyātmam yat idam viprāḥ puruṣasya iha paṭhyate yuṣmabhyam kathayiṣyāmi tasya vyākhyā avadhāryatām bhūmiḥ āpaḥ tathā jyotiḥ vāyuḥ ākāśam eva ca mahābhūtāni yaḥ ca eva sarva bhūteṣu bhūta kṛt munayaḥ ūcuḥ ākāśa ādyam śarīreṣu katham tat upavarṇayet indriyāṇām guṇāḥ kecid katham tān upalakṣayet vyāsaḥ uvāca śṛṇudhvam tat iha aikāgryāḥ yathātattvam yathā ca tat śabdaḥ śrotram tathā khāni trayam ākāśa lakṣaṇam prāṇaḥ ceṣṭā tathā sparśaḥ ete vāyu guṇāḥ trayaḥ rūpam cakṣuḥ vipākaḥ ca tridhā jyotiḥ vidhīyate ghreyam ghrāṇam śarīram ca bhūmeḥ ete guṇāḥ trayaḥ etāvān indriya grāmaḥ vyākhyātaḥ pāñcabhautikaḥ ākāśa prabhavaḥ śabdaḥ gandhaḥ bhūmi guṇaḥ smṛtaḥ manaḥ buddhiḥ svabhāvaḥ ca guṇāḥ ete sva yoni jāḥ te guṇān ativartante guṇebhyaḥ paramāḥ matāḥ yathā kūrmaḥ iva aṅgāni prasārya saṃniyacchati manaḥ ṣaṣṭhāni sarvāṇi buddhyāḥ bhāvāt kutas guṇāḥ indriyāṇi naraiḥ pañca ṣaṣṭham tat manaḥ ucyate saptamīm buddhim eva āhuḥ kṣetrajñam viddhi ca aṣṭamam cakṣuḥ ālokanāya eva saṃśayam kurute manaḥ buddhiḥ adhyavasānāya sākṣī kṣetrajñaḥ ucyate samāḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu tān guṇān upalakṣayet yat tu saṃtāpa saṃyuktam kāye manasi vā bhavet praharṣaḥ prītiḥ ānandam svāmyam svastha ātma citta tā akasmāt yadi vā kasmāt vadanti sāttvikān guṇān abhimānaḥ mṛṣāvādaḥ lobhaḥ mohaḥ tathā akṣamā tathā mohaḥ pramādaḥ ca tandrī nidrā prabodhi tā kathaṃcid abhivartante vijñeyāḥ tāmasāḥ guṇāḥ manaḥ prasṛjate bhāvam buddhiḥ adhyavasāyinī buddhiḥ ātmā manuṣyasya buddhiḥ eva ātma nāyikā yadā vikurute bhāvam tadā bhavati sā manaḥ indriyāṇām pṛthagbhāvāt buddhiḥ vikurute hi anu śṛṇvatī bhavati śrotram spṛśatī sparśaḥ ucyate paśyantī ca bhavet dṛṣṭiḥ rasantī rasanā bhavet indriyāṇi tu tāni āhuḥ teṣām vṛttyā vitiṣṭhati svayam bhāva ātmikā bhāvān trīn etān ativartate saritām sāgaraḥ bhartā mahā velām iva ūrmimān yadā prārthayate kiṃcid tadā bhavati sā manaḥ adhiṣṭhāne ca vai buddhyā pṛthak etāni saṃsmaret indriyāṇi ca medhyāni vicetavyāni kṛtsnaśas sarvāṇi eva anupūrveṇa yat yadā ca vidhīyate a śocan saṃprahṛṣyan ca nityam vigata matsaraḥ na hi ātmā śakyate draṣṭum indriyaiḥ kāma gocaraiḥ teṣām tu manasā raśmīn yadā samyak niyacchati tadā prakāśate dīpa dīptā yathā ākṛtiḥ sarveṣām eva bhūtānām tamasi upagate yathā vimukta ātmā tathā yogī guṇa doṣaiḥ na lipyate evam eva kṛta prajñaḥ na doṣaiḥ viṣayān caran sarva bhūta ātma bhūtasya guṇa saṅgena sajjataḥ na guṇāḥ viduḥ ātmānam guṇān veda sa sarvadā paridadhyāt guṇānām sa draṣṭā ca eva yathātatham sṛjate tu guṇān ekaḥ ekaḥ na sṛjate guṇān iṣikā vā yathā muñje pṛthak ca saha ca eva ha vyāsaḥ uvāca sṛjate tu guṇān sattvam kṣetrajñaḥ tu adhitiṣṭhati guṇān vikriyataḥ sarvān udāsīna vat īśvaraḥ svabhāva yuktam tat sarvam yat imān sṛjate guṇān ūrṇanābhiḥ yathā sūtram sṛjate tat guṇān tathā an ādi nidhanaḥ hi ātmā tam buddhvā viharet naraḥ iti evam hṛdaye sarvaḥ buddhi cintā mayam dṛḍham anityam sukham āsīnam aśocyam chinna saṃśayaḥ tarayet pracyutām pṛthvīm yathā pūrṇām nadīm narāḥ avagāhya ca vidvāṃsaḥ viprāḥ lolam imam tathā evam vicintya ca ātmānam kevalam jñānam ātmanaḥ tām tu buddhvā naraḥ sargam bhūtānām āgatim gatim etat dvijanma sāmagryam brāhmaṇasya viśeṣataḥ ātma jñāna sama sneha paryāptam tat parāyaṇam vijñāya etat vimucyante kṛtakṛtyāḥ manīṣiṇaḥ bhavati hi yā viduṣaḥ sanātanī munayaḥ ūcuḥ yaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ ca bhūtebhyaḥ tat bhavān prabravītu naḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca dharmam ca saṃpravakṣyāmi purāṇam ṛṣibhiḥ stutam viśiṣṭam sarva dharmebhyaḥ śṛṇudhvam muni sattamāḥ indriyāṇi pramāthīni buddhyā saṃyamya tattvataḥ sarvatas prasṛtāni iha pitā bālān iva ātmajān manasaḥ ca indriyāṇām ca api aikāgryam paramam tapaḥ tāni sarvāṇi saṃdhāya manaḥ ṣaṣṭhāni medhayā tadā ca eva ātmanā ātmānam param drakṣyatha śāśvatam sarva ātmānam mahātmānam vidhūmam iva pāvakam prapaśyanti mahātmānam brāhmaṇāḥ ye manīṣiṇaḥ yathā puṣpa phala upetaḥ bahu śākhaḥ mahā drumaḥ ātmanaḥ na abhijānīte kva me puṣpam kva me phalam jñāna dīpena dīptena paśyati ātmānam ātmanā dṛṣṭvā ātmānam tathā yūyam virāgāḥ bhavata dvijāḥ parām buddhim avāpya iha api acintāḥ vigata jvarāḥ sarvatas srotasam ghorām nadīm loka pravāhiṇīm lobha moha tṛṇa channām kāma krodha sarīsṛpām satya tīrtha anṛta kṣobhām krodha paṅkām sarit varām avyakta prabhavām śīghrām kāma krodha samākulām prataradhvam nadīm buddhyā dustarām akṛtātmabhiḥ saṃsāra sāgara gamām yoni pātāla dustarām ātmajanma udbhavām tām tu jihvā āvarta durāsadām yām taranti kṛtaprajñāḥ dhṛtimantaḥ manīṣiṇaḥ tām tīrṇaḥ sarvatas muktaḥ vidhūta ātmā ātmavān śuciḥ uttīrṇaḥ sarva saṃkleśān prasanna ātmā vikalmaṣaḥ bhūyiṣṭhāni iva bhūtāni sarva sthānāt nirīkṣya ca a krudhyan a prasīdan ca na nṛśaṃsa matiḥ tathā tatas drakṣyatha sarveṣām bhūtānām prabhava apyayam dharmam dharma bhṛtām śreṣṭhāḥ munayaḥ satya darśinaḥ ātmānaḥ vyāpinaḥ viprāḥ iti putra anuśāsanam ātma jñānam idam guhyam sarva guhyatamam mahat abravam yat aham viprāḥ ātma sākṣikam añjasā na etat jñātvā pumān strī vā punarbhavam avāpnuyāt yathā matāni sarvāṇi tathā etāni yathā tathā dṛṣṭvā hitam prīta manāḥ yad artham munayaḥ ūcuḥ mokṣaḥ pitāmahena uktaḥ upāyāt na an upāyataḥ tam upāyam yathānyāyam śrotum icchāmahe mune vyāsaḥ uvāca asmāsu tat mahā prājñāḥ yuktam nipuṇa darśanam yad upāyena sarva arthān mṛgayadhvam sadā anaghāḥ evam dharma ādi upāya arthe na anya dharmeṣu kāraṇam ekaḥ panthāḥ hi mokṣasya tat śṛṇudhvam mama anaghāḥ kṣamayā krodham ucchindyāt kāmam saṃkalpa varjanāt apramādāt bhayam rakṣet rakṣet kṣetram ca saṃvidam icchām dveṣam ca kāmam ca dhairyeṇa vinivartayet nidrām ca pratibhām ca eva jñāna abhyāsena tattva vid upadravān tathā yogī hita jīrṇa mita aśanāt lobham moham ca saṃtoṣāt viṣayān tattva darśanāt āyatyā ca jayet āśām sāmarthyam saṅga varjanāt anitya tvena ca sneham kṣudhām yogena paṇḍitaḥ kāruṇyena ātmanā ātmānam tṛṣṇām ca paritoṣataḥ maunena bahu bhāṣām ca śauryeṇa ca bhayam jayet yacchet vāc manasī buddhyā tām yacchet jñānacakṣuṣā jñānam ātmā mahān yacchet tam yacchet śāntiḥ ātmanaḥ tat etat upaśāntena boddhavyam śuci karmaṇā kāmam krodham ca lobham ca bhayam svapnam ca pañcamam dhyānam adhyayanam dānam satyam hrīḥ ārjavam kṣamā śaucam ācārataḥ śuddhiḥ indriyāṇām ca saṃyamaḥ dhūta pāpaḥ sa tejasvī laghu āhāraḥ jita indriyaḥ kāma krodhau vaśe kṛtvā nirviśet brahmaṇaḥ padam eṣa mārgaḥ hi mokṣasya prasannaḥ vimalaḥ śuciḥ tathā vāc kāya manasām niyamāḥ kāmataḥ avyayāḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca sāṃkhyāḥ sāṃkhyam praśaṃsanti yogān yoga vid uttamāḥ vadanti kāraṇaiḥ śreṣṭhaiḥ sva pakṣa udbhavanāya vai anīśvaraḥ katham mucyet iti evam muni sattamāḥ vadanti kāraṇaiḥ śreṣṭham yogam samyak manīṣiṇaḥ vadanti kāraṇam vedam sāṃkhyam samyak dvijātayaḥ vijñāya iha gatīḥ sarvāḥ viraktaḥ viṣayeṣu yaḥ etat āhuḥ mahā prājñāḥ sāṃkhyam vai mokṣa darśanam sva pakṣe kāraṇam grāhyam samartham vacanam hitam śiṣṭānām hi matam grāhyam bhavadbhiḥ śiṣṭa saṃmataiḥ pratyakṣam hetavaḥ yogāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ śāstra viniścayāḥ ubhe ca ete mate jñāte muni indrāḥ śiṣṭa saṃmate anuṣṭhite yathāśāstram nayetām paramām gatim tulyam śaucam tayoḥ yuktam dayā bhūteṣu ca anaghāḥ vratānām dhāraṇam tulyam darśanam tu asamam tayoḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ yadi tulyam vratam śaucam dayā ca atra mahā mune vyāsaḥ uvāca rāgam moham tathā sneham kāmam krodham ca kevalam yoga asthira uditān doṣān pañca etān prāpnuvanti tān yathā vā animiṣāḥ sthūlam jālam chittvā punar jalam prāpnuvanti tathā yogāt tat padam vīta kalmaṣāḥ tathā eva vāgurām chittvā balavantaḥ yathā mṛgāḥ prāpnuyuḥ vimalam mārgam vimuktāḥ sarva bandhanaiḥ lobha jāni tathā viprāḥ bandhanāni bala anvitaḥ chittvā yogāt param mārgam gacchanti vimalam śubham acalāḥ tu āvilāḥ viprāḥ vāgurāsu tathā apare bala hīnāḥ ca vipra indrāḥ yathā jālam gatāḥ dvijāḥ yathā ca śakunāḥ sūkṣmam prāpya jālam ariṃdamāḥ tatra aśaktāḥ vipadyante mucyante tu bala anvitāḥ alpakaḥ ca yathā viprāḥ vahniḥ śāmyati durbalaḥ ākrāntaḥ indhanaiḥ sthūlaiḥ tadvat yoga balaḥ smṛtaḥ samīraṇa gataḥ kṛtsnām dahet kṣipram mahīm imām tattva jñāna balaḥ yogī dīpta tejāḥ mahā balaḥ antakāle iva ādityaḥ kṛtsnam saṃśoṣayet jagat durbalaḥ ca yathā viprāḥ srotasā hriyate naraḥ viśanti vā vaśāt vā atha yogāt yoga bala anvitāḥ prajāpatīn manūn sarvān mahābhūtāni ca īśvarāḥ ātmanām ca sahasrāṇi bahūni dvijasattamāḥ yogam kuryāt balam prāpya taiḥ ca sarvaiḥ mahīm caret prāpnuyāt viṣayān kaścid punar ca ugram tapaḥ caret saṃkṣipyet ca punar viprāḥ sūryaḥ tejaḥ guṇān iva vimokṣa prabhavam viṣṇum upapannam asaṃśayam nidarśana artham sūkṣmāṇi vakṣyāmi ca punar dvijāḥ ātmanaḥ ca samādhāne dhāraṇām prati vā dvijāḥ nidarśanāni sūkṣmāṇi śṛṇudhvam muni sattamāḥ yuktaḥ samyak tathā yogī mokṣam prāpnoti asaṃśayam sneha pātre yathā pūrṇe manaḥ ādhāya niścalam puruṣaḥ yuktaḥ ārohet sopānam yukta mānasaḥ yathā ca nāvam vipra indrāḥ karṇadhāraḥ samāhitaḥ mahā arṇava gatām śīghram nayet viprān tu pattanam durgamam sthānam āpnoti hitvā deham imam dvijāḥ sārathiḥ ca yathā yuktaḥ sat aśvān su samāhitaḥ deśam iṣṭam nayati āśu dhanvinam puruṣa ṛṣabham tathā eva ca dvijāḥ yogī dhāraṇāsu samāhitaḥ prāpnoti āśu param sthānam lakṣya muktaḥ iva āśugaḥ āviśya ātmani ca ātmānam yaḥ avatiṣṭhati saḥ acalaḥ pāśam hatvā iva mīnānām padam āpnoti saḥ ajaram nābhyām śīrṣe ca kukṣau ca hṛdi vakṣasi pārśvayoḥ darśane śravaṇe vā api ghrāṇe ca amita vikramaḥ sthāneṣu eteṣu yaḥ yogī mahā vrata samāhitaḥ ātmanā sūkṣmam ātmānam yuṅkte samyak dvijottamāḥ su śīghram acala prakhyam karma dagdhvā śubha aśubham munayaḥ ūcuḥ āhārān kīdṛśān kṛtvā kāni jitvā ca sattama vyāsaḥ uvāca kaṇānām bhakṣaṇe yuktaḥ piṇyākasya ca bho dvijāḥ snehānām varjane yuktaḥ yogī balam avāpnuyāt bhuñjānaḥ yāvakam rūkṣam dīrgha kālam dvijottamāḥ ekāhārī viśuddha ātmā yogī balam avāpnuyāt pakṣān māsān ṛtūn citrān saṃcaran ca guhāḥ tathā apaḥ pītvā payaḥ miśrāḥ yogī balam avāpnuyāt akhaṇḍam api vā māsam satatam muni sattamāḥ upoṣya samyak śuddha ātmā yogī balam avāpnuyāt kāmam jitvā tathā krodham śīta uṣṇam varṣam eva ca bhayam śokam tathā svāpam pauruṣān viṣayān tathā aratim durjayām ca eva ghorām dṛṣṭvā ca bho dvijāḥ sparśam nidrām tathā tandrām durjayām muni sattamāḥ dīpayanti mahātmānam sūkṣmam ātmānam ātmanā vīta rāgāḥ mahā prājñāḥ dhyāna adhyayana saṃpadā durgaḥ tu eṣa mataḥ panthāḥ brāhmaṇānām vipaścitām yaḥ kaścid vrajati kṣipram kṣemeṇa muni puṃgavāḥ yathā kaścid vanam ghoram bahu sarpa sarīsṛpam abhaktam aṭavī prāyam dāva dagdha mahīruham panthānam taskara ākīrṇam kṣemeṇa abhipatet tathā yoga mārgam samāsādya yaḥ kaścid vrajate dvijaḥ kṣemeṇa uparamet mārgāt bahu doṣaḥ api saṃmataḥ āstheyam kṣura dhārāsu niśitāsu dvijottamāḥ dhāraṇā sā tu yogasya durgā iyam akṛtātmabhiḥ viṣamāḥ dhāraṇāḥ viprāḥ yānti vai na śubhām gatim netṛ hīnāḥ yathā nāvaḥ puruṣāṇām tu vai dvijāḥ yaḥ tu tiṣṭhati yoga ādhau dhāraṇāsu yathāvidhi maraṇam janma duḥkhi tvam sukhi tvam sa viśiṣyate nānā śāstreṣu niyatam nānā muni niṣevitam param yogasya panthānam niścitam tam dvijātiṣu brahmāṇam īśam vara dam ca viṣṇum bhavam ca dharmam ca mahā anubhāvam tamaḥ ca kaṣṭam su mahat rajaḥ ca sattvam ca śuddham prakṛtim parām ca siddhim ca devīm varuṇasya patnīm tārādhipam khe vimalam su tāram viśvān ca devān uragān pitṝn ca śailān ca kṛtsnān udadhīn ca vā acalān nadīḥ ca sarvāḥ sa nagān ca nāgān sādhyān tathā yakṣa gaṇān diśaḥ ca parasparam prāpya mahān mahātmā viśeta yogī nacirāt vimuktaḥ kathā ca yā vipra varāḥ prasaktā nārāyaṇam tam drutam āpnuvanti munayaḥ ūcuḥ samyak kriyā iyam vipra indra varṇitā śiṣṭa saṃmatā yoga mārgaḥ yathānyāyam śiṣyāya iha hita eṣiṇā sāṃkhye tu idānīm dharmasya vidhim prabrūhi tattvataḥ triṣu lokeṣu yat jñānam sarvam tat viditam hi te vyāsaḥ uvāca śṛṇudhvam munayaḥ sarvam ākhyānam vidita ātmanām vihitam yatibhiḥ vṛddhaiḥ kapila ādibhiḥ īśvaraiḥ guṇāḥ ca yasmin bahavaḥ doṣa hāniḥ ca kevalā jñānena parisaṃkhyāya sa doṣān viṣayān dvijāḥ mānuṣān durjayān kṛtsnān paiśācān viṣayān tathā viṣayān auragān jñātvā gandharva viṣayān tathā pitṝṇām viṣayān jñātvā tiryaktvam caratām dvijāḥ suparṇa viṣayān jñātvā marutām viṣayān tathā mahā ṛṣi viṣayān ca eva rājarṣi viṣayān tathā āsurān viṣayān jñātvā vaiśvadevān tathā eva ca devarṣi viṣayān jñātvā yogānām api vai parān viṣayān ca pramāṇasya brahmaṇaḥ viṣayān tathā āyuṣaḥ ca param kālam lokaiḥ vijñāya tattvataḥ sukhasya ca param kālam vijñāya muni sattamāḥ prāpta kāle ca yat duḥkham patatām viṣaya eṣiṇām svargasya ca guṇān jñātvā doṣān sarvān ca bho dvijāḥ veda vāde ca ye doṣāḥ guṇāḥ ye ca api vaidikāḥ jñāna yoge ca ye doṣāḥ jñāna yoge ca ye guṇāḥ sāṃkhya jñāne ca ye doṣān tathā eva ca guṇāḥ dvijāḥ sattvam daśaguṇam jñātvā rajaḥ navaguṇam tathā tamaḥ ca aṣṭaguṇam jñātvā buddhim saptaguṇām tathā ṣaḍguṇam ca nabhaḥ jñātvā tamaḥ ca triguṇam mahat dviguṇam ca rajaḥ jñātvā sattvam ca ekaguṇam punar mārgam vijñāya tattvena pralaya prekṣaṇena tu jñāna vijñāna saṃpannāḥ kāraṇaiḥ bhāvitātmabhiḥ prāpnuvanti śubham mokṣam sūkṣmāḥ iva nabhaḥ param rūpeṇa dṛṣṭim saṃyuktām ghrāṇam gandha guṇena ca śabda grāhyam tathā śrotram jihvām rasa guṇena ca tvacam sparśam tathā śakyam vāyum ca eva tad āśritam moham tamasi saṃyuktam lobham moheṣu saṃśritam viṣṇum krānte bale śakram koṣṭhe saktam tathā analam apsu devīm samāyuktām āpaḥ tejasi saṃśritāḥ tejaḥ vāyau tu saṃyuktam vāyum nabhasi ca āśritam rajaḥ sattvam tathā saktam sattvam saktam tathā ātmani saktam ātmānam īśe ca deve nārāyaṇe tathā jñātvā sattva guṇam deham vṛtam ṣoḍaśabhiḥ guṇaiḥ svabhāvam bhāvanām ca eva jñātvā deha samāśritām dvitīyam karma vai jñātvā vipra indrāḥ viṣaya eṣiṇām indriyāṇi indriya arthān ca sarvān ātmani saṃśritān prāṇa apānau samānam ca vyāna udānau ca tattvataḥ ādyam ca eva anilam jñātvā prabhavam ca anilam punar saptadhā tān tathā śeṣān saptadhā vidhivat punar prajāpatīn ṛṣīn ca eva sargān ca su bahūn varān saptarṣīn ca bahūn jñātvā rājarṣīn ca paraṃtapān surarṣīn marutaḥ ca anyān brahmarṣīn sūrya saṃnibhān aiśvaryāt cyāvitān dṛṣṭvā kālena mahatā dvijāḥ mahatām bhūta saṃghānām śrutvā nāśam ca bho dvijāḥ gatim vācām śubhām jñātvā arcā arhāḥ pāpa karmaṇām vaitaraṇyām ca yat duḥkham patitānām yama kṣaye yoniṣu ca vicitrāsu saṃcārān aśubhān tathā jaṭhare ca aśubhe vāsam śoṇita udaka bhājane śleṣma mūtra purīṣe ca tīvra gandha samanvite śukra śoṇita saṃghāte majjā snāyu parigrahe śirā śata samākīrṇe nava dvāre pure atha vai vijñāya hitam ātmānam yogān ca vividhān dvijāḥ tāmasānām ca jantūnām ramaṇīya anṛta ātmanām sāttvikānām ca jantūnām kutsitam muni sattamāḥ garhitam mahatām arthe sāṃkhyānām vidita ātmanām upaplavān tathā ghorān śaśinaḥ tejasaḥ tathā tārāṇām patanam dṛṣṭvā nakṣatrāṇām ca paryayam dvaṃdvānām viprayogam ca vijñāya kṛpaṇam dvijāḥ anyonya bhakṣaṇam dṛṣṭvā bhūtānām api ca aśubham bālye moham ca vijñāya pakṣa dehasya ca aśubham rāgam moham ca saṃprāptam kvacid sattvam samāśritam sahasreṣu naraḥ kaścid mokṣa buddhim samāśritaḥ durlabha tvam ca mokṣasya vijñānam śruti pūrvakam viṣayāṇām ca daurātmyam vijñāya ca punar dvijāḥ gatāsūnām ca sattvānām dehān bhittvā tathā śubhān vāsam kuleṣu jantūnām maraṇāya dhṛta ātmanām sāttvikānām ca jantūnām duḥkham vijñāya bho dvijāḥ brahma ghnānām gatim jñātvā patitānām su dāruṇām surā pāne ca saktānām brāhmaṇānām durātmanām guru dāra prasaktānām gatim vijñāya ca aśubhām tena jñānena vijñāya gatim ca aśubha karmaṇām tiryagyoni gatānām ca vijñāya ca gatīḥ pṛthak veda vādān tathā citrān ṛtūnām paryayān tathā kṣayam saṃvatsarāṇām ca māsānām ca kṣayam tathā pakṣa kṣayam tathā dṛṣṭvā divasānām ca saṃkṣayam kṣayam vṛddhim ca candrasya dṛṣṭvā pratyakṣataḥ tathā vṛddhim dṛṣṭvā samudrāṇām kṣayam teṣām tathā punar kṣayam dhanānām dṛṣṭvā ca punar vṛddhim tathā eva ca saṃyogānām tathā dṛṣṭvā yugānām ca viśeṣataḥ ātma doṣān ca vijñāya sarvān ātmani saṃsthitān sva dehāt utthitān gandhān tathā vijñāya ca aśubhān munayaḥ ūcuḥ kān utpāta bhavān doṣān paśyasi brahma vittama etam naḥ saṃśayam kṛtsnam vaktum arhasi aśeṣatas vyāsaḥ uvāca pañca doṣān dvijāḥ dehe pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ mārga jñāḥ kāpilāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ śṛṇudhvam muni sattamāḥ kāma krodhau bhayam nidrā pañcamaḥ śvāsaḥ ucyate ete doṣāḥ śarīreṣu dṛśyante sarva dehinām chindanti kṣamayā krodham kāmam saṃkalpa varjanāt sattva saṃsevanāt nidrām apramādāt bhayam tathā chindanti pañcamam śvāsam alpa āhāra tayā dvijāḥ guṇān guṇa śataiḥ jñātvā doṣān doṣa śataiḥ api hetūn hetu śataiḥ citraiḥ citrān vijñāya tattvataḥ apām phena upamam lokam viṣṇoḥ māyā śataiḥ kṛtam tamaḥ saṃbhramitam dṛṣṭvā varṣa budbuda saṃnibham nāśa prāyam sukha ādhānam nāśa uttara mahā bhayam sāṃkhyāḥ viprāḥ mahā prājñāḥ tyaktvā sneham prajā kṛtam jñāna jñeyena sāṃkhyena vyāpinā mahatā dvijāḥ rājasān aśubhān gandhān tāmasān ca tathāvidhān puṇyān ca sāttvikān gandhān sparśa jān deha saṃśritān chittvā ātma jñāna śastreṇa tapaḥ daṇḍena sattamāḥ tatas duḥkha ādikam ghoram cintā śoka mahā hradam tamaḥ kūrmam rajaḥ mīnam prajñayā saṃtaranti uta sneha paṅkam jarā durgam sparśa dvīpam dvijottamāḥ karma agādham satya tīram sthitam vrata manīṣiṇaḥ harṣa saṃgha mahā vegam nānā rasa samākulam nānā prīti mahā ratnam duḥkha jvara samīritam śoka tṛṣṇā mahā āvartam tīkṣṇa vyādhi mahā rujam asthi saṃghāta saṃghaṭṭam śleṣma yogam dvijottamāḥ dāna muktā ākaram ghoram śoṇita udgāra vidrumam hasita utkruṣṭa nirghoṣam nānā jñāna su duṣkaram rodana aśru mala kṣāram saṅga yoga parāyaṇam ahiṃsā satya maryādam prāṇa yoga maya urmilam vṛnda anugāminam kṣīram sarva bhūta payaḥ dadhim mokṣa durlabha viṣayam vāḍabā sukha sāgaram taranti yatayaḥ siddhāḥ jñāna yogena ca anaghāḥ tatas tān sukṛtīn jñātvā sūryaḥ vahati raśmibhiḥ padma tantu vat āviśya pravahan viṣayān dvijāḥ tatra tān pravahaḥ vāyuḥ pratigṛhṇāti ca anaghāḥ vīta rāgān yatīn siddhān vīrya yuktān tapodhanān sūkṣmaḥ śītaḥ su gandhaḥ ca sukha sparśaḥ ca bho dvijāḥ saptānām marutām śreṣṭhaḥ lokān gacchati yaḥ śubhān sattvam vahati śuddha ātmā param nārāyaṇam prabhum prabhuḥ vahati śuddha ātmā paramātmānam ātmanā paramātmānam āsādya tad bhūtāḥ yatayaḥ amalāḥ paramā sā gatiḥ viprāḥ nirdvaṃdvānām mahātmanām satya ārjava ratānām vai sarva bhūta dayāvatām munayaḥ ūcuḥ ājanma maraṇam vā te ramante tatra vā na vā tvat ṛte mānavam na anyam praṣṭum arhāma sattama mokṣa doṣaḥ mahān eṣa prāpya siddhim gatān ṛṣīn pravṛtti lakṣaṇam dharmam paśyāma paramam dvija vyāsaḥ uvāca yathānyāyam muni śreṣṭhāḥ praśnaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ ca saṃkaṭaḥ budhānām api saṃmohaḥ praśne asmin muni sattamāḥ atra api tattvam paramam śṛṇudhvam vacanam mama buddhiḥ ca paramā yatra kapilānām mahātmanām indriyāṇi api budhyante sva deham dehinām dvijāḥ karaṇāni ātmanaḥ tāni sūkṣmam paśyanti taiḥ tu saḥ ātmanā viprahīṇāni kāṣṭha kuḍya samāni tu sūkṣmaḥ carati sarvatra nabhasi iva samīraṇaḥ sa paśyati yathānyāyam smṛtvā spṛśati ca anaghāḥ indriyāṇi ha sarvāṇi sve sve sthāne yathāvidhi anīśa tvāt pralīyante sarpāḥ viṣa hatāḥ iva indriyāṇām tu sarveṣām sva sthāneṣu eva sarvaśas ākramya gatayaḥ sūkṣmāḥ varati ātmā na saṃśayaḥ sattvasya ca guṇān kṛtsnān rajasaḥ ca guṇān punar guṇān ca tamasaḥ sarvān guṇān buddheḥ ca sattamāḥ guṇān ca manasaḥ ca api nabhasaḥ ca guṇān tathā guṇān vāyoḥ ca sarva jñāḥ sneha jān ca guṇān punar apām guṇāḥ tathā viprāḥ pārthivān ca guṇān api sarvān eva guṇaiḥ vyāpya kṣetrajñeṣu dvijottamāḥ ātmā carati kṣetrajñaḥ karmaṇā ca śubha aśubhe śiṣyāḥ iva mahātmānam indriyāṇi ca tam dvijāḥ prakṛtim ca api atikramya śuddham sūkṣmam parāt param nārāyaṇam mahātmānam nirvikāram parāt param vimuktam sarva pāpebhyaḥ praviṣṭam ca hi anāmayam parama ātmānam aguṇam nirvṛtam tam ca sattamāḥ śreṣṭham tatra manaḥ viprāḥ indriyāṇi ca bho dvijāḥ āgacchanti yathākālam guroḥ saṃdeśa kāriṇaḥ śakyam vā alpena kālena śāntim prāptum guṇān tathā evam uktena vipra indrāḥ sāṃkhya yogena mokṣiṇīm sāṃkhyāḥ viprāḥ mahā prājñāḥ gacchanti paramām gatim jñānena anena vipra indrāḥ tulyam jñānam na vidyate atra vaḥ saṃśayaḥ mā bhūt jñānam sāṃkhyam param matam an ādi madhya nidhanam nirdvaṃdvam kartṛ śāśvatam kūṭastham ca eva nityam ca yat vadanti śama ātmakāḥ evam śaṃsanti śāstreṣu pravaktāraḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ sarve viprāḥ ca vedāḥ ca tathā sāma vidaḥ janāḥ samyak uktāḥ tathā yogāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ ca amita darśanāḥ amūrtiḥ tasya vipra indrāḥ sāṃkhyam mūrtiḥ iti śrutiḥ abhijñānāni tasya āhuḥ mahānti muni sattamāḥ dvividhāni hi bhūtāni pṛthivyām dvijasattamāḥ agamya gamya saṃjñāni gamyam tatra viśiṣyate jñānam mahat vai mahataḥ ca viprāḥ yat ca api dṛṣṭam vidhivat purāṇe sāṃkhya āgatam tat nikhilam muni indrāḥ yat ca itihāseṣu mahatsu dṛṣṭam yathā artha śāstreṣu viśiṣṭa dṛṣṭam jñānam ca loke yat iha asti kiṃcid sāṃkhya āgatam tat ca mahā muni indrāḥ samasta dṛṣṭam paramam balam ca jñānam ca mokṣaḥ ca yathāvat uktam tapāṃsi sūkṣmāṇi ca yāni ca eva sāṃkhye yathāvat vihitāni viprāḥ gacchanti sāṃkhyāḥ satatam sukhena tān ca api saṃdhārya tatas kṛtārthāḥ hitvā ca deham praviśanti mokṣam divaukasaḥ ca api ca yoga sāṃkhyāḥ sāṃkhye dvijāḥ bho iha śiṣṭa juṣṭe teṣām tu tiryaggamanam hi dṛṣṭam na adhas gatiḥ pāpa kṛtām nivāsaḥ sāṃkhyam viśālam paramam purāṇam mahā arṇavam vimalam udāra kāntam kṛtsnam hi sāṃkhyāḥ munayaḥ mahātma nārāyaṇe dhārayata aprameyam nārāyaṇāt viśvam idam purāṇam saṃhāra kāle ca hareta bhūyaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ akṣara akṣarayoḥ vyaktim pṛcchāmaḥ tvām mahā mune tvam hi jñāna vidām śreṣṭhaḥ procyase vedapāragaiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ ca mahābhāgaiḥ yatibhiḥ ca mahātmabhiḥ na tṛptim adhigacchāmaḥ śṛṇvantaḥ amṛtam uttamam vyāsaḥ uvāca atra vaḥ varṇayiṣyāmi itihāsam purātanam vasiṣṭhasya ca saṃvādam karālajanakasya ca vasiṣṭham śreṣṭham āsīnam ṛṣīṇām bhāskara dyutim papraccha janakaḥ rājā jñānam naiḥśreyasam param maitrāvaruṇim āsīnam abhivādya kṛtāñjaliḥ papraccha ṛṣi varam rājā karālajanakaḥ purā yasmin na punarāvṛttim prāpnuvanti manīṣiṇaḥ yat ca akṣaram iti proktam śivam kṣemam anāmayam vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca śrūyatām pṛthivīpāla kṣarati idam yathā jagat yatra kṣarati pūrveṇa yāvatkālena ca api atha sṛjati ananta karmāṇi mahāntam bhūtam agrajam mūrtimantam amūrta ātmā viśvam śaṃbhuḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ aṇimā laghimā prāptiḥ īśānam jyotiḥ avyayam sarvatas pāṇi pāda antam sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukham sarvatas śrutimat loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati sāṃkhye ca paṭhyate śāstre nāmabhiḥ bahudhā ātmakaḥ vicitra rūpaḥ viśvātmā eka akṣaraḥ iti smṛtaḥ dhṛtam eka ātmakam yena kṛtsnam trailokyam ātmanā tathā eva bahu rūpa tvāt viśvarūpaḥ iti śrutaḥ eṣa vai vikriyā āpannaḥ sṛjati ātmānam ātmanā ahaṃkāram mahā tejāḥ prajāpati namaskṛtam mahāntam ca api ahaṃkāram avidyā sarge eva ca vidyā avidyā iti vikhyāte śruti śāstra anucintakaiḥ bhūta sargam ahaṃkārāt tṛtīyam viddhi pārthiva ahaṃkāreṣu nṛpate caturtham viddhi vaikṛtam vāyuḥ jyotiḥ atha ākāśam āpaḥ atha pṛthivī tathā śrotram tvac cakṣuṣī jihvā ghrāṇam eva ca pañcamam buddhīndriyāṇi ca etāni tathā karmendriyāṇi ca saṃbhūtāni iha yugapad manasā saha pārthiva eṣā tattva caturviṃśā sarva ākṛtiḥ pravartate yām jñātvā na abhiśocanti brāhmaṇāḥ tattva darśinaḥ veditavyam nara śreṣṭha sadā eva naraka arṇave sa cāraṇa piśāce vai sa deva ṛṣi niśācare sa daṃśa kīṭa maśake sa pūti kṛmi mūṣake śuni śvapāke caiṇeye sa cāṇḍāle sa pulkase jale bhuvi tathā ākāśe na anyatra iti viniścayaḥ sthānam dehavatām āsīt iti evam anuśuśruma kṛtsnam etāvataḥ tāta kṣarate vyakta saṃjñakaḥ ahani ahani bhūtātmā yat ca akṣaraḥ iti smṛtam kathitam te mahā rāja yasmāt na āvartate punar pañcaviṃśatikaḥ amūrtaḥ sa nityaḥ tattva saṃjñakaḥ sattva saṃśrayaṇāt tattvam sattvam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ yat amūrtiḥ sṛjat vyaktam tat mūrtim adhitiṣṭhati caturviṃśatimaḥ vyaktaḥ hi amūrtiḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ saḥ eva hṛdi sarvāsu mūrtiṣu ātiṣṭhata ātmavān cetayan cetanaḥ nityam sarva mūrtiḥ a mūrtimān gocare vartate nityam nirguṇaḥ guṇa saṃjñitaḥ evam eṣa mahātmā ca sarga pralaya koṭiśas vikurvāṇaḥ prakṛtimān na abhimanyeta buddhimān tamasā tāmasān bhāvān vividhān pratipadyate rajasā rājasān ca eva sāttvikān sattva saṃśrayāt śukla lohita kṛṣṇāni rūpāṇi etāni trīṇi tu sarvāṇi etāni rūpāṇi jānīhi prākṛtāni tu tāmasāḥ nirayam yānti rājasāḥ mānuṣān atha puṇya pāpeṣu mānuṣyam puṇya mātreṇa devatāḥ evam avyakta viṣayam mokṣam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ pañcaviṃśatimaḥ yaḥ ayam jñānāt eva pravartate vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca utpadyati tapaḥ yogāt guṇaiḥ saha guṇa kṣayāt manuṣya tvāt divam yāti devaḥ mānuṣyam eti ca mānuṣyāt niraya sthānam ālayam pratipadyate koṣakāraḥ yathā ātmānam kīṭaḥ samabhirundhati sūtra tantu guṇaiḥ nityam tathā ayam aguṇaḥ guṇaiḥ śīrṣa roge akṣi roge ca danta śūle galagrahe yāni ca anyāni dvaṃdvāni prākṛtāni śarīriṇām abhimāna atimānānām tathā eva sukṛtāni api eka vāsāḥ catur vāsāḥ śāyī nityam adhas tathā maṇḍūkaśāyī ca tathā vīrāsana gataḥ tathā vīram āsanam ākāśe tathā śayanam eva ca bhasma prastara śāyī ca bhūmi śayyā anulepanaḥ vīrasthāna ambupāke ca śayanam phalakeṣu ca vividhāsu ca śayyāsu phala gṛhya anvitāsu ca udyāne khala lagne tu kṣauma kṛṣṇa ajina anvitaḥ maṇi vāla parīdhānaḥ vyāghra carma paricchadaḥ siṃha carma parīdhānaḥ paṭṭa vāsāḥ tathā eva ca caturtha aṣṭama kālam ca ṣaṣṭha kālikam eva ca ṣaṣ rātra bhojanaḥ ca eva tathā ca aṣṭa aha bhojanaḥ māsa upavāsī mūla āśī phala āhāraḥ tathā eva ca vāyubhakṣaḥ ca piṇyāka dadhi gomaya bhojanaḥ go mūtra bhojanaḥ ca eva kāśa puṣpa aśanaḥ tathā vartayan śīrṇa parṇaiḥ ca prakīrṇa phala bhojanaḥ vividhāni ca kṛcchrāṇi sevate siddhi kāṅkṣayā cāndrāyaṇāni vidhivat liṅgāni vividhāni ca cāturāśramya yuktāni dharma adharma āśrayāṇi api upāśrayān api aparān pākhaṇḍān vividhān api viviktāḥ ca śilā chāyāḥ tathā prasravaṇāni ca kānaneṣu viviktāḥ ca śailānām mahatīḥ guhāḥ niyamān vividhān ca api vividhāni tapāṃsi ca yajñān ca vividha ākārān vidyāḥ ca vividhāḥ tathā vaṇikpatham dvija kṣatra vaiśya śūdrān tathā eva ca dānam ca vividha ākāram dīna andha kṛpaṇa ādiṣu prakṛtyā ātmānam eva ātmā evam pravibhajati uta svāhākāra vaṣaṭkārau svadhākāra namaskriye śubha aśubha bhayam sarvam etat āhuḥ sanātanam divasa ante guṇān etān atītya ekaḥ avatiṣṭhate raśmi jālam iva ādityaḥ tad kālam saṃniyacchati ātma rūpa guṇān etān vividhān hṛdaya priyān evam etām prakurvāṇaḥ sarga pralaya dharmiṇīm kriyām kriyā pathe raktaḥ triguṇaḥ triguṇa adhipaḥ prakṛtyā sarvam evā idam jagat andhīkṛtam vibho evam dvaṃdvāni atītāni mama vartanti nityaśas nistartavyāṇi atha etāni sarvāṇi iti narādhipa yāvat eva tu me saukhyam jātyām jātyām bhaviṣyati sukha duḥkham hi mānuṣyam niraye ca api majjanam nirayāt ca api mānuṣyam kālena eṣyāmi aham punar manuṣya tvāt ca deva tvam deva tvāt pauruṣam punar eṣaḥ evam dvijātīnām ātmā vai sa guṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ sarga koṭi sahasrāṇi maraṇa antāsu mūrtiṣu saḥ evam phalam āpnoti triṣu lokeṣu mūrtimān prakṛtiḥ kurute karma śubha aśubha phala ātmakam prakṛtiḥ ca tathā āpnoti triṣu lokeṣu kāmagā trīṇi sthānāni ca etāni jānīyāt prākṛtāni ha sa liṅga antaram āsādya prākṛtam liṅgam avraṇam vraṇa dvārāṇi adhiṣṭhāya karmāṇi ātmani manyate śrotra ādīni tu sarvāṇi pañca karmendriyāṇi atha rāga ādīni pravartante guṇeṣu iha guṇaiḥ saha aliṅgaḥ liṅgam ātmānam akālam kālam ātmanaḥ asattvam sattvam ātmānam amṛtam mṛtam ātmanaḥ amṛtyum mṛtyum ātmānam acaram caram ātmanaḥ akṣetram kṣetram ātmānam asaṅgam saṅgam ātmanaḥ janma antara sahasrāṇi maraṇa antāni gacchati candramāḥ iva kośānām punar tatra sahasraśas kalā pañcadaśī yoniḥ tat dhāma iti paṭhyate nityam eva vijānīhi somam vai ṣoḍaśa aṃśakaiḥ dhīmān ca ayam na bhavati nṛpaḥ evam hi jāyate ṣoḍaśī tu kalā sūkṣmā sa somaḥ upadhāryatām akṣara kṣarayoḥ eṣa dvayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ iṣyate ṛte tu puruṣam na iha strī garbhān dhārayati uta ṛte striyam na puruṣaḥ rūpam nirvartate tathā anyonyasya abhisaṃbandhāt anyonya guṇa saṃśrayāt ṛtau nirvartate rūpam tat vakṣyāmi nidarśanam ye guṇāḥ puruṣasya iha ye ca mātuḥ guṇāḥ tathā asthi snāyu ca majjā ca jānīmaḥ pitṛtaḥ dvija tvak
