māṃsa śoṇitam ca iti mātṛ jāni anuśuśruma evam etat dvijaśreṣṭha veda śāstreṣu paṭhyate pramāṇam yat ca veda uktam śāstra uktam yat ca paṭhyate veda śāstra pramāṇam ca pramāṇam tat sanātanam evam eva abhisaṃbandhau nityam prakṛti pūruṣau mokṣa kāmāḥ vayam ca api kāṅkṣāmaḥ yat anāmayam vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca na ca grantha artha tattva jñaḥ tasya tad dhāraṇam vṛthā granthasya artham sa pṛṣṭaḥ tu mādṛśaḥ vaktum arhati sa katham manda vijñānaḥ grantham vakṣyati nirṇayāt a jñātvā grantha tattvāni vādam yaḥ kurute naraḥ lobhāt vā api athavā dambhāt sa pāpī narakam vrajet nirṇayam ca api chidra ātmā na tat vakṣyati tattvataḥ saḥ api iha asya artha tattva jñaḥ yasmāt na eva ātmavān api tasmāt tvam śṛṇu rāja indra yathā etat anudṛśyate yathā tattvena sāṃkhyeṣu yogeṣu ca mahātmasu yat eva yogāḥ paśyanti sāṃkhyam tat anugamyate ekam sāṃkhyam ca yogam ca yaḥ paśyati sa buddhimān tvac māṃsam rudhiram medaḥ pittam majja asthi snāyu ca dehāt deham avāpnoti bījāt bījam tathā eva ca katham guṇāḥ bhaviṣyanti nirguṇa tvāt mahātmanaḥ evam guṇāḥ prakṛti jāḥ jāyante na ca yānti ca tvac māṃsam rudhiram medaḥ pittam majja asthi snāyu ca aṣṭau tāni atha śukreṇa jānīhi prākṛtena vai pumān ca eva a pumān ca eva strīliṅgam prākṛtam smṛtam vāyuḥ eṣa pumān ca eva rasaḥ iti abhidhīyate yathā puṣpa phalaiḥ nityam mūrtam ca amūrtayaḥ tathā pañcaviṃśatikaḥ tāta liṅgeṣu niyata ātmakaḥ kevalam tu abhimāni tvāt guṇeṣu guṇaḥ ucyate guṇāḥ guṇavataḥ santi nirguṇasya kutas guṇāḥ tasmāt evam vijānanti ye janāḥ guṇa darśinaḥ yadā tu eṣa guṇān etān prākṛtān abhimanyate tadā sa guṇavān eva guṇa bhedān prapaśyati yat tat buddheḥ param prāhuḥ sāṃkhya yogam ca sarvaśas budhyamānam mahā prājñāḥ prabuddha parivarjanāt aprabuddham yathā vyaktam sva guṇaiḥ prāhuḥ īśvaram nirguṇam ca īśvaram nityam adhiṣṭhātāram eva ca prakṛteḥ ca guṇānām ca pañcaviṃśatikam budhāḥ sāṃkhya yoge ca kuśalāḥ budhyante parama eṣiṇaḥ budhyamānam prabudhyante dvābhyām pṛthak ariṃdama paraspareṇa etat uktam kṣara akṣara nidarśanam ekatvam akṣaram prāhuḥ nānātvam kṣaram ucyate pañcaviṃśati niṣṭhaḥ ayam tadā samyak pracakṣate ekatva darśanam ca asya nānātvam ca asya darśanam pañcaviṃśatibhiḥ tattvam tattvam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ nistattvam pañcaviṃśasya param āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ sthūla buddhyā na paśyāmi tattvam etat na saṃśayaḥ akṣara kṣarayoḥ uktam tvayā yat api kāraṇam dvaṃdvam ca eva aniruddham ca budhyamānam ca tattvataḥ sāṃkhya yogam ca kṛtsnena buddha abuddhim pṛthak pṛthak vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca yoga kṛtyam mahā rāja pṛthak eva śṛṇuṣva me yoga kṛtyam tu yogānām dhyānam eva param balam tat ca api dvividham dhyānam āhuḥ vidyā vidaḥ janāḥ ekāgra tā ca manasaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ tathā eva ca prāṇāyāmaḥ tu sa guṇaḥ nirguṇaḥ mānasaḥ tathā dvikālam na upabhuñjīta śeṣam bhuñjīta tatparaḥ daśa dvādaśabhiḥ vā api caturviṃśāt param yatas tiṣṭhantam ajaram tam tu yat tat uktam manīṣibhiḥ viśvātmā satatam jñeyaḥ iti evam anuśuśruma pūrvarātre para ardhe ca dhārayīta manaḥ hṛdi manaḥ buddhyā sthiram kṛtvā pāṣāṇaḥ iva niścalaḥ sthāṇu vat ca api akampyaḥ syāt dāru vat ca api niścalaḥ na śṛṇoti na ca āghrāti na ca paśyati kiṃcana na ca sparśam vijānāti na ca saṃkalpate manaḥ tadā prakṛtim āpannam yuktam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ na bhāti hi yathā dīpaḥ dīptiḥ tadvat ca dṛśyate niliṅgaḥ ca adhas ca ūrdhvam ca tiryaggatim avāpnuyāt vaidyutaḥ agniḥ iva ākāśe paśyati ātmānam ātmani yam paśyanti mahātmānaḥ dhṛtimantaḥ manīṣiṇaḥ sarvatra sarva bhūteṣu dhruvam tiṣṭhat na dṛśyate mahataḥ tamasaḥ tāta pāre tiṣṭhat na tāmasaḥ vimalaḥ vimataḥ ca eva nirliṅgaḥ aliṅga saṃjñakaḥ yogaḥ eṣa hi lokānām kim anyat yoga lakṣaṇam evam paśyan prapaśyeta ātmānam ajaram param sāṃkhya jñānam pravakṣyāmi parisaṃkhyā nidarśanam avyaktam āhuḥ prakhyānam parām prakṛtim ātmanaḥ ahaṃkāraḥ tu mahataḥ tṛtīyaḥ iti naḥ śrutam pañcabhūtāni ahaṃkārāt āhuḥ sāṃkhya ātma darśinaḥ etāḥ prakṛtayaḥ tu aṣṭau vikārāḥ ca api ṣoḍaśa pañca ca eva viśeṣāḥ ca tathā pañca indriyāṇi ca etāvat eva tattvānām sāṃkhyam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ sāṃkhye sāṃkhya vidhāna jñāḥ nityam sāṃkhya pathe sthitāḥ līyante pratilomāni gṛhyante ca antarātmanā guṇāḥ guṇeṣu satatam sāgarasya ūrmayaḥ yathā evam eva ca rāja indra vijñeyam jñāna kovidaiḥ bahudhā ātmā prakurvīta prakṛtim prasava ātmikām tat ca kṣetram mahān ātmā pañcaviṃśaḥ adhitiṣṭhati adhiṣṭhānāt adhiṣṭhātā kṣetrāṇām iti naḥ śrutam kṣetram jānāti ca avyaktam kṣetrajñaḥ iti ca ucyate kṣetram avyaktaḥ iti uktam jñātāram pañcaviṃśakam anyat eva ca jñānam syāt anyat jñeyam tat ucyate jñānam avyaktam iti uktam jñeyaḥ vai pañcaviṃśakaḥ anīśvaram atattvam ca tattvam tat pañcaviṃśakam catvāriṃśat caturviṃśat pratisaṃkhyāya tattvataḥ saṃkhyā sahasrakṛtyā tu nistattvaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ pañcaviṃśatī prabuddha ātmā budhyamānaḥ iti śrutaḥ yadā budhyati ātmānam tadā bhavati kevalaḥ evam etat vijānantaḥ sāmya tām pratiyānti uta samyak nidarśanam nāma pratyakṣam prakṛteḥ tathā na tu evam vartamānānām āvṛttiḥ vartate punar vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca sāṃkhya darśanam etāvat uktam te nṛpa sattama vidyā avidye tu idānīm me tvam nibodha anupūrvaśas yathā uktam ṛṣibhiḥ tāta sāṃkhyasya ati nidarśanam karmendriyāṇām sarveṣām vidyā buddhīndriyam smṛtam buddhīndriyāṇām ca tathā viśeṣāḥ iti naḥ śrutam viṣayāṇām manaḥ teṣām vidyām āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ manasaḥ pañca bhūtāni vidyāḥ iti abhicakṣate ahaṃkāraḥ tu bhūtānām pañcānām na atra saṃśayaḥ ahaṃkāraḥ tathā vidyā buddhiḥ vidyā nareśvara buddhyā prakṛtiḥ avyaktam tattvānām parama īśvaraḥ vidyā jñeyā nara śreṣṭha vidhiḥ ca paramaḥ smṛtaḥ avyaktam aparam prāhuḥ vidyā vai pañcaviṃśakaḥ jñānam avyaktam iti uktam jñeyam vai pañcaviṃśakam tathā eva jñānam avyaktam vijñātā pañcaviṃśakaḥ ubhau etau kṣarau uktau ubhau etau anakṣarau kāraṇam tu pravakṣyāmi yathājñānam tu jñānataḥ tattva saṃjñau ubhau eva procyete jñāna cintakaiḥ tat etat guṇa sargāya vikurvāṇam punar punar guṇānām mahat ādīnām utpadyati parasparam adhiṣṭhānam kṣetram āhuḥ etat vai pañcaviṃśakam tat aham tat guṇaiḥ taiḥ tu pañcaviṃśe vilīyate guṇāḥ guṇeṣu līyante tat ekā prakṛtiḥ bhavet kṣetrajñaḥ api tadā tāvat kṣetrajñaḥ saṃpraṇīyate yadā akṣaram prakṛtiḥ yam gacchate guṇa saṃjñitā evam eva ca kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetra jñāna parikṣayāt prakṛtyāḥ nirguṇaḥ tu eṣaḥ iti evam anuśuśruma kṣaraḥ bhavati eṣa yadā guṇavatī guṇeṣu atha prakṛtim tu atha jānāti nirguṇa tvam tathā ātmanaḥ prakṛtyā ca eṣa rāja indra miśraḥ anyaḥ anyasya dṛśyate yadā tu guṇa jālam tat prākṛtam vijugupsate paśyate ca param paśyan tadā paśyan nu saṃsṛjet kim mayā kṛtam etāvat yaḥ aham kāla nimajjanaḥ ātmānam tat avajñānāt anyam ca eva na vedmi aham sāmyam eka tva tām yātaḥ yādṛśaḥ tādṛśaḥ tu aham yaḥ aham ajñāna saṃmohāt ajñayā saṃpravṛttavān saṃsargāt atisaṃsargāt sthitaḥ kālam imam tu aham saḥ aham evam vaśībhūtaḥ kālam etam na buddhavān uttama adhama madhyānām tām aham katham āvase sahavāsam na yāsyāmi kālam etam vivañcanāt amūrtiḥ ca api amūrta ātmā mamatvena pradharṣitaḥ prakṛtyā ca tayā tena tāsu tāsu iha yoniṣu yoniṣu vartamānena naṣṭa saṃjñena cetasā samatā na mayā kācid ahaṃkāre kṛtā mayā ātmānam bahudhā kṛtvā saḥ ayam bhūyas yunakti mām mamatvam manasā nityam ahaṃkāra kṛta ātmakam apalagnām imām hitvā saṃśrayiṣye nirāmayam anena sāmyam yāsyāmi na anayā aham acetasā evam parama saṃbodhāt pañcaviṃśaḥ anubuddhavān avyaktam vyakta dharmāṇam sa guṇam nirguṇam tathā nirguṇam prathamam dṛṣṭvā tādṛś bhavati maithila mayā iha jñāna saṃpannam yathā śruti nidarśanāt niḥsaṃdigdham ca sūkṣmam ca viśuddham vimalam tathā sāṃkhya yogaḥ mayā proktaḥ śāstra dvaya nidarśanāt prabodhana param jñānam sāṃkhyānām avanīpate vispaṣṭam procyate tatra śiṣyāṇām hita kāmyayā bṛhat ca evam idam śāstram iti āhuḥ viduṣaḥ janāḥ asmin ca śāstre yogānām punarbhava puraḥsaram pañcaviṃśāt param tattvam paṭhyate ca narādhipa sāṃkhyānām tu param tattvam yathāvat anuvarṇitam vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca guṇānām dhārya tām tattvam sṛjati ākṣipate tathā ajaḥ hi krīḍayā bhūpa vikriyām prāptaḥ iti uta ātmānam bahudhā kṛtvā nānā iva praticakṣate guṇān ācarate hi eṣa sṛjati ākṣipate tathā pañcaviṃśam mahātmānam na ca asau api budhyate ṣaḍviṃśam vimalam buddham aprameyam sanātanam satatam pañcaviṃśam tu caturviṃśam vibudhyate dṛśya adṛśye hi anugata tad svabhāve mahā dyute pañcaviṃśam caturviṃśam ātmānam anupaśyati budhyate ca parām buddhim viśuddhām amalām yathā ṣaḍviṃśam rāja śārdūla tadā buddhaḥ kṛtaḥ vrajet nirguṇām prakṛtim veda guṇa yuktām acetanām tattva saṃśravaṇāt eva tattva jñaḥ jāyate nṛpa pañcaviṃśati tattvāni pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ na ca eva tattvavān tāta saṃsāreṣu nimajjati eṣām upaiti tattvam hi kṣipram budhyasva lakṣaṇam ṣaḍviṃśaḥ ayam iti prājñaḥ gṛhyamāṇaḥ ajara amaraḥ etat nānātvam iti uktam sāṃkhya śruti nidarśanāt saṅga dharmā bhavati eṣa niḥsaṅga ātmā narādhipa niḥsaṅga ātmānam āsādya ṣaḍviṃśam karma jam viduḥ caturviṃśam agādham ca ṣaḍviṃśasya prabodhanāt etāvat mokṣaḥ iti uktaḥ jñāna vijñāna saṃjñitaḥ pañcaviṃśatikasya āśu yaḥ ayam dehe pravartate vimokṣiṇā vimokṣaḥ ca sametya iha tathā bhavet śaṭhāya klībāya na jihma buddhaye na paṇḍita jñāna para upatāpine deyam tathā śiṣya vibodhanāya śraddhā anvitāya atha guṇa anvitāya para apavādāt viratāya nityam kṛpāvate atha kṣamiṇe hitāya vivikta śīlāya vidhi priyāya vivāda hīnāya bahuśrutāya na śreyase yokṣyati tādṛśe kṛtam pṛthvīm imām vā yadi ratna pūrṇām nirāmayam vīta bhayam śivam ca samīkṣya moham paravāda saṃjñam pṛṣṭaḥ tvayā ca asmi yathā narendra mahā jñānam mokṣa vidām parāyaṇam vyāsaḥ uvāca pañcaviṃśam muni śreṣṭhāḥ vasiṣṭhena yathā purā punarāvṛttim āpnoti paramam jñānam avyayam etat niḥśreyasa karam jñānam bhoḥ paramam mayā kathitam tattvataḥ viprāḥ śrutvā devarṣitaḥ dvijāḥ hiraṇyagarbhāt ṛṣiṇā vasiṣṭhena samāhṛtam vasiṣṭhāt ṛṣi śārdūlaḥ nāradaḥ avāptavān idam mā śucadhvam muni śreṣṭhāḥ śrutvā etat paramam padam avijñānāt ca mūḍha ātmā punar punar upadravān pretya jāti sahasrāṇi maraṇa antāni upāśnute deva lokam tathā tiryak mānuṣyam api ca aśnute yadi vā mucyate vā api tasmāt ajñāna sāgarāt tasmāt agādhāt avyaktāt upakṣīṇāt sanātanāt tasmāt yūyam virajaskāḥ vitamaskāḥ ca bho dvijāḥ evam mayā muni śreṣṭhāḥ sārāt sārataram param kathitam paramam mokṣam yam jñātvā na nivartate na nāstikāya dātavyam na abhaktāya kadācana na duṣṭa mataye viprāḥ na śraddhā vimukhāya ca lomaharṣaṇaḥ uvāca evam purā munīn vyāsaḥ purāṇam ślakṣṇayā girā daśa aṣṭa doṣa rahitaiḥ vākyaiḥ sārataraiḥ dvijāḥ pūrṇam asta malaiḥ śuddhaiḥ nānā śāstra samuccayaiḥ jāti śuddha samāyuktam sādhu śabda upaśobhitam śrāvayitvā yathānyāyam virarāma mahāmatiḥ te api śrutvā muni śreṣṭhāḥ purāṇam veda saṃmitam ādyam brāhma abhidhānam ca sarva vāñchā phala pradam hṛṣṭāḥ babhūvuḥ su prītāḥ vismitāḥ ca punar punar praśaśaṃsuḥ tadā vyāsam kṛṣṇadvaipāyanam munim munayaḥ ūcuḥ aho tvayā muni śreṣṭha purāṇam śruti saṃmitam sarva jñaḥ tvam mahābhāga deveṣu iva bṛhaspatiḥ namasyāmaḥ mahā prājñam brahmiṣṭham tvām mahā munim yena tvayā tu veda arthāḥ bhārate prakaṭīkṛtāḥ kaḥ śaknoti guṇān vaktum tava sarvān mahā mune adhītya caturaḥ vedān sa aṅgān vyākaraṇāni ca kṛtavān bhāratam śāstram tasmai jñāna ātmane namaḥ yena tvayā bhārata taila pūrṇaḥ prajvālitaḥ jñāna mayaḥ pradīpaḥ ajñāna timira andhānām bhrāmitānām kudṛṣṭibhiḥ jñāna añjana śalākena tvayā ca unmīlitāḥ dṛśaḥ jagmuḥ yathāgatam sarve kṛtakṛtyāḥ svam āśramam tathā mayā muni śreṣṭhā kathitam hi sanātanam purāṇam su mahā puṇyam sarva pāpa praṇāśanam yathā bhavadbhiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ aham saṃpraśnam dvijasattamāḥ vyāsa prasādāt tat sarvam mayā saṃparikīrtitam idam gṛhasthaiḥ śrotavyam yatibhiḥ brahmacāribhiḥ dhana saukhya pradam nṝṇām pavitram pāpa nāśanam śrotavyam su prayatnena samyak śreyaḥ bhikāṅkṣibhiḥ prāpnoti brāhmaṇaḥ vidyām kṣatriyaḥ vijayam raṇe vaiśyaḥ tu dhanam akṣayyam śūdraḥ sukham avāpnuyāt yam yam kāmam abhidhyāyan śṛṇoti puruṣaḥ śuciḥ tam tam kāmam avāpnoti naraḥ na asti atra saṃśayaḥ purāṇam vaiṣṇavam tu etat sarva kilbiṣa nāśanam viśiṣṭam sarva śāstrebhyaḥ puruṣa artha upapādakam etat vaḥ yat mayā ākhyātam purāṇam veda saṃmitam śrute asmin sarva doṣa utthaḥ pāpa rāśiḥ praṇaśyati upoṣya yat avāpnoti tat asya śravaṇāt naraḥ mahā puṇya mayam viprāḥ tat asya śravaṇāt sakṛt yat jyeṣṭha śukla dvādaśyām snātvā vai yamunā jale mathurāyām harim dṛṣṭvā prāpnoti puruṣaḥ phalam tat āpnoti phalam samyak samādhānena kīrtanāt purāṇe asya hitaḥ viprāḥ keśava arpita mānasaḥ tat phalam samavāpnoti yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt api idam yaḥ śraddhayā nityam purāṇam veda saṃmitam yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt martyaḥ sa yāti bhuvanam hareḥ śrāvayet brāhmaṇaḥ yaḥ tu sadā parvasu saṃyataḥ ekādaśyām dvādaśyām ca viṣṇu lokam sa gacchati idam yaśasyam āyuṣyam sukha dam kīrti vardhanam bala puṣṭi pradam nṝṇām dhanyam duḥsvapna nāśanam trisaṃdhyam yaḥ paṭhet vidvān śraddhayā su samāhitaḥ idam variṣṭham ākhyānam sa sarvam īpsitam labhet bhayāt vimucyate bhītaḥ āpad āpannaḥ āpadaḥ jātismara tvam vidyām ca putrān medhām paśūn dhṛtim dharmam ca artham ca kāmam ca mokṣam tu labhate naraḥ yān yān kāmān abhipretya paṭhet prayata mānasaḥ tān tān sarvān avāpnoti puruṣaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ yaḥ ca idam satatam śṛṇoti manujaḥ svarga apavarga pradam viṣṇum lokagurum praṇamya vara dam bhakti ekacittaḥ śuciḥ paścāt yāti hareḥ padam su vimalam muktaḥ guṇaiḥ prākṛtaiḥ vaiśyaiḥ ca anudinam viśuddha kula jaiḥ śūdraiḥ tathā dhārmikaiḥ arthāḥ striyaḥ ca nipuṇaiḥ api sevyamānāḥ dharmeṇa rājyam labhate manuṣyaḥ āyuḥ ca kīrtim ca tapaḥ ca dharmam dharmeṇa mokṣam labhate manuṣyaḥ idam rahasyam śreṣṭham ca purāṇam veda saṃmitam na deyam duṣṭa mataye nāstikāya viśeṣataḥ idam mayā uktam pravaram purāṇam ājñāpayadhvam munayaḥ vrajāmi
